U7 chit8 e5 Ong5-kok kio3 choe3 ThiaN3

1 Kou-LU2 A-HOA E5 SIN-SE3
¡§A-hoa, A-hoa li2 iau2 teh khun3 tioh8-m?!  Li2 chin-kaN2!  Li2 iau2 m7-chai thang khi2-lai5!¡¨
A-hoa ti7 bang7-tiong u7 thiaN-kiN3 thau5-ke-niu5 hiong5-ok e5 siaN-im teh kio3 i, chiu7 kin2-kin2 tui3 i teh khun3 hit-e5 la5-sam5 piah-piN e5 ui7 tio5 khi2-lai5.
¡§Thau5-ke-niu5 ah, goa2 khi2- lai5 lah!¡¨  A-hoa chhin-chhiuN7 chin kiaN-sim e5 khoan2 lai5 chau2 kau3 chau3-kha khi3.  Khiok iau2 si7 chin cha2, thiN iau2-boe7 kng, koh si7 han5-leng2 e5 ji7-geh8 cha2-khi2.
A-hoa poaN3-khun3 poaN3-chheN2 e5 khoan2-sit lai5 beh khai-si2 i mui2-jit8 e5 kong-chok.  I soe3-soe3 e5 sin-khu in-ui7 koaN5 khu-khu-chhoah, i kin2-kin2 khi2-hoe2 ti7 lou5-nih, jian5-au7 chiu7 theh8 chui2-thang2 beh chhut-khi3 chhiuN7-chui2.
Chong2-si7 han5-leng2 e5 pak-hong chhin-chhiuN7 beh chhi3-jip8 ti7 hit-e5 phoa3-noa7 e5 saN pau-teh e5 sin-khu.  I chiu7 sim7 chit8-e7, lai5 beh thiaNhit-e5 thang kiaN e5 thau5-ke-niu5 u7 ke3-siok8 ti7 i e5 chhng5-lai7 teh khun3 a2-bo5???  I u7 thiaN-tioh8 teh hoN5 e5 siaN, chiu7 siuN7 beh lai5 eng7 hit-e5 siu7-kim3 e5 chui2.  A-hoa sio2-sim lai5 beh thau-iuN2 chui2-kng-lai7 e5 chui2, chong2-si7 i soe3-soe3 e5 sin-chai5 boe7-thang khoaN3 tioh8 hit e5 toa7 koh koan5 e5 chui2-kng-lai7, soah8 ti7 sio2-sim e5 tiong-kan khi3 khap-tioh8 chui2-kng lai5 hoat-chhut siaN.
¡§Chit-e5 si2-kui2 koh teh thau-eng7 lai7-bin7 e5 chui2 lah!¡¨  Thau5-ke-niu5 chhou-toa7 e5 siaN hut-jian5 kin7-oa2 lai5 kau3 A-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, ¡§PhaiN2-mih8, li2 long2 bo5 thiaN-chhui3!¡¨, lai5 an2-ni jiong2, soah chhut-chhiu2 sian3 A-hoa e5 bin7.
¡§Thau5-ke-niu5 ah, gon2 beh khi3 goa7-bin7 chhiuN7 lah!¡¨  A-hoa na2 so i e5 chhui3-phoe2 lai5 khui-mng5 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 tiaN5, koh khui au7-bin7 mng5 chhut-khi3 hang7-lou7.  Ti7 hang7-boe2 u7 chit8-e5 toa7 kou2-chiN2, in-ui7 chin cha2 koh chin koaN5 long2 iau2 bo5 lang5 chhut-lai5 teh eng7 chui2.  A-hoa tioh8 ti7 hit e5 chhim-chhim e5 toa7-chiN2 lai5 chhiuN7-chhut tam7-poh8 e5 chui2 khi2-lai5.  Hit-e5 si7 put-chi2 khun3-lan5 e5 kang-chok, ti7 i soe3-soe3 e5 ni5-ki2 si7 cham2-jian5 oh tam7-tng e5 su7.  I in-ui7 koaN5 chiu7 khai-si2 teh gim5-si, lian5 hit e5 siaN-im ia7 khu-khu-chhoah e5 khoan2.
A-hoa tauh8-tauh8 chhiuN7, kau3 moa2 thang2 chiu7 koh thoa hit-e5 pi2 i khah tang7 e5 chui2 lai5 jip8 au7 bin7 mng5.  I e5 chhui3 iau2 teh gim5-si, i chhin-chhiuN7 long2 bo5 teh siuN7 i e5 khun3-lan5.  Ti7 i soe3-soe3 e5 sin-khu u7 moa2-moa2 e5 jim2-siu7-lat8 thang tui3-hu3 se3-kan long2-chong2 e5 khun3-lan5 kap put-heng7 e5 khoan2.
A-hoa koaN7-chui2 jip8 lai5 e5 si5 i e5 kha-chhiu2 long2 ba5 kau3 m7-chai si7 i e5--bah.  I chiu7 oa2-kin7 ti7 lou5-nih lai5 hang i e5 chhiu2, hou7 i e5 sin-khu u7 tam7-poh8 e5 sio-lo7, jian5-au7 chiu7 soe2-bi2 lai5 chu2 cha2-tng3.  I ti7 chhui3-lai7 iau2 chin soe3-siaN teh gim5-si, in-ui7 thau5-ke-niu5 m7-ai3 i gim5-si.
ThiN i2-keng kng lah, chhu3-piN e5 lang5 long2 khai-si2 teh chun2-pi7 cha2-tng3.  Keh-piah e5 eN-a2 A-gi7 teh hau2, lau7-bu2 teh ka7 i io.  U7 boe7-mih8 e5 lang5 e5 siaN, teh koe3-lou7 e5 lang5 kong2 oe7 e5 siaN long2 u7 thiaN-kiN3.
Chong2-si7 A-hoa iau2 kam2-kak chin koaN5, ia7 kam2-kak khun3 bo5 kau3-giah8 e5 khoan2, sou2-i2 chiu7 khut-sin ti7 lou5-piN beh bih-koaN5.  I e5 bin7 u7 ia3-sian7, soe-jiok8 e5 khoan2-sit hou7 lang5 khoaN3 sui5-si5 beng5-pek.  Iau2-ku2 hit-tui3 toa7-lui2 e5 bak8-chiu u7 hian2-chhut i thian-seng3 put-khut e5 oat8-phoat beng5-long2 ti7-teh.  Niau-a2 Li7-li7 khoaN3-kiN3 A-hoa theng5-chhiu2 chiu7 kin2 kin2 chau2-oa2 lai5 hou7 A-hoa pho7.  A-hoa khoaN3-tioh8 niau-a2 chin hoaN-hi2 i, chiu7 chhim-chhim lam2-oa2 ti7 i e5 heng5-cheng5, khiok an2-ni liam7.
¡§Bo5 lang5 ai3 e5 si2 niau-a2, li2 chau2 lai5 chia beh cho3 sim2-mih8?!¡¨
A-hoa si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2 lang5?  I si7 chit8-e5 bo5-pe7 bo5-bu2, kok-lai7 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2.  I e5 pe7-bu2 ti7 Tai7-tang-a chian3-cheng e5 si5 lai5 hi-seng si2-khi3, lau7-pe7 si7 tng-peng ti7 chian3-tiuN5, lau7-bu2 si7 ti7 to5-chau2 e5 lan5-bin5 e5 tiong-kan lai5 koe3-sin.  Kou-ji5 A-hoa chiu7 ti7 A-chek e5 chhiu2 lai5 koe3 i iu3-eN e5 seng-oah8.  Kau3 ti7 A-hoa si3-hoe3 e5 si5, chian3-cheng i2-keng kiat-sok, ti7 Siong7-hai2 u7 chit8-tui3 siau3-lian5 e5 hu-hu7 ai3 beh pun gin2-na2, A-chek thiaN-tioh8 chiu7 chiong A-hoa pho7 kau3 Siong7-hai2 lai5 pun hou7 in.
Chit-tui3 hu-hu7 kiat-hun sou3-ni5 long2 bo5 gin2-na2, sou2-i2 chiau3 se3-siok8 e5 le7 ai3 pun chit8 e5 gin2-na2 lai5 cho3 chhoa7-thau5.
A-hoa ti7 Siong7-hai2 bo5-ku2 chiu7 koh tu2-tioh8 Tiong-kiong7 e5 chhim-hoan7 Tai7-liok8.  Chian3-hoe2 it-hoat, toa7 pou7-hun7 soan2-tek8 chu7-iu5 e5 peh-seN3 liok8-siok8 ta3-chun5 to5-chau2 kau3 peng5-an e5 hai2-to2 Tai5-oan5 lai5.  A-hoa kap i e5 iuN2 pe7-bu2 ia7 put-chhut ki5-ta, hun-jip8 ti7 lan5-bin5 e5 tiong-kan chau2-kau3 Tai5-oan5 lai5.
Chit e5 iN7-hiong e5 sio2 ka-teng5 au7-lai5 chiu7 an-ku ti7 Tai5-pak.  IuN2-pe7 ke3-siok8 hok8-bu7 ti7 gun5-hang5 e5 kang-chok, tak8 cha2-khi2 chhut-khin5, e7-pou si5 chiu7 tng2-lai5.  IuN2-bu2 chin hoaN-hi2 Tai5-oan5, chiu7 siong5-siong5 chhoa7 A-hoa chhut-goa7 thit-tho5.
A-hoa ti7 chit-e5 ka-teng5 khiok-si7 chin heng7-hok.  IuN2 pe7-bu2 chin u7 koan-sim A-hoa, khoaN3-kou3 i e5 chheng7-chhah, i e5 seng-oah8, tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 in teh khoaN3-kou3 in pang5-keng, in e5 i2-toh, in sou2 siok8 it-chhe3 e5 mih8-kiaN7 chit8-iuN7.  A-hoa e5 thau5 kau3 boe2 long2 it-it tit-tioh8 in e5 i3-su3 lai5 siu-cheng2 koan2-li2.  Thau5-mng5 e5 the2-heng5, saN e5 iuN7-sek, oe5 e5 khoan2-sit, long2 boe7 sai2-tit chhin3-chhai2 A-hoa ti7 chit-e5 ka-teng5 tu2-tu2 si7 chit8-e5 oah8 e5 ang5-a2 chit8-iuN, lau7-bu2 na7 kio3 i an2-choaN2 i chiu7 an2-choaN2.  I e5 iuN2-bu2 tak8-jit8 tioh8 chhoa7 A-hoa chhut-goa7 khi3 hong2-bun7 chhin-lang5 peng5-iu2.
¡§A-hoa li2 khi3 chheng7 hit-nia2 ang5-sek e5 goa7-saN, oaN7 hit-siang bo5-toa3 e5 ou-oe5, ma-ma beh chhoa7 li2 chhut-khi3.¡¨  Cha2-khi2 si5 kau3 chit e5 si5-kan, iuN2-bu2 chiu7 an2-ni hoan-hu3 A-hoa.

A-hoa chin hoaN-hi2, i si7 chit8-e5 oah8-phoat hoN3-ki5 e5 gin2-na2, sou2-i2 kin2-kin2 chiu7 khi3 oaN7-saN chun2-pi7 chhut-mng5.  Tui3 u7 chit-e5 sip8-koan3, A-hoa na7 kau3 hit e5 si5-kan chiu7 ti7 sim-lai7 teh tan2-hau7 ma-ma beh tui3 i kong2 hia e5 oe7.  Kau3-boe2 hit-e5 si5 na7 kau3, A-hoa chiu7 m7-bian2 ma-ma7 tui3 i kong2, i ka-ki7 seng khi3 oaN lau7-bu2 phah-sng3 ai3 i chheng7 e5 saN kap oe5.  A-hoa e5 chun2-chat long2 u7 tioh8, kau3 lau7-bu2 ka7 i kong2 e5 si5 i long2 chun2-pi7 ho2-se3 lah.
Kong-hok8 chap8-goa7 ni5 liau2-au7 e5 Tai5-pak, chha-put-to u7 kok-che3 tou-chhi7 e5 hoan5-hoa5.  Bi2-kok e5 bun5-beng5 long2 tit8-chiap oe7-thang thoan5-jip8 ti7 chit-e5 tou-chhi7.  U7 goa7-seng2 lai5 e5 lan5-bin5 ong2-moa2 ti7 mui2 chit8-e5 ke-lou7 hang7-kak.  Kun-jin5, goa7 kok lang5, siong-jin5 kok-chiong2 e5 jin5-but8, kok-chiong2 e5 heng5-sek ti7 hia e5 ai3-hou7 hu-eng5 e5 lang5 e5 sim cho3-chiaN5 chin-toa7 e5 chok-chong.  A-hoa e5 bak8-chiu sou2 chu3-i3 e5 si7 hia e5 tiam3-thau5 hoa5-bi2 e5 hoe-iuN7 kap pai5-liat8 ti7 thang-lai7 e5 ang5-a2, hi5-ki5 e5 thit-tho5 mih8.
Hia e5 put-si5 teh pian3-tong7 hoan5-chap8 e5 ke-lou7 hian2-chhut chit8-pak khoaN3 boe7-sian7 e5 oah8-keng2.  A-hoa toe3 iuN2-bu2 ti7 tiam3-thau5, ti7 jin5-ke, ti7 ke-lou7, ti7 chhia-teng2, ti7 chhi7-tiuN5 lai5 him-siuN2 sia7-hoe7 siong7 tak8-khoan2 e5 cheng5-heng5 kong-keng2.
Tu5-khi3 chiah e5 su7 i2-goa7 A-hoa e5 seng-oah8 long2-si7 ti7 lau5-teng2 e5 pang5-keng, i ti7 hia ka-ki7 thit-tho5.
¡§Chit e5 si7 goa2 e5 eN-a2.¡¨  A-hoa eng7 pou3 cho3 chit8-sian eN-a2 lai5 kap i kong2 oe7.  ¡§Ma-ma beh chhoa7 li2 chhut-khi3 thit-tho5, beh che7-chhia khi2 ke-a2, li2 tioh8 kin2-kin2 loah li2 e5 thau5-mng5; li2 e5 thau5-mng5 chin-sui2, ia7 tioh8 oaN7 hit-nia2 ma-ma cho3 hou7 li2 e5 ang5-saN.  Li2 chheng7 hit-nia2 chin-chiaN3 sui2, oe5 tioh8 chheng7 hit-siang bo5-toa3 e5-, na7 bo5, li2 e5 kha oe7 thiaN3.¡¨  A-hoa chiong iuN2-bu2 siong5 tui3 i kong2 e5 oe7 lai5 tui3 eN-a2 kong2.
¡§Chit-tiap8 si7 chhi7-cheng3-hu2 cheng5, u7 lang5-kheh beh loh8-chhia a2-bo5?  ChhiaN2 lin2 m7-thang kheh, tioh8 tan2-hau7, tioh8 pai5-liat8 loh8-chhia!¡¨  A-hoa oh8 chhia-chiang2 e5 oe7 e5 khoan2-sit.

¡§Lai5-che7!  Li2 a-chai ai3 khiam3-eng7 sim2-mih8?  Gu5-ni a2-si7 koe-nng7?  Goan2 e5 koe-nng7 si7 sin-sian2 e5......¡¨, Che-si7 chap8-hoe3 tiam3 e5 oe7.  A-hoa chiong sou2 thiaN sou2 khoaN3e5,ti7 kou-tok8 e5 si5 chiu7 lai5 piau2-ian2.
A-hoa ti7 chit-e5 ka-teng5 thang-kong2 si7 chin heng7-hok, ¡§A-hoa loh8-lai5 chiah8-png7!¡¨  Na7 kau3 png7-tng3, lau7-bu2 chiu7 lai5 kau3 lau5-thui-kha kio3 i chiah8-png7, u7-si5 lau7-pe7 ia7 lai5 kau3 lau5-teng2 kio3 i chiah8 png7, soah kap i kong2 oe7.  ¡§A-hoa pa-pa chhoa7 li2 loh8-lai5!¡¨  A-hoa chiu7 khan pa-pa e5 chhiu2, nng7-lang5 chiu7 saN-kap cho3-sng2 lai5 loh8-thui.
¡§A-hoa li2 ngeh nng7-te3 bah, pa-pa ma-ma ia7 long2 ngeh nng7-te3.¡¨  Tak8-lang5 che7 toh e5 si5, ma-ma chiu7 theh8 bah e5 phiat lai5 hou7 tak8-lang5 long2 ngeh nng7-te3.
¡§A-hoa li2 ai3-chiah8 bah e5 khoan2, pa-pa chit te3 koh hou7 li2.¡¨  IuN2-pe7 chiu7 tui3 i e5 hun7-giah8 theh8 chit8-te3 hou7 A-hoa.  Kou-ji5 A-hoa ti7 chit e5 ka-teng5 e5 seng-oah8 sit8-chai7 chin chhu3-bi7.  Lau7-bu2 tak8-jit8 chhoa7 i chhut-mng5, lau7-pe7 na7 tng2-lai5, u7-si5 iah8 boe2 tam7-poh8 mih8-kiaN7 hou7 A-hoa.  Bo5 loa7-ku2 iuN2-bu2 u7 hoat-kak i e5 seng-li2 pian3-iuN7, chiu7 sui5-si5 beng5-pek8 u7 hoai5-in7.  In e5 sim chin-toa7 hoaN-hi2, kin2-kin2 thong-ti hou7 chhin-lang5 chai-iaN2.  Tui3 chit-si5 khi2 chit-e5 ka-teng5 tim5-tiong7 e5 khong-khi3 u7 toa7 pian3-oaN7.  Ki5-thai7 hoaN-hi2 e5 khoai3-lok8 hou7 chit-e5 ka-teng5 pian3 chin u7 oah8-khi3.  Lau7-bu2 chiu7 kiam2-chio2 chhut-goa7, siong5-siong5 teh hioh-khun3.
Chong2-si7 A-hoa hoat-hian7 i e5 hoaN-hi2 chiam7-chiam7 bo5-khi3.  Hia e5 kui-chek-tek e5 seng-oah8 soah chih8-cham7, boe7 an3-sng3-tit.  I e5 si5-kan chiam7-chiam7 kam2-kak leng2-tam7 bo5 chhu3-bi7.  Khiok A-hoa iau2 chiau3 si5-kan chiu7 oaN7-saN teh tan2-hau7 lau7-bu2.
Kau3 ti7 chit-e5 si5 lau7-bu2 chiu7 long2 bo5 chhoa7 A-hoa chhut-mng5 lah.  Sit-bang7 e5 A-hoa chiu7 long2 ti7 i e5 pang-keng lai5 ka-ki7 thit-tho5.  Ti7 A-hoa e5 pang5-keng u7 chit8-e5 thang, oe7-thang khoaN3-tioh8 tui3-bin7 e5 chit8-keng pang5-keng e5 kong-keng2.  Hit-e5 si7 keh-piah e5 soe3-kiaN2 A-long5 e5 a-ma2 e5 pang5-keng.  Tui3 chit-tiap8 A-hoa sou2 u7 e5 it-chhe3 chiu7-si7 kau3 ti7 chit-e5 thnag-a2-piN lai5 khoaN3 A-long5 e5 su7.
¡§A-ma2, goa2 tng2-lai5 lah!¡¨  A-long5 na7 tui3 hak8-hau7 tng2-lai5 chiu7 kau3 A-ma2 e5 pang5-keng, in-ui7 i kap A-ma2 cho3-hoe2 khun3.
¡§A-long5, li2 tng2-lai5 lah, tioh8-m7?!¡¨  Chit8-e5 chu5-pi e5 lau7 hu7-jin5-lang5 hoaN-thau5 hi2-bin7 chhut-lai5 pho7 A-long5.
¡§Li2 kin-a2-jit8 u7 kap lang5 oan-ke bo5!¡¨  A-ma2 chiu7 pang-chan7 A-long5 thng3-saN, khng3 i e5 hak8 eng7-phin2 lai5 an2-ni mng7 i.
¡§Goa2 bo5 ka7 lang5 phah, chong2-si7 A-seng tai7-seng ka7 goa2 phah, goa2 chiah ka7 i phah.¡¨  A-long5 chiu7 au3-bin7 au3-bin7 lai5 kong2.  Khiok A-ma2 sui5-si5 pian3 giam5 siok e5 bin7, thoa-oa2 A-long5 lai5 i e5 bin7-cheng5.
¡§A-long5, siat-su2 u7 lang5 ka7 li2 phah, li2 ia7 m7 thang phah-lang5, lan2 na7 phah-lang5 thiN-teng2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, in khoaN3 li2 chhut-chhiu2 phah lang5 e5 si5 beh chin tioh8-kiaN, chin iu-siong.  Lan2 hou7 Chu2 Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 bo5 hoaN-hi2 kiam2-ho2?!  Au7-pai2 tioh8 chu3-i3, taN chhiaN2 li2 ka7 goa2 kong2 goa2 m7 phah-lang5!¡¨  A-long5 it-hoat au3-bin7 khiau3-chhui3 lai5 kong2.
¡§Goa2 m7-phah lang5!¡¨  A-ma2 chin hoaN-hi2 e5 bin7 kong2, ¡§An2-ni chiah u7 koai, Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 long2 chin hoaN-hi2 A-long5; ia7 beh chiok-hok A-long5.  TaN chia u7 thng5-a2 hou7 li2 chiah8.¡¨
¡§Lan2 m7-thang phah-lang5, lan2 na7 phah-lang5 thiN-teng2 e5 Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, in beh chin kan-khou2 sim.¡¨  A-hoa sui5-si5 chiong chiah e5 oe7 lai5 ka3-si7 i e5 ang5-a2.
U7 chit8-jit8 A-hoa koh khoaN3-kiN3 A-long5 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, i e5 a-ma2 chiu7 koh mng7 i u7 koai a2-bo5.

¡§A-ma2, goa2 ti7 hak8-hau7 khioh-tioh8 chit8-kak, si7 A-nga2 ka-lauh8 e5, i bo5 hoaN3-kiN3 sou2-i2 goa2 ka7 khioh-lai5.¡¨  A-ma2 thiaN-tioh8 chit-e5 su7 chin tioh8-kiaN, ti3-kau3 i bo5 oe7 thang kong2 sim2-mih8.  A-ma2 chin kan-khou2-sim, sou2-i2 bo5 chek-pi7 i, kau3 hit chit8-am3 beh khun3 e5 si5, A-ma2 chiah kio3 A-long5 lai5 kau3 thang-a2 piN.  ¡§A-long5 li2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 hia e5 thiN-teng2 e5 chhiN bo5?¡¨  A-long5 e5 sim chiu7 bo5 peng5-an, si7 beng5-pek8 a-ma2 in-ui7 i khioh chiN5 e5 su7 teh bo5 hoaN-hi2.
¡§A-ma2 goa2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 moa2-thiN e5 chhiN!¡¨  ¡§A-long5, hia e5 chhiN long2 teh khoaN3 li2, hia e5 si7 thiN-sai3 e5 bak8-chiu, teh khoaN3 li2.  Li2 khioh e5 chiN5 theh8 chhut-lai5!¡¨  A-long5 tui3 i e5 te7-a2 jim5 chit8-kak gun5 khi2-lai5 hou7 a-ma2.  ¡§A-long5, chit-e5 chiN5 tioh8 koh theh8 khi3 heng5 A-nga2, A-nga2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, chong2-si7 thiN-teng2 e5 thiN-sai3 long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.¡¨
A-long5 chu3-sin5 lai5 khoaN3 hia E5 chhiN-sin5, long2 chhin-chhiuN7 teh gin5 i, hou7 i siN-chhut kiaN-hiaN5.  ¡§A-long5, li2 au7-pai2 m7-thang cho3 hit-ho7 am3-sam3 e5 su7, na7 an2-ni Ia5-sou m7-tih8 li2, a-ma2 ia7 m7-tih8 li2.¡¨  A-long5 khoaN3-kiN3 a-ma2 toa7 siu7-khi3 e5 bin7 soah hau2 chhut-lai5.  A-ma2 chiu7 kio3 A-long5 kui7-teh, lai5 chhoa7 i ki5-to2¡§Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 A-long5 bo5 tham-sim, bo5 cho3 am3-sam3 e5 su7, hou7 i u7 kng-beng5 e5 sim.¡¨
¡§Chu2 ah, kiu5 Li2 hou7 goa2 e5 eN-a2 bo5 tham-sim, bo5 cho3 am3-sam3 e5 su7, hou7 i u7 kng-beng5 e5 sim.¡¨  A-hoa keh cha2-khi2 chiu7 kui7 ti7 i e5 pang5-keng lai5 kap i e5 eN-a2 cho3 ki5-to2 e5 thit-tho5.  A-hoa kau3 am3-mi5 chiu7 eng7 ki5-koai3 e5 bak8-chiu lai5 khoaN3 hia e5 thiN-chhiN.  ¡§Ti7 hia u7 Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 e5 bak8-chiu long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.¡¨
A-hoa e5 seng-oah8 koh chin3-jip8 ti7 chit8-e5 sin e5 kai-toaN7 lah, i taN bo5 koh 
chheng7-saN lai5 tan2-hau7 iuN2 bu2 beh chhoa7 i chhut-khi3 lah.  I chi2-u7 ti7 thang-a2-piN lai5 tan2-hau7 A-long5 tng2-lai5, thang thiaN i e5 siaN, kap i saN-kap u7 hun7 long2-chong2 e5 hoaN-hi2 kap iu-siong.  Sou2-i2 A-long5 sou2 oe7-hiau2 gim5 e5 si5, A-hoa ia7 oe7-hiau2 gim5.
Keng-koe3 kui2 geh8-jit8 au7, ti7 chit-e5 ka-teng5 u7 ke-thiN chit8-e5 ta-pou eN-a2.  IuN2-bu2 e5 hoaN-hi2 boe7-thang heng5-iong5, in e5 sim-lai7 chiong-jit8 long2 chhiong-moa2 eN-a2 e5 su7, chhin-chhiuN7 tu2-tu2 chiah hoat-hian7 tioh8 seng-oah8 e5 i3-gi7, tu2-tu2 chiah kiN3-tioh8 jit8-kng chit8-iuN7, moa2-moa2 e5 heng7-hok khoai3-lok8.  In bo5-me5 bo5-jit8 lai5 chiau3-kou3 chit8-e5 chiang2-tiong e5 po2-poe3.
¡§Chin hok-siong3 e5 bin7, bak8-chiu chin u7 chai5-khi3!  Chit e5 eN-a2 toa7-han3 khi2-lai5 oe7 cho3 gau5 lang5, lan2 tioh8 lai5 boe2 chit8-nia2 siong7-teng2 e5 saN hou7 i chheng7, chit-ho7 peng5-siong5 e5 saN khah bo5 hah i, ia7 tioh8 chit8-nia2 chin kui3-khi3 e5 than2-na2, na7 khah toa7-han3 chiu7 thang am than2-na2 chhut-khi3 thit-tho5.  Koh bo5 ku2 chiu7 oe7 kiaN5, ia7 oe7 kong2 oe7, oe7 kio3 pa-pa ma-ma, lan2 chiu7 chhoa7 i kau3 iu3-ti7-hng5, i sou2 chheng7 e5 si7 te7-it sui2 e5 saN.  Ah, hit-e5 hoaN-hi2, hit-e5 heng7-hok!¡¨
IuN2 pe7-bu2 siong5-siong5 siuN7 kau3 chiah e5 su7 lai5 sim-moa2 i3-chiok.  Tui3 cha2 kau3 am3 long2 si7 teh kong2 eN-a2 e5 su7, ti7 chit e5 ka-teng5 e5 cheng5-tou5 u7 chin toa7 e5 hoaN-hi2 kap ng3-bang7.
Chong2-si7 A-hoa na2 kam2-kak tioh8 kou-tok8, iu-ut, tek8-piat na7 A-long5 khi3 thak8-chheh, i chiu7 kap i e5 ang5-a2 thit-tho5 kong2-oe7, u7-si5 tioh8 cho3 choa2 e5 saN, choa2 e5 oe5 hou7 i chheng7.
¡§Li2 si7 goa2 e5 eN-a2, goa2 e5 po2-poe3, goa2 beh cho3 chit8-nia2 chin sui2 e5 saN hou7 li2 chheng7, si7 peh8-sek e5 saN, na7 bo5, chiah-nih8 koaN5 goa2 e5 eN-a2 oe7 koaN5-tioh8, ouh, goa2 e5 eN-¡¥a2 na7 koaN5-tioh8, goa2 beh an2-choaN2,goa2 chiu7 siong-sim, goa2 beh kong2, goa2 e5 siN3-mia7, goa2 e5 khoai3-lok8!¡¨  A-hoa chiong iuN2-bu2 e5 oe7 lai5 teng5-sut8 ti7 i e5 ang5-a2.  Kau3 A-long5 beh tng2-lai5 e5 si5-khek, A-hoa chiu7 pang3-sak i e5 ang5-a2 lai5 ti7 thang-a2 piN tan2-hau7 i, ai3 beh thiaN in e5 oe7.

¡§A-ma2, goan2 kin-a2-jit8 u7 thiaN-tioh8 Liap8-sat-lou7 e5 kou3-su7.  Liap8-sat-lou7 si7 chit8-e5 kho2-lin5 e5 khit-chiah8.  I 011long2 bo5 pa-pa ma-ma, i ia7 bo5 chhu3, i to2 ti7 ho2-giah8 lang5 e5 mng5-khau2, lai5 khioh in e5 sut-a2 teh chiah8.  I ia7 bo5 lang5 beh koan-sim i, chi2-u7 kau2-a2 lai5 chiN7 i siN-thiaN3 e5 ui7.  I choan5-sin long2 siN-thiaN3, chin siu7-khou2.  Chong2-si7 i u7 sin3 Siong7-te3, siong5-siong5 giah8-bak8 giong2-bong7 thiN-teng2, sou2-i2 kau3-boe2 i si2 e5 si5 u7 chin toa7-kun5 e5 thiN-sai3 tui3 thiN kang3-loh8 lai5 ngia5-chih i chiuN7 thiN-teng2 khi3, kau3 ti7 lau7-pe7 A-pek-liap8-han2 e5 heng-cheng5.  Ti7 hia Liap8-sat-lou7 chin hoaN-hi2, chin khoai3-lok8, long2 bo5 koh thang3-thiaN3 siu7-khou2 lah.¡¨
A-long5 chiong i thiaN-tioh8 e5 kou3-su7 lai5 kong2 hou7 A-m7a thiaN.  Hit chit8-me5 A-hoa kiaN5-kau3 thang-a2-piN e5 si5, i chiu7 koh siuN7-tioh8 Liap8-sat-lou7 e5 su7 lai5 giah8-bak8 khoaN3-thiN an2-ni kong2.  ¡§Liap8-sat-lou7 ti7 hia bo5 koh siu7-khou2 lah!¡¨
U7 chit8 am3-tng3 iuN2 pe7-bu2 nng7-lang5 teh chiah8-png7 e5 si5 iuN2-pe7 hut-jian5 siuN7-tioh8 A-hoa.
¡§Lan2 soah long2 boe7 ki3-tit kio3 A-hoa chiah8-png7!¡¨  IuN2-pe7 chiu7 khi2-lai5 kio3 A-hoa.
¡§A-hoa, li2 tioh8 ka-ki7 loh8 lai5 chiah8-png7, m7-thang hou7 lang5 kio3, goan2 long2 chin bo5-eng5.¡¨  IuN2-bu2 khoaN3-tioh8 A-hoa che7-ui7 ho2-se3 e5 si5 chiu7 an2-ni kong2.
¡§Goan2 sit8-chai7 chin bo5-eng5!¡¨  Keh kui2-jit8 iuN2-pe7 koh hoat-kak A-hoa bo5 loh8-lai5 chiah8-png7, i chiu7 beh khi3 kio3 i, khiok iuN2-bu2 chiu7 kong2, ¡§Bo5 iau3-kin2, i ka- ki7 oe7 loh8-lai5 chiah8.¡¨  Tui3 an2-ni liau2-au7 in chiu7 long2 bo5 koh kau3 lau5-thui kha khi3 kio3 A-hoa chiah8-png7.
A-hoa e5 kou-tok8 na2 chhim-tim5, i ti7 chit e5 ka-teng5 kam2-kak chin leng2-tam7 put-heng7.
Chit e5 cheng5-keng2 koe3 liau2 saN si3 geh8-jit8, eN-a2 i2-keng chin sim-sek lah.
EN-a2 oe7 sng2-chhio3 lah, oe7 eng7 chin kou2-chui e5 bak8-chiu teh jin7 lang5 lah!  
Lan2 oe7-thang pho7 i chhut-goathit7-tho5 lah.  IuN2-bu2 chiu7 khai-si2 pho7 eN-a2 chhut-mng5.  ¡§A-hoa, li2 tioh8 tiam3 chhu3-nih8 kou3 chhu3, goa2 beh pho7 eN-a2 chhut-khi3.¡¨  IuN2-bu2 chiu7 kau3 A-hoa e5 pang5-keng lai5 an2-ni kong2.  A-hoa u7 thiaN-kiN3 iuN2-bu2 loh8-lai5, ti7 lau5-e7 teh kap lang5 kong2-oe7, koaiN-mng5 chhut-khi3 e5 siaN.  Chhu3-lai7 long2 an-cheng7 khi3 e5 si5, A-hoa chiu7 chhiN-leng2-sun2 chit8-e7.  A-hoa ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7 u7 kam2-kak siu7 khi3-sak e5 pi-ai kap kou-tok8 e5 iu-siong.
Khiok i chiu7 pho7 i e5 ang5-a2 lai5 saN-kap cho3 Liap8-sat-lou7 e5 iu5-hi3.
¡§Kho2-lin5 e5 Liap8-sat-lou7 si2-khi3 lah.  U7 chin-choe7 peh8-saN e5 thiN-sai3 gim5-si loh8 lai5 kau3 Liap8-sat-lou7 e5ui.¡¨ ¡§Kho2-lin5 e5 Liap8-sat-lou7, li2 e5 siu7-khou2 i2-keng soah lah.  TithiN7-teng2 u7 pi7-pan7 li2 e5 ui7, hou7 li2 jip8 ti7 an-hioh kap khoai3-lok8.¡¨  ¡§Liap8-sat-lou7 ti7 thiN-sai3 e5 tiong-kan, bo5 koh kou-toaN iu-siong, in-ui7 thiN-sai3 long2 teh gim5-si thiau3-bu2 hou7 Liap8-sat-lou7 khoaN3.¡¨
¡§La-la-la-la-la, la-la-la-la-la.¡¨A-hoa khai-si2 gim5-si thiau3-bu2 khi2-lai5.
Kau3 chit e5 si5 iuN2-bu2 soah ia7 long2 bo5 koh tui3 A-hoa kong2 i beh chhut-khi3, i chi2-u7 so2 mng5 khi2-lai5, chiu7 cho3 i khi3.  Ti7 i e5 bak8-chiu lai7 A-hoa e5 chun5-chai7 long2 bo5-khi3 lah.  Kau3 ti7 siuN7-tioh8 A-hoa e5 si5, i kam2-kak A-hoa si7 chit8-e5 oan5-choan5 bo5 su-iau3, bo5 i-su3 e5 lang5.
¡§Li2 a-chai u7 kam2-kak A-hoa kin7-lai5 chin koh-iuN7 a2-bo5?¡¨  U7 chit8-me5 iuN2-bu2 ti7 chhng5-nih8 e5 si5 an2-ni tui3 iuN2-pe7 mng7.
¡§A-hoa chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-e5 gu5-gong7 e5 gin2-na2, soah long2 boe7 kong2-oe7, lian7 chiah8-png7 ia7 m7-chai thang chiah8, saN-khou3 long2 boe7-hiau2 oaN7.¡¨  IuN2-bu2 an2-ni kong2 lai5 giah8 i e5 keng-thau5 piau2-si7 chin sit-bang7.
¡§A-hoa iau2 chin soe3-han3, sit8-chai7 tioh8 koh lang5 pang-chan7 i.¡¨ IuN2-pe7 an2-ni in3.
¡§Goa2 khoaN3 i m7-si7 chit8-e5 peng5-siong5 e5 gin2-na2, cheng5 ia7 m7-si7 an2-ni.¡¨  IuN2-bu2 chin siong-sim e5 khoan2.  ¡§Lan2 chhi7 chit e5 tu3-gong7 e5 gin2-na2 u7 sim2-mih8 ng3-bang7.¡¨

¡§Chong2-si7 kiam2 u7 pat8-e5 hoat-tou7, ki3-jian5 pun lai5 chhi7 lah.¡¨  IuN2-pe7 kong2.
¡§Goa2 siuN7 lan2 chiong A-hoa pun hou7 pat8-lang5 chhi7, tui3 ti7 lan2 kap i long2 u7 li7-ek.¡¨  IuN2-bu2 e5 bin7 chin koat-i3.  ¡§Kiam2 u7 lang5 beh chhi7 i?¡¨  IuN2-pe7 e5 bin7 siap-siap.  ¡§Hit e5 tiam phoe5-oe5 e5 A-hoa u7 teh kong2 ai3 pun chit8-e5 chhin-chhiuN7 A-hoa hit-khoan2 e5 gin2-na2, lan2 lai5 pun hou7 in, in kiat-hun chiaN5 chap8-ni5, hu7-jin5 lang5 khiok iau2 bo5 u7 gin2-na2.¡¨  IuN2-pe7 an-cheng7 bo5 in3 sim2-mih8.
Tui3 iuN2-bu2 the5-chhut chit e5 su7 liau2-au7 bo5 loa7-ku2, u7 chit8 cha2-khi2 u7 chit8-tui3 e5 tiong-lian5 e5 ang-bou2 chhoa7 lai5 hong2-bun7 chit e5 ka-teng5.  Tiong7-hu si7 chit8-e5 lo3-lo3 san2-san2 si3-chap8 goa7 hoe3 e5 tiong-sit8 lang5.  Hu7-jin5 lang5 si7 oe2-oe2 pui5-pui5 bo5 chheng-chhai2 e5 bin7.  Tiong7-hu tiam7-tiam7, chong2-si7 hu7-jin5 lang5 tui3 thau5 kau3 boe2 tit8-tit8 kong2 oe7 bo5 soah.  IuN2-bu2 chhoa7 in kau3 lau5-teng2 e5 si5, chiu7 chi2 A-hoa hou7 in khoaN3.
¡§Sou2 kong2 e5 gin2-na2 chiu7-si7 chit e5.¡¨
IuN2-bu2 kong2, ¡§Chit e5 chiu7-si7 A-hoa ouh?¡¨  Tiam phoe5-oe5 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 khai-si2 tui3 thau5 kau3 boe2 lai5 kam3-chhat A-hoa e5 sin-chiuN7.  Hit e5 chinN gin3-gin3 e5 bak8-chiu, chhou-toa7 e5 siaN, bo5 chheng-chhai2 e5 bin7 hou7 A-hoa chin tam2-sim.
¡§An2-ni ho2, goa2 koat-teng7 beh chhoa7 chit e5 gin2-na2 tng2-khi3, kaN u7 gou7-hoe3 lah houN3?  I ia7 oe7 ka7 goa2 piaN3-sau3 cheng2-li2 lai7-bin7, eN-a2 na7 chhut-si3 ia7 oe7 ka7 goa2 aiN7 khi3 goa7-bin7 thit-tho5, koh khah khi3, ia7 oe7 ka7 goa2 chu2-png7.¡¨  Chit e5 phaiN2-khoaN3 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 teh cho3-bang7 e5 khoan2 lai5 an2-ni kong2, khiok tiam7-tiam7 tiong-sit8 e5 tiong7-hu bin7 ng3 chhu3-teng2, chhin-chhiuN7 kong2, ¡§Goa2 long2 bo5 teh thiaN li2 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.¡¨
Ti7 goan2 chia goa2 long2 bo5 hou7 i cho3 sim2-mih8 kang, goan2 sit8-chai7 chin ho2 khoan2-thai7 i.¡¨  IuN2-bu2 chiu7 an2-ni kong2. 
¡§A-hoa, chit e5 a-peh a-m2 beh chhoa7 li2 khi3 in tau, li2 u7 hoa-hi2 khi3 bo5?¡¨  IuN2-bu2 chiu7 khut-sin lai5 mng7 A-hoa.  A-hoa long2 m7 chai-iaN2 tioh8 in3 sim2-mih8, i chi2-u7 eng7 tioh8-kiaN e5 bak8-chiu lai5 khoaN3 chit-e5 m7-bat e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 bin7.  A-hoa ka-leng2 sun2 chit8-e7--, in-ui7 beng5-pek8 i tioh8 ai3 toe3 chit-e5 thang kho2-gi5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 khi3.  Sou2-i2 i bo5 kong2 sim2-mih8, chi2-u7 khai-si2 chheng7 i e5 oe5, theh8 i e5 ang5-a2, ti3 i e5 bo5-a2.
IuN2-bu2 ia7 beng5-pek8 A-hoa e5 in3-tap, chiu7 theh8 chit8-nng7 nia2 khah ho2 e5 saN hou7 A-hoa.
¡§Goan2 cho3 chin-choe7 saN hou7 i chheng7 liau2 lah, chit-siang khah ho2 e5 oe5 li2 ia7 thang theh8-khi3..., goan2 ui7-tioh8 A-hoa eng7 chin-choe7 chiN5 lah.¡¨  IuN2-bu2 ka-ki7 an2-ni liam7.
¡§Chiah-nih8 toa7-han3 boe7-oe7 si-pun2, tioh8 hou7 i choe3 kang.  An2-ni ho2, goan2 beh chhoa7 i lai5 khi3 lah.¡¨
Hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 khan A-hoa e5 chhiu2 lai5 loh8 lau5-thui.  A-peh ia7 tiam7-tiam7 ia7 toe3 in e5 au7-bin7.
A-hoa chiam7-chiam7 li7-khui chit-e5 ku2-ku2 sou2 toa3 e5 chhu3.  I oat8-thau5 lai5 khoaN3 A-long5 e5 thang-a2, hut-jian5 u7 bak8-sai2 lau5 chhut-lai5.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 chhiu2 an5-an5 chhin-chhiuN7 chhiu2-kha3 liah8 i.
2 A-HOA THOAT-CHHUT CHHIM-IAN
Tiam phoe5-oe5 e5 A-peh si7 toa3 ti7 chit8-e5 hang7-lou7 e5 piN-kak.  Tui3 toa7-lou7 jip8 chit8 e5 sio2 hang7-lou7, kiaN5 kau3 hang7-boe2, u7 chit8-keng ku7-ku7 la5-sam5 e5 chhu3, chit-keng chiu7-si7 in e5 chhu3.  U7 A-peh cho3 kang e5 sou2-chai7, ia7 cho3 chiah8-png7 thiaN kiam kheh-thiaN, koh u7 chit8-keng pang5-keng, ia7 u7 chit8-keng chau3-kha.  A-hoa e5 chhng5 si7 siat ti7 A-peh teh cho3 kang e5 piN-kak e5 sou2-chai7, ti7 hia u7 ke7-ke7 e5 chha5-siuN, teng2-bin7 u7 chhu chhau2-chhioh8.

Lai7-bin7 e5 mih8-kiaN7 long2 bo5 cheng2-che5, chin hok8-chap8 loan7-soaN3 chit8-tiuN5.  U7 ke-kak thiau3 chiuN7 toh-teng2 teh chiah8-mih8, u7 la5-sam5 iau2 ti7 pang-keng.  Chiah e5 kong-keng2 teh cheng3-beng5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 jin5-but8.  I jip8 mng5 chiu7 khai-si2 me7 ke, theng5 bo5 ku2 niau-a2 tioh8 koh thau chiah8 i e5 hi5, i chiu7 phah niau-a2, koh toa7 me7 hit-chiah niau-a2.  I e5 chhui3 long2 bo5 hioh-khun3 teh me7.  Khiok A-peh chhin-chhiuN7 long2 bo5 khoaN3 tioh8 bo5 thiaN tioh8 sim2-mih8 e5 khoan2, ti7 i e5 sou2-chai7 teh cho3 kang. I e5 bin7 long2 m7-kaN2 khoaN3 pat8-ui7, i e5 sim u7 teh tiuN-ti5, kiaN-liau2 hit e5 thang-kiaN e5 loe2-me7 oe7 choan2-kau3 i e5 sin-chiuN7.  Ko2-jian5 u7-iaN2, chu2-hu7 chiu7 hiong3 A-peh lai5 toa7-me7 i, kong2 i bo5 siu chiah8-mih8 hou7 ho2-se3, koh bo5 koaN2 niau-a2 chau2.  A-hoa chi2-u7 che7 ti7 i e5 chhng5-ui7 lai5 teh kam3-chhat chiah e5 cheng5-heng5.  I e5 sim chin kin2-tiuN, chhin-chhiuN7 chhoan2-khui3 ia7 khun3-lan5.  Kau3 ti7 chu2-hu7 kio3 A-hoa e5 mia5 e5 si5, A-hoa chiu7 sim-cheng5 chin kip lai5 in3 i.  ¡§Ma-ma goa2 ti7 chia.¡¨  ¡§An2-ni tioh8!  Li2 tioh8 kio3 goa2 ma-ma, chong2-si7 goa2 siuN7 kio3 goa2 A-bu2 khah ho2.¡¨  Chu2-hu7 e5 sim u7 tam7-poh8 hoaN-hi2 si7 in-ui7 u7 lang5 kio3 i ma-ma.
¡§A-hoa li2 m7-thang thit-tho5 ang5-a2, ti7 chia tioh8 cho3 kang.¡¨  Chu2-hu7 kin7-oa2 A-hoa lai5, tui3 i e5 chhiu2 chhiuN2 ang5-a2 khi2-lai5.  ¡§Chia u7 sau3-chhiu2, hia u7 toh-pou3, tioh8 ai3 cho3 kang.¡¨  A-bu2 chiu7 giah8 sau3-chhiu2 hou7 A-hoa, koh soah chi2-si7 i tioh8 cho3 e5 kang.
A-hoa chiu7 khai-si2 lai5 sau3-te3.  I tu2-tu2 si7 moa2 gou7-hoe3 e5 gin2-na2, chong2-si7 chiau3-khoaN3 si7 si3-hoe3 na7-tiaN7, iau2-ku2 chin soe3-han3.  A-hoa chin chhong-beng5 pun2-su7, sou2-i2 chiah oe7-thang eng3-hu3 chit e5 bo5-li2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5.
Keng-koe3 lak8 ge8-jit8 au7, lin2 na7 siat-su2 koh khoaN3-tioh8 A-hoa, lan2 beh tioh8-kiaN koh ui7-tioh8 i lai5 siong-sim.  Ti7 chhu3-lai7 it-chhe3 iu5-goan5 si7 chin loan7-chap8, la5-sam5.  Hu7-jin5-lang5 na7 m7-si7 teh khun3 chiu7-si7 ti7 chhu3-piN teh kong2 eng5-oe7, na7 bo5 chiu7 ti7 chhu3-lai7 teh jiang2-loan7.  A-peh tak8-si5 long2 tiam7-tiam7 bo5 kong2-oe7 teh cho3 kang.  I chit8-poaN3 khah-ke e5 si5-kan long2 taN taN3 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 teh cho3 kang.  Khiok A-hoa lan2 hiam2-hiam2 tioh8 boe7 jin7-tit i, in-ui7 i piN3-chiaN5 chit8-e5 chin la5-sam5 phaiN2-khoaN3 e5 gin2-na2, i e5 bin7 chin chiau-chui7, i e5 kha-chhiu2 kap sin-khu long2 u7 siu7 phah e5 siong-hun5.

I goan5-lai5 si7 chit8-e5 beng5-long2 oah8-phoat e5 gin2-na2, iau2-ku2 ti7 chit e5 khoan5-keng2 hou7 i u7 chin toa7 e5 khoa3-sim, kiaN-liau2 u7 sim2-mih8 kang-chok cho3 bo5 ho2-se3 koh hou7 lau7-bu2 phah me7.  Sou2-i2 lau7-bu2 na7 ti7 chhu3-lai7 e5 si5, ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7 long2 bo5 u7 chit8 si5-khek e5 peng5-an.  A-hoa e5 kha-chhiu2 long2 bo5 si5-theng5 teh cho3 kang, in-ui7 chai-iaN2 na7 an2-ni cho3 oe7-thang tam7-poh8 kiam2-chio2 lau7-bu2 e5 hoat-seng3.  Sou2-i2 sui-jian5 long2 bo5 sim2-mih8 thang cho3, iau2-ku2 A-hoa e5 kha-chhiu2 tioh8 ke3-siok8 tong7-chok.  Ti3-kau3 A-hoa e5 sim tit8-tit8 ng3-bang7 A-bu2 bo5 ti7 chhu3-lai7 a2-si7 khi3 khun3, thang tit-tioh8 tam7-poh8 e5 pang3-sim kap chu7-iu5.  Na7 khoaN3-kiN3 A-bu2 chhut mng5-khau2, i chiu7 pang3 i e5 sau3-chhiu2 a2-si7 toh-pou3, thou3 chit8-e5 khui3, lai5 che7 ti7 thou5-kha, eng7 sui5-pian7 e5 mih8-kiaN7 lai5 cho3 ang5-a2, kap niau-a2 kong2-oe7, cho3 hi3 hou7 niau-a2 khoaN3, chiong2-chiong2 thian-chin e5 iu5-hi3.  Niau-a2 Li7-li7 si7 i ho2 e5 peng5-iu2, i siong5-siong5 kap niau-a2 cho3-hoe2 kong2-oe7.  ¡§Si2 niau-a2, li2 chin bo5 lou7-eng7, li2 tak8-jit8 long2 teh thit-tho5, long2 m7 cho3 kang.  Ho2!  E7-am3 tek-khak m7 hou7 li2 chiah8-png7!¡¨
A-hoa oh8 A-bu2 e5 khau2-khi3 lai5 me7 niau-a2, u7 si5 tioh8 ke2-iaN2 phah niau-a2.  Khiok chit chiah niau-a2 si7 A-hoa ti7 hoan7-lan7 tiong e5 ho2 tang5-phoaN7.  I ia7 kap niau-a2 saN-kap thiau3-bu2, ia7 ka3 niau-a2 gim5-si.
¡§Li2 chin-chiaN3 long2 bo5 lou7-eng7!  Ka7 li2 ka3 hiah-nih8 choe7-pai2 li2 long2 boe7-hiau2-tit!  Tioh8 an2-ni pi2 lah, siang-chhiu2 khui-khui, thau5-khak oai-oai, kha tioh8 khut-khut, ai3-ah, li2 chit e5 si2-mih8 long2 boe7-hiau2-tit, li2 si7 to2-ui7 e5 iam3-chian7 mih8, chiah-nih8 gong7, chiah-nih8 khiap-si3!¡¨
¡§Chit teng2 si7 goa2 e5 bo5-a2, goa2 cho3 sin-niu5 e5 si5 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 sang3 goa2 e5--, chit-teng2 si7 goa2 e5 po2-poe3, in-ui7 chit-si5 long2 bo5 thang boe2 chit-khoan2 e5 mih8.¡¨
¡§U7 chin ho2-khoaN3 bo5?  Tek-khak u7!  Kho2-sioh goa2 long2 bo5 eN-a2, na7-u7 goa2 e5 eN-a2 toa7-han3 e5 si5, goa2 beh sang3 goa2 e5 bo5-a2 hou7 i, i tek-khak chin-sui2!¡¨
¡§An2-ni tioh8, an2-ni tioh8!  M7-thang thng3 khi2-lai5, ai3-ah, li2 chit e5 phaiN2-mih8 sit8-chai7 chin gong7!¡¨

A-hoa u7 thian-seng3 e5 chhong-beng5 kap ki3-ek, lai5 teng5-sut8 A-bu2 ti7 tam7-oe7 tiong sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.
¡§Chit e5 gin2-a2 koh kap niau-a2 teh cho3 sng2 thit-tho5!¡¨  Hut-jian5 A-bu2 e5 siaN hou7 A-hoa tioh8-kiaN.  ¡§Li2 khoaN3, ke-kak koh thiau3-khi3 toh-teng2 teh chiah8-png7 lah!¡¨  Ko2-jian5 u7-iaN2 toh-teng2 e5 png7 hou7 ke chheng2 kau3 moa2 si3-koe3.  A-bu2 chin toa7 siu7-khi3 lai5 giah8 tiau3 ti7 piah-teng2 e5 chhoe5 khi2-lai5 phah A-hoa.
¡§A-bu2 m7-kaN2 lah, A-bu2 m7-kaN2 lah!¡¨  Chai-lan7 ti7 bo5 gi5-gou7 e5 tiong-kan koh lim5-kau3 lai5 kio3-hoe5 A-hoa kau3 ti7 chit e5 pi-chham2 put-heng7 e5 hian7-sit8.
¡§Si2-kui2, li2 i2-au7 m7-thang kio3 goa2 a-bu2!¡¨  Tui3 an2-ni A-hoa chiu7 bo5 kio3 i a-bu2, si7 chiau3 boe7-chhai3 e5 lang5 kio3 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, ¡§Thau5-ke-niu5.¡¨
TaN chit e5 tau5-ke-niu5 mi5-jit8 su-liam7, ai3 siN chit8-e5 eN-a2.  ¡§Goa2 liam-piN beh u7 gin2-na2 lah!¡¨  Thau5-ke niu ka7 i chhin-bit8 e5 chhu3-piN kong2.  I ia7 siong-sin3 i beh u7 gin2-na2.  Chiu7 mi5-jit8 to2 chhnng5. ¡§Lan2 e5 siu-jip8 siuN-chio2, gin2-na2 na7 chhut-si3 beh an2-choaN2 seng-oah8!¡¨  Thau5-ke niu5 tioh8 tui3 A-peh an2-ni kong2, m7-si7 kong2, si7 an2-ni jiong2 lai5 ui-hat i.  Chong2-si7 A-peh e5 sim-lai7 teh chhio3, ¡§Hi, hi, li2 beh siN chit8-e5 kui2 lah!¡¨
Thau5-ke niu5 tak8-jit8 teh khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 pian3-hoa3 a2-bo5, u7-si5 ti7 mi5-si5 khoaN3 chhin-chhiuN7 u7, kau3 cha2-khi2 si5 koh tioh8 pian3 bo5.  Iau2-ku2 i tak8-jit8 siuN7 kong2 i u7 gin2-na2 lai5 teh tan2-hau7.
¡§Goa2 teh beh u7 gin2-na2 lah, sou2-i2 A-hoa i2-au7 tioh8 hu7-tam chu2-png7, gin2-na2 na7 chhut-si3 tioh8 hu7-tam aiN7 gin2-na2.¡¨  A-hoa e5 tang7-taN3 tit8-tit8 ke-thiN, i e5 siu7-khou2 ia7 na2 chhim.
Chong2-si7 koh keng-koe3 poaN3-ni5,thau5-ke niu5 long2 bo5 u7 gin2-na2, i chin choat8-bang7, chin oan3-chheh, chiu7 koh-khah ke-thiN hoat-seng3 lai5 khou2-chhou2 kiau2-jiau2 chhu3-lai7.  In-ui7 an2-ni A-peh chiu7 chha-put-to long2 chhut-khi3 ti7 goa7-bin7, cha2-cha2 chhut, am3-am3 chiah jip8-mng5, si7 beh to5-siam2 chit e5 hiong5-ok ia2-ban5 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5.

Khiok A-hoa bo5 hoat-tou7 thang to5-siam2, chiu7 it-chhe3 e5 chai-hai7 long2 lim5-kau3 ti7 i loan2-jiok8 e5 sin-chiuN7.
Kho2-lin5 e5 A-hoa, i e5 bin7 soah piN3 chhin-chhiuN7 lau7-lang5 e5 bin7, i e5 iuN7-siuN3 chin la5-sam5 thang-kiaN.  Thau5-ke niu5 tak8-jit8 long2 u7 li2-iu5 lai5 phah i, sou2-i2 i ia7 ba5-phoe5 ba5-phoe5, hou7 i phah a2-si7 liam3, u7 thang chiah8 a2-si7 bo5 thang chiah8 long2 bo5 liah8-cho3 sim2-mih8 lai5 kan-khou2, ui7-tioh8 thit-tho5 hou7 lang5 phah, chong2-si7 phah-liau2 i iu5-goan5 koh thit-tho5.  Chhoe5-kau3 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7 e5 si5 ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 long2 bo5 kam2-kak oe7 thiaN3 e5 khoan2.
Thau5-ke-niu5 na7 ti7 chhu3-lai7, i chiu7 ke2 choe3 kang lai5 tin2-tang7 kha-chhiu2, na7 bo5 chiu7 khai-si2 thit-tho5.
¡§Niau-bi5, li2 chin bai2, Li2 long2 boe7 cho3 sim2-mih8, Goa2 beh liah8 li2 khi3 pang3-seN, Kau3 ti7 chhim-soaN khong3-ia2, Hou7 li2 kou-toaN bo5-lou7, Am3-mi5 u7 phaiN2-mih8 e5 sou2-chai7.
Li2 beh hau2, goa2 e5 chhu3, Goa2 e5 chhu3 ti7 to2-ui7, Chhiu7-na5 lai7 e5 am3-kong-chiau2 beh kong2, PhaiN2-khoaN3 bo5 chhu3 e5 sio2-niau, Li2 e5 chhu3 ti7 thiN-chhiN e5 teng2-koan5, Chhai2-kheng7 e5 boe2-liu, Hng7-hng7 poaN5-koe3 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu.¡¨
A-hoa e5 keh-piah u7 chit8-e5 eN-a2 kio3-cho3 A-gi7.  I e5 ma-ma tak8-jit8 tioh8 liam7 chin-choe7 io5-na5 si lai5 io5 A-gi7 khun3.
U7 chit8-pai2 A-gi7 e5 a-pa ti7 me5-si5 jip8-mng5 e5 si5, i chiu7 tui3 ma-ma kong2.
¡§Goa2 tu2-chiah beh tng2-lai5 e5 si5, ti7 hit e5 hang7-lou7 u7 tu2-tioh8 chit8-chiah kau2-a2, hit-chiah kau2-a2 hou7 goa2 chin ki5-koai3, in-ui7 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 teh gim5-si e5 khoan2, chau2 tui3 goa2 e5 sin-piN koe3-khi3.¡¨  A-pa chin put-kho2 su-gi5 e5 bin7.  Chong2-si7 ma-ma sui5-si5 lai5 kai2-tap chit e5 su7.
¡§Hit e5 m7-si7 kau2-a2 lah, si7 keh-piah e5 gin2-na2 A-hoa lah!¡¨
¡§Chong2-si7 goa2 u7 thiaN-kiN3 chau2 kau3 hang7-thau5 e5 si5 u7 kaiN chit8-siaN.¡¨  
¡§M7-si7 lah, hit e5 si7 A-hoa in-ui7 kiaN teh hau2 e5 siaN lah, hit cham7 lou7 chin am3-sam3, A-hoa na7 chau2 kau3 hit sou2-chai7 tek-khak tioh8 hau2 chit8-siaN lah.¡¨
¡§Chong2-si7 hiah-nih8 soe3-han3 chiah am3 beh khi3 to2-ui7?¡¨  A-pa e5 bin7 iau2 khah put-kho2 su-gi5.  ¡§Thau5-ke-niu5 kio3 i tioh8 khi3 boe2 tiam2-sim¡¨, ma-ma an2-ni kong2.  A-pa ti7 i e5 chhui3-lai7 an2-ni liam7, ¡§Hiah-nih8 soe3-han3 kiam2 oe7-thang cho3 hit khoan2 e5 su7.¡¨
A-gi7 in pe7-bu2 long2 to2-chhng5 khi3 khun3 e5 si5, hut-jian5 u7 thiaN-tioh8 chit8 e5 iN7-siong5 e5 siaN.
¡§Sim2-mih8 lang5 ti7 toa7-lou7 teh sio-phah!¡¨  A-pa kin2-kin2 khi2-sin beh khi2-lai5, chong2-si7 ma-ma chhun-chhiu2 chou2-tong3 i kong2, ¡§Hit e5 m7-si7 teh sio-phah, si7 keh-piah e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 teh phah-me7 A-hoa lah!¡¨  ¡§Ui7 sim2-mih8 chiah am3 teh phah-me7 hiah-nih8 soe3-han3 e5 gin2-na2?!¡¨  A-pa e5 bin7 chin kat.  ¡§Phah-sng3 si7 boe2 m7-tioh8 mih8 tng2-lai5, na7 bo5 chiu7-si7 chhia-to2 mih8 lah!¡¨  ¡§Chin kho2-lin5, hiah-nih8 soe3-han3 beh kio3 i cho3 sim2-mih8!¡¨  A-pa thou3 chit8-e5 khui3, koh to2 loh8-khi3.
¡§Sou2-i2 tak8-jit8 tek-khak tui3 cha2-khi2 phah kau3 poaN3-me5.  Goa2 i2-keng chin koan3-si3 lah!¡¨  In nng7-lang5 long2 tiam7-tiam7, chong2-si7 in e5 sim-lai7 iau2-ku2 ui7-tioh8 A-hoa kap thau5-ke niu5, chit nng7-e5 jin5-but8 lai5 teh kan-khou2 sim.
Ko2-jian5 keh cha2-khi2 chin cha2 A-hoa chiu7 siu7 kio3 khi2-lai5 chu2-png7.  I2-keng si7 chin-koaN5 e5 ji7-geh8 thiN lah!  A-hoa siuN7 beh thau-eng7 lai7-bin7 e5 chui2, chong2-si7 sui5-si5 siu7 hoat-kak, chiu7 chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 chhiuN7-chui2, jip8-lai5 soe2-bi2 chu2-moe5.  Liau2-au7 i chiam7-si5 khut-sin lai5 bih-koaN5, niau-a2 ia7 thiau3-jip8 ti7 i e5 hoai5-tiong.
I sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 i2-keng koe3-thau5 ti7 i sou2 oe7-thang tam-tng, koaN5-leng2 kap ia3-sian7 kau-pek ti7 i loan2-jiok8 e5 sin-the2, hou7 i kho2-ai3 e5 thian-seng3 long2 siau-biat8 khi3.
I ia7 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 pat8 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 e5 ka-teng5, heng7-hok khoai3-lok8 e5 seng-oah8, lau7-bu2 thiaN3 kiaN2, ka-teng5 thoan5-lok8 e5 cheng5-heng5 lai5 mou7-hong2 in e5 kong2-oe7, khiok i e5 sim m7-chai sim2-mih8 si7 him-soan7, oan3-than3.  It-chhe3 e5 
put-heng7 ti7 i put-ko3 si7 chu7-jian5 e5 su7.  ¡§Si2-mih8, moe5 phu7 chhut-lai5 iau2 m7-chai!¡¨  A-hoa ti7 poaN3 tu3-bin5 e5 tiong-kan u7 koh thiaN-tioh8 thau5-ke niu5 hiong5-ok e5 siaN teh jiong2, i chiah chai-iaN2 chit e5 sio-lo7 e5 hoe2-lou5 hou7 i khun3-khi3.  Thau5-ke niu5 tui3 pang5-keng chau2 chhut-lai5, thau5-mng5 sam3-sam3 hiong5-ok e5 bak8-chiu, thang-kiaN e5 heng5-chong7 lai5 kau3 A-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 chiu7 chiong A-hoa hiong5-hiong5 thoa tui3 au7-bin7 khi3.  A-hoa chiu7 poah8-to2 ti7 thou5-kha.  ¡§Thau5-ke niu5 ah, m7-kaN2 lah!¡¨  ¡§M7-kaN2 khi3 si2!¡¨  Thau5-ke niu5 an2-ni toa7 siaN jiong2 soa3 eng7 moe5-siah lai5 phah seN-oe hou7 i piak chit8 e5--lai5 chan7 i e5 hiong5-se3.
¡§Si2-kui2, long2 boe7-che3 sim2-mih8, cha2-khi2 tek-khak m7 hou7 li2 chiah8, koh beh hou7 li2 kui7, tek-khak beh hou7 li2 kio3 khou2!¡¨  Thau5-ke niu5 ke3-siok8 jiong2-me7 phah-loan7 bo5 soah.  A-hoa tiam7-tiam7 khia7 teh, eng7 kha-chng-thau5-a2 lai5 ngeh niau-bi5 e5 boe2. A-peh ia7 khi2-lai5 lah, chiu7 teh khoan2 taN3 beh chhut mng5, si7 in-ui7 kiaN liau2 loe2-me7 oe7 kau3 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7, chiu7 ti7 thau5-ke niu5 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 si5 beh siam2 chhut-khi3, khiok kau3 mng5-khau2 e5 si5 siu7 hoat-kian3 tioh8.
¡§Li2 hiah-nih8 cha2 beh khi3 to2-ui7 si2!¡¨  Thau5-ke niu5 chiu7 toa7-siaN lai5 me7 i.  A-peh m7-kaN2 tin2-tang7.  ¡§Jip8 lai5 chiah8 moe5!¡¨  A-peh chiu7 koh taN taN3 jip8 lai5, koh che7 ti7 i2 lai5 tan2-hau7 chiah8 moe5.  Hit e5 cheng5-heng5 tu2-tu2 si7 sio2-hak8 e5 gin2-na2 hoan7-choe7 teh kiaN lau7-bu2 chit8-iuN7, ti3-kau3 hou7 A-hoa ia7 kam2-kak ho2 chhio3.
Thau5-ke-niu5 e5 chhui3 ke3-siok8 teh me7, kau3 chiah8-png7 e5 si5 iau2-ku2 bo5 soah, chiah8 chit8-chhui3 me7 chit8-chhui3, long2 bo5 leng2-cheng7.
A-hoa ti7 hit-e5 si5-kan chiu7 che7 ti7 thou5-kha lai5 kap niau-a2 thit-tho5.
Kho-lin5 bo5 chhu3 e5 sio2-niau, Li2 si7 tui3 to2-ui7 chit8-kok lai5, ChhiN-sin5 e5 teng2-koan5 chhai2-kheng7 e5 boe2-liu, Hng7-hng7 poaN5-koe3 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu.
Li2 siang-kha tah8 ti7 ou-am3 e5 tin5-se3, Li2 e5 sim khiok bang7-siong2 bo5 soah, Sun5-chin si7 li2 e5 mia5, Chin-sit8 si7 li2 un2-bat8 e5 sit-giau2.

Thau5-ke-niu5 chiah8-pa2 e5 si5 ko2-jian5 chiu7 kio3 A-hoa khi3 kui7.  ¡§Khi3 kui7!  Goa2 siuN7 long2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang hou7 li2 kio3 khou2, goa2 m7 sin3 goa2 long2 bo5 hoat-tou7!¡¨  A-hoa chiu7 kiaN5-kau3 sou2 chi2-teng7 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 kui7 ti7 thou5-kha.  Thau5-ke-niu5 ke3-siok8 chau7-chau7 me7.  A-peh kin2-kin2 liam kha-chhiu2 lai5 liu chhut-khi3.
¡§Ki5-to2 e5 si5 chhiu2 tioh8 hap8-hap8, bak8-chiu tioh8 ng3 thiN-teng2, ti7 hia u7 Ia5-sou, u7 thiN-sai3, u7 Siong7-te3 e5 po2-cho7 teh thiaN lan2 e5 ki5-to2.¡¨
Niau-a2 oa2 lai5 e5 si5 A-hoa chiu7 an2-ni soat-beng5.
¡§Goa2 m7-sin3 goa2 long2 bo5 hoat-tou7 lah!  Goa2 tek-khak beh hou7 li2 kio3-khou2!¡¨  Thau5-ke-niu5 khoaN3-lai5 khoaN3-khi3, chhoe7-khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 thang lai5 khou2-chhou2 A-hoa a2-bo5, si7 khoaN3 i put-chi2 thai3-jian5 chu7-jiok8 bo5 kiaN-sim.  Thau5-ke-niu5 khoaN3-tioh8 chau3-kha e5 bin7-thang2 chiu7 siuN7 chit8-e5 ho2 e5 hoat-hou7.  ¡§Iam3-chian7 mih8!  Li2 chit-e5 bin7-thang2 tioh8 gia5 ti7 thau5-khak-teng2, na7 phah ka-lauh8 lai5 kong3-phoa3, li2 chiu7 kai-si2!  Hit-si5 goa2 tek-khak tiau3 li2 ti7 chhu3-teng2!¡¨  A-hoa e5 chhiu2 chiu7 sit-loh8 chu7-iu5 lah.  I eng7 siang-chhiu2 lai5 gia5 hit-e5 peng2-khap e5 bin7-thang2.
¡§Na7 ka7 goa2 phah ka-lauh8, hit-si5 li2 tioh8 si2!  Goa2 m7-sin3 goa2 long2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang tui3-hu3 li2!¡¨  Thau5-keniu5 kam2-kak i siuN7-chhut chit-e5 hoat-tou7 chin ho2, i chin boan2-chiok, chin pang3-sim khi3 cheng2-li2 i e5 thau5-mng5.  ¡§Na7 ka7 goa2 ka-lauh8 li2 tioh8 kai-si2!  Kau3 goa2 khi3 boe2 chhai3 tng2-lai5 long2 m7-thang tin2-tang7!¡¨  Thau5-ke-niu5 e5 chhui3 long2 bo5 hioh-khun3.
¡§Ti7 ke-a2 kui3-khi3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 long2 tioh8 ti3 bo7-a2, u7 lang5 ti3 oaN2 bo7-a2 ti7 thau5-khak sim, u7 lang5 ti3 bin7-thang2 bo7-a2, tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 an2-ni.  Chit-e5 bin7-thang2 bo7-a2 si7 kui3-khi3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chhut-goa7 e5 si teh ti3 e5.¡¨  A-hoa chiu7 koh tui3 niau-a2 soat-beng5 i e5 cheng5-heng5.  Thau5-ke-niu5 beh chhut-mng5 e5 si5 u7 khoaN3-tioh8 A-hoa peng3-bo5 liah8 hit-e5 cho3 kan-khou2, hoan2-tng2 eng7 bin7-thang2 ti3 ti7 thau5-khak, chit8-chhiu2 hoaN7, chit8-chhiu2 teh cho3 pa2-hi3, i chiu7 chin toa7 siu7-khi3.
¡§Goa2 m7-sin3 long2 bo5 hoat-tou7 lah!¡¨  I chiu7 ko tui3 tu5-teng2 giah8 chit8-ki hoe-kan loh8-lai5, lai5 he7 ti7 bin7-thang2-teng2.  ¡§Li2 koh tin2-tang7 khoaN3, li2 na7 ka7 goa2 phah-phoa3 chit-ki hoe-kan, li2 chiu7 bo5 mia7, goa2 tek-khak tiau3 li2 ti7 chhu3-teng2 lai5 phah hou7 li2 si2.¡¨
Chit-e5 su7 hou7 A-hoa chin kin2-tiuN, i long2 m7-kaN2 tin2-tang7, si7 chai-iaN2 chit-e5 si7 chin toa7 e5 mou7-hian2, koh i ia7 sin3 thau5-ke-niu5 tek-khak oe7 chiau3 i e5 oe7 phah si2 i, sou2-i2 chit-si5 i chiu7 oan5-choan5 sit-loh8 chu7-iu5 lah.  Thau5-ke-niu5 chai3-saN chai3-si3 pang3-tiau chiu7 so2 mng5 chhut-khi3.  I e5 sim kam2-kak chin boan2-chiok, in-ui7 taN hou7 A-hoa bo5 chu7-iu5 lah, chit-e5 pan7-hoat put-chi2 hian2-beng5.
Bo5 loa7-ku2 e5 kin2-tiuN, A-hoa e5 chhiu2 chiu7 khai-si2 khu-khu-chhoah sit-leng5, i e5 the2-liok8 ia7 put-chi2 bo5, sim7-chi3 cha2-khi2 ia7 bo5 chiah8 sim2-mih8.  A-hoa sit8-chai7 u7 kam2-kak kan-lan5.
I long2 bo5 koh kap niau-a2 cho3 sim2-mih8 sng2, i e5 sim chi2-u7 teh khoa3-lu7 kin2-sin7.  Put-ko3 i tioh8 chap8-hun e5 theng5-cheng7.  Iau2-ku2 chit8-chiong2 e5 kin2-tiuN ti7 hian7-si5 e5 A-hoa si7 put-kho2-leng5 e5 su7, i e5 chhiu2 long2 bo5 leng5-lat8 lah, i e5 sin-khu ia7 sit-loh8 chi2-lat8, i e5 thau5-nau2 ia7 chiam7-chiam7 jip8 ti7 tu3-bin5 e5 lai7-bin7, i khiok u7 kam2-kak kui2-na7-pai2 hiam2-hiam2 tioh8 ka-lauh8 hoe-kan, iau2-ku2 i e5 i3-sek chiam7-chiam7 bo5-khi3, hou7 i bo5 hoat-tou7 thang ti2-khong3.
¡§Ph-siap!!¡¨  Chit8-e5 thang-kiaN e5 siaN kio3-chheN2 A-hoa e5 it-chhe3.  I khoaN3-kiN3 hit-e5 mia7-un7 e5 hoe-kan i2-keng ti7 sit-sin5 e5 tiong-kan ka-lauh8 phoa3-chhui3 ti7 thou5-kha.
¡§Goa2 e5 hoe-kan!  A-hoa toa7 tioh8-kiaN lai5 lam2-oa2 hit-e5 phoa3-chhui3 e5 hoe-kan ti7 i e5 heng5-cheng5.  I giah8-bak8 beh chhoe7 khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 chin2-kiu3 a2-bo5, chong2-si7 i sou2 khoaN3-tioh8 e5 si7 chit8-tiau5 soh tui3 chhu3-teng2 tui7-loh8 teh tan2-hau7 A-hoa, chit-tiau5 soh si7 thau5-ke-niu5 i2-cheng5 tioh8 chun2-pi7 khi2-lai5 khng3, iau2-boe7 sit8-heng5 e5 soh.  A-hoa khoaN3-liau2 chiu7 chin toa7-kiaN, lai5 ka-leng2-sun2.  ¡§Goa2 e5 thiN-sai3 ah, pang-chan7 goa2!¡¨  Iau2-ku2 A-hoa u7 khoa3-kiN3 chit8-e5 poaN3-khui e5 thang-a2, oe7-thang to5-chau2 chhut-khi3.  A-hoa chiu7 long2 bo5 kho2-lu7 sim2-mih8, kin2-kin2 peh-chiuN7 thang-a2 lai5 thiau3 chhut goa7-bin7 khi3.

A-hoa chiu7 kin2-kin2 chau2-kau3 hit-e5 hang7-khau2 khi3, jian5-au7 chiu7 chau2-jip8 khi3 toa7-lou7, ti7 hiah-e5 koe3-lou7 e5 lang5 e5 lai7-bin7 lai5 sit-loh8 i e5 iaN2.
3 PUT-HENG7 KAP PUT-HENG7 BEH SAN-GU7
A-hoa long2 bo5 siuN7 i e5 cheng5-tou5, i chi2-u7 kiaN thau5-ke niu5 lai5 tit8-tit8 chau2.
Chhi7-lai7 e5 kau-thong tu2-tu2 si7 chin jiat8-khai e5 si5, kok-chiong2 e5 chhia bo5-lang3 tang-chau2 se-phun chhin-chhiuN7 sia7-chiN3 e5 kau-liu5, jin5-kun5 chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-chui2 ek-lai5 ek-khi3 bo5-si5 tiaN7.
Chhi7-tiong e5 tong5-hong5 khong2-toa7 chhin-chhiuN7 soaN-meh8, teng5-teng5 thah8-thah8 ui5-khun3 hou7 A-hoa chhoe7 bo5 chit8-e5 chau2-lou7 thang chau2-chhut chit e5 jin5-moa2 e5 ke-chhi7.  I soe3-soe3 e5 sin-the2 long2 bo5 kiaN sim2-mih8 gui5-hiam2 lai5 phun-jip8 ti7 hit e5 jin5-hai2 e5 lai7-bin7, u7-si5 chhia kip-chau2 kau3 i e7 bin7-cheng5 hut-jian5 tong3-tiam7, chhia-lai7 e5 lang5 tham3-thau5 chhut-lai5, toa7-me7 i.  I kam2-kak chiah e5 lang5 long2 si7 teh tui-chhe7 i, hou7 i ti7 hit lai7-bin7 long2 bo5 an-sim.
A-hoa chiu7 chhoe7 khah an-cheng7 e5 lou7 lai5 tit8-tit8 chin3-heng5.
Ti7 Tai5-pak chhi7 u7 chit8 sou2-chai7 hou7 lan2 kam2-kak khah an-cheng7 pang3-sim, chiu7-si7 Tam5-chui2 khoe-piN e5 chui2-mng5 lou7.
Kau3 hit tiong-tau3 A-hoa chiah chhut-hian7 ti7 chit8-e5 chui2-mng5 khau2.  Sio-lo7 e5 thai3-iong5, hoan2-chio3 ti7 khoe-chui2, lai5 hoat-chhut peh8-jiat8, iam7-ng5 e5 kng.  Un-loan2 kap kng-liang7 moa2-moa2 ti7 koe3-lou7 e5 lang5 e5 bin7 kap sou2 khoaN3 long2-chong2 e5 mih8 e5 teng2-bin7.
U7 chit8-kun5 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 ti7 jit8-kng e5 e7-bin7 teh pan7 ke-kou-hoe3.  Ti7 khoe-te2 u7 sai2-chun5 e5 hi5-jin5 teh chhiuN3-khek.  U7 boe7-mih8 e5 lang5 teh o, teng2-teng2.
A-hoa kiaN5 kau3 chit e5 sou2-chai7, i e5 sim chiu7 kam2-kak chin pang3-sim, khui-khoah.

I chiu7 khai-si2 lai5 koan-chhat ti7 koe3-lou7 e5 lang5.  I e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 i2-keng boe7 ki3-tit i au7-bin7 e5 su7-cheng5 lah.  Kau3 chit e5--si5, i chiu7 ti7 chhui3-lai7 teh gim5-si.  I kiaN5 kau3 pan7 ke-kou-hoe3 e5 gin2-na2 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7 khia7 ti7 hia lai5 khoaN3 in e5 thit-tho5.
Au7-lai5 u7 chit8-tin7 chau2 sio-jiok e5 ta-pou gin2-na2 tui3 i e5 sin-piN koe3, i chiu7 toe3 hia e5 ta-pou gin2-na2 khi3, lai5 kap in jip8-sin5 ti7 hit e5 thit-tho5, u7-si5 hoah, u7-si5 chiu7 phah-chhiu2.
U7 chin-choe7 sin-ki5 e5 su7 kap cheng5-keng2 moa2-moa2 ti7 chit e5 chui2-piN-lou7.  A-hoa kam2-kak ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7 u7 chu7-iu5 kap khoai3-lok8.
Hut-jian5 ti7 bin7-cheng5 bo5 hng7 e5 sou2-chai7, u7 lang5 teh oe-khim5 gim5-si e5 siaN hiang2-lai5.
Hia e5 gin2-na2 chiu7 theng5-chi2 in e5 thit-tho5 long2 chau2-khi3 khoaN3 hit e5 gim5-si e5 lang5.  A-hoa ia7 kin2-kin2 toe3 in oa2-kin7 hit e5 oe-khim5 gim5-si e5 sou2-chai7.
U7 chit8-e5 30 goa7 hoe3 e5 tiong-lian5 lang5, khia7 ti7 khoe-piN khah koan5 e5 ui7, thau5-khak kap keng-thau5 e5 tiong-kan giap chit8-ki chhiu2-the5-khim5, ian-lou7 oe, ian-lou7 teh gim5-si.
Tiong-tau3 e5 thai3-iong5 kng-chio3 ti7 hit e5 lang5 e5 thau5-khak kap choan5-sin.  Ti7 e7-bin7 e5 khoe-chui2 chin an-cheng7 teh lau5.  Hng7-hng7 ti7 khoe e5 tiong-cham7 u7 chit8-cho7 toa7-kio5, u7 chin-choe7 lang5 kap chhia ti7 hit bo5-eng5 sih-sih teh kau-ong2.
Hit e5 gim5-si e5 lang5 e5 khoan2-sit put-chi2 u7 tek8-piat, kap phou2-thong e5 lou7-piN khit-chiah8 long2 bo5 siang5.  I chheng7 chit8-su poaN3-ku7 ou-sek e5 iuN5-hok8, am7-kun2 ia7 u7 nia2-toa3, kha ia7 u7 oe5.  Tak8-hang7 long2 chin cheng2-che5, chin ho2 khoan2-sit, hou7 khoaN3 e5 lang5 oe7 kam2-kak i si7 chit8 e5 ko-siong7 bun5-nga2 e5 chhut-sin.
Sui-jian5 si7 an2-ni, i long2-chong2 e5 piau2-cheng5 toa3-tioh8 chin toa7 e5 kou-toaN kap iu5-ut.  Hit e5 soe3-siaN teh gim5-si e5 bin7 u7 choat8-bang7 kap pi-siong e5 iaN2 kau-chit ti7 lai7-bin7, hou7 khoaN3 e5 lang5 oe7 seN-chhut chit8-chiong2 tim5-tang7 put-heng7 e5 kam2-cheng5.

Chit-e5 lou7-piN teh gim5-si e5 lang5 e5 jin5-but8 kap i e5 hian7-sit8 oe7 hou7 lang5 ai3 oa2-khi3 lai5 kam2-chhat i, soah chhoe7-khoaN3 u7 sim2-mih8 thang li2-kai2 i a2-bo5.
Bo5 loa7-ku2 lan2 chiu7 hoat-kian3 i si7 chit8-e5 chhiN-mi5 lang5, hong-bat8 ti7 ou-am3 tiong e5 bong7-jin5.
Ti7 i e5 kha-cheng5 u7 chit8-teng2 peng2-phak e5 bo7-a2, ti7 hit lai7-bin7 u7 chit8 nng7 e5 gun5-kak-a2.  I2-goa7 u7 chit8-e5 phoe5-pau, iu5-goan5 ti7 kha-e7.  I bak8-chiu khoeh-khoeh, chhin-chhiuN7 teh cho3 bang7 e5 lang5 e5 piau2-cheng5 lai5 oe-khim5, gim5-si.
Tang-thiN, li2 si7 si2 e5 chhe-sai3, Li2 lai5, hou7 goa2 kou-toaN pi-chham2, Chhiu7-na5-lai7 bo5 koh u7 hoaN-hi2 e5 siaN-im, Chhau2-pou e5 hoe ia7 chhoe7 boe7-tioh8.
Tang-thiN, li2 si7 goa2 chi3-ho2 sim-iu2, Li2 lai5, piau2-beng5 choat8-keng2 khou2-cheng5, SoaN-ia2 e5 pak-hong hiu7-hiu7 hau2, Chhiu7-bak8 loh8-hioh8 leng2 chhin3-chhin3.
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 gim5-si liau2 e5 si5 u7 lang5 phah-chhiu2, ia7 u7 lang5 jim5 chiN5 lai5 hiat ti7 i e5 bo7-a2-lai7.
¡§To-sia7!¡¨  I an2-ni kong2 lai5 chhoan2 chit8-e5 toa7-khui3.
Au7-lai5 lang5 long2 si3-soaN3 liau2, chit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 lang5 chiah khut-sin lai5 khioh i e5 chiN5.
Chi2-u7 A-hoa long2 bo5 li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7, lai5 chu3-sin5 khoaN3 chit e5 put-heng7 e5 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 heng5-tong7.  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 khia7 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, A-hoa u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8-e5 gun5-kak-a2 ti7 thou5-kha, chiu7 kin2-kin2 khioh hou7 chhiN-mi5 lang5.
¡§A-peh, chiah iau2 koh chit8-e5--, li2 khioh bo5-tioh8!¡¨
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, chin to-sia7!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 chhun-chhiu2, phaiN2-se3 
phaiN2-se3 lai5 chih hit e5 chiN5.  ¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, li2 na7 koh khoaN3-tioh8 pat8-e5 gun5-kak-a2, li2 thang te7 ti7 li2 e5 lak-te7-a2!¡¨  I kin2-kin2 tui3 A-hoa an2-ni hoan-hu3.
¡§M7-thang, an2-ne choe3 thiN-teng2 e5 Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, in bo5 hoaN-hi2 lang5 u7 chit-chiong2 am3-sam3, bo5 kng-beng5 e5 sim.¡¨
A-hoa chin jin7-chin e5 bin7 lai5 tui3 chhiN-mi5 lang5 an2-ni in3.
Chit ku3 oe7 u7 phah-tioh8 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 sim.
¡§Chit e5 gin2-na2 si7 sim2-mih8 lang5?¡¨  I e5 sim am2-ni siuN7.  Chong2-si7 mng7 i, 
¡§Li2 si7 Ki-tok-tou5 mah?¡¨
¡§Goa2 m7-chai!  Goa2 kan-taN chai-iaN2 Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 ti7 thiN-nih8, in-ui7 A-long5 e5 a-ma2 an2-ni kong2!¡¨
¡§Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 ti7 thiN-nih8!?¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 koh chit8-pai2 ti7 i e5 chhui3-lai7 lai5 liam7 hiah e5 oe7.  Cha-bou2 gin2-na2 kong2 chhut-lai5 e5 oe7, chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 tu2-tu2 teh chhoe7, teh tham3-mng7 e5__ khiok chhoe7 boe7-tioh8, ti7 hit e5 choat8-bang7 tiong hut-jian5 tu2-tioh8 chit8 e5 khe2-si7 chit8-poaN.  I u7 i3-su3 ai3 beh tui3 gin2-na2 tham3-mng7 tam7-poh8 oe7, khiok siuN7 boe7-chhut u7 sim2-mih8 thang mng7 i, koh ia7 phah-sng3 chit e5 gin2-na2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang tui3 i cho3 sim2-mih8.  I chiu7 beh li7-khui chit e5 sou2-chai7.
¡§Gin2-na2 chai3-hoe7!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 chiong i e5 khim5 ngeh8 ti7 hiap8-e7, ti3 i e5 bo7-a2, theh8 i e5 phoe5-pau, chiu7 kiaN5-khui khi3.  I ban7-ban7-na2 lai5 kiaN5 tui3 hit e5 an-cheng7 e5 chhiu7-kha khi3.  A-hoa tiam7-tiam7 khia7 ti7 hia lai5 khoaN3 hit e5 lang5 e5 au7-bin7.  I e5 sim hut-jian5 kam2-kak chin kou-toaN, in-ui7 i chhin-chhiuN7 sit-loh8 chit8-e5 chhin-bit8 e5 lang5 chit8-iuN7.
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 kiaN5 kau3 chit8-chang5 chhiu7-kha chiu7 theng5-tiam7, lai5 che7 ti7 hit e5 khoe-piN e5 chhau2-teng2, thng3 i e5 bo7-a2, tui3 i e5 phoe5-pau-a2 lai7 teh theh8 mih8.
A-hoa khoaN3-tioh8 chit e5 su7, sim-lai7 koh hok8-to3 hoaN-hi2.  I sui5-si5 kiaN5 kau3 hit e5 chhiu7-kha, lai5 che7 ti7 chhiu7-thau5 lai5 khoaN3 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 sou2-choe3.
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 u7 thng3 i e5 goa7-saN khi2-lai5, jian5-au7 chiu7 tui3 i e5 pau-lai7 theh8 i e5 piaN2, si7 i e5 tiong-sit8 khi2-lai5 chiah8.  I e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 teh siuN7 sim2-mih8 e5 khoan2, chhim-chhim tim5-bek8 lai5 chiah8 i e5 piaN2.
A-hoa khoaN3-kiN3 hit e5 cheng5-heng5 soah kam2-kak tioh8 i chin iau, koh ia7 siuN7-tioh8 i e5 su7-cheng5 soah siong-sim lai5 lau5 bak8-sai2, i chiu7 soe3-siaN ti7 chhui3-lai7 teh hau2.  A-hoa na2 hau2 na2 pi-chham2, i e5 siaN-im kau3-boe2 u7 kio3-chhiN2 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 sim.
¡§Sim2-mih8 lang5 teh hau2???¡¨  I oat8-thau5 lai5 mng7 i.  A-hoa kin2-kin2 tiam7-khi3.
¡§Li2 si7 tu2-chiah hit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 tioh8 m7?¡¨
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 bo5 in3-tap chiu7 koh an2-ni mng7.  A-hoa long2 bo5 in3 i, chong2-si7 hut-jian5 siuN7-tioh8 khou2-keng2 lai5 toa7-siaN hau2 chhut-lai5.
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, li2 siaN2-su7 teh hau2?¡¨
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 tiong-chi2 i e5 tiong-sit8, eng7 chhiu2 lai5 beh bong A-hoa, in-ui7 i beng5-pek8 si7 tu2-chiah hit e5 gin2-na2.  ¡§Goa2 pak-tou2 chin iau!  Goa2 tui3 cha2-khi2 long2 bo5 chiah8 sim2-mih8!¡¨  A-hoa chiu7 koh tiam7-tiam7 eng7 beng5-liau5 e5 siaN lai5 kong2.
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 koh chit8-pai2 thiaN-tioh8 leng7-goa7 chit8-e5 ki5-koai3 e5 oe7, i m7-chai beh an2-choaN2, chiu7 kin2-kin2 chiong i chhiu2 theh8 e5 piaN2 chhun-chhut beh hou7 A-hoa chiah8.
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, goa2 chit te3 piaN2 hou7 li2 chiah8!  Ah, chit-te3 goa2 u7 chiah8-tioh8, 
goa2 koh theh8 pat8-te3 e5 hou7 li2 chiah8!¡¨  I an2-ni kong2 chiu7 sui5-si5 tui3 pau-lai7 theh8-chhut chit8-te3 piaN2 hou7 A-hoa.  A-hoa khoaN3 i e5 bin7, koh khoaN3 hit-te3 piaN2, chiu7 chih piaN2 khi2-lai5.
¡§A-peh, to-sia7!¡¨  I chiu7 khai-si2 chiah8.  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 chin hoaN-hi2, eng7 i e5 chhiu2 bong A-hoa e5 thau5-khak, ¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, lin2 tau ti7 to2-ui7, li2 chiah bo5 tng2-khi3 chiah8-png7?¡¨
¡§Goa2 m7-chai goan2 tau, thau5-ke niu5 beh ka7 goa2 tiau3 ti7 chhu3-teng2, sou2-i2 goa2 kin2-kin2 chau2 chhut-lai5, in-ui7 goa2 cha2-khi2 kong3-phoa3 hoe-kan, hoe-kan si7 thau5-ke niu5 po2-poe3 e5 mih8-kiaN7.¡¨
A-hoa chin sek8-sai7 e5 khoan2 lai5 chiah8 chit8-chhui3, kong2 chit8-chhui3, i e5 bak8-chiu ia7 chin kng-beng5 lah.
Chiah e5 oe7 hou7 chhiN-mi5 lang5 tam7-poh8 gong5-ngiah8, ¡§Chit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 u7 sim2-mih8 put-heng7 e5 su7?¡¨  I ti7 sim-lai7 ki5-koai3.
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-a2, li2 e5 mia5 kio3-choe3 sim2-mih8?¡¨
¡§Goa2 m7-chai, i2-cheng5 lang5 kio3 goa2 A-hoa, thau5-ke niu5 long2 kio3 goa2 si2-kui2, chhu3-piN e5 a-po5 kio3 goa2 a-soaN gin2-na2, ia7 u7 lang5 kio3 goa2 bo5-chhu3 niau.  Li7-li7 ia7 si7 kio3 choe3 bo5-chhu3 niau, i ka-ki7 lai5 jip8 thau5-ke niu5 e5 chhu3, si7 chin chok-giat8 e5 sio2-niau, i ia7 si7 goa2 e5 peng5-iu2.¡¨
A-hoa e5 bin7 i2-keng chin hoaN-hi2, i long2 boe7 ki3-tit i e5 su7 lah. ¡§Bo5-chhu3 niau!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 kam2-kak chit e5 gin2-na2 kap i sou2 kong2 e5 oe7, long2 chin chhut-ki5 sin5-pi3, chin thau3-thiat i e5 sim-su.  I chiu7 koh theh8 chit8-te3 piaN2 hou7 A-hoa, i pun2-sin ia7 ke3-siok8 chiah8.  A-hoa ti7 chiah8 piaN2 e5 tiong-kan ia7 chu3-sin5 teh khoaN3 hit e5 chhiN-mi5 lang5.
¡§A-peh, li2 bak8-chiu bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 chin kan-khou2 bo5?!¡¨  A-hoa pe5-oa2 lai5 khut ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, tit8-tit8 khoaN3 hit e5 koh-iuN7 e5 bak8-chiu.  Khiok A-peh chi2-u7 ng3 i bi5-chhio3 chit8-e5, long2 bo5 in3-tap sim2-mih8.

¡§A-peh, li2 e5 bak8-chiu sim2-mih8 si5 chiah oe7 khoaN3-kiN3?  In-ui7 chin-choe7 ho2-khoaN3 e5 kong-keng2, a2-si7 sui2 e5 mih8 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 si7 chin kho2-lin5 e5 su7, kiaN5-lou7 e5 si5, a2-si7 chiah8-png7 e5 si5 kiam2 m7-si7 chin kan-khou2!  A-peh ah, li2 si7 chin kho2-lin5 e5 lang5!¡¨
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 giah8 i e5 keng-thau5, bo5 koh chiah8 i e5 piaN2 lah.
¡§Chong2-si7 phah-sng3 oe7 koh khoaN3-kiN3 chiah-tioh8!  Lan2 na7 kau3 thian-tong5 khi3 e5 si5-chun7, Ia5-sou oe7 hou7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu oe7 khoaN3-kiN3, in-ui7 ti7 hit u7 chin-choe7 sui2 e5 kong-keng2, chin-choe7 hoaN-hi2, khoai3-lok8 e5 su7, na7 si7 bak8-chiu bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 chiu7 long2 bo5 sim-sek.¡¨
A-hoa kui7 ti7 A-peh e5 bin7-cheng5, eng7 chhiu2 lai5 pi2 thiN-teng2, A-peh khiok aN3-thau5 lai5 thiaN i e5 oe7.
¡§Ne2, A-peh ah, li2 kiam2 u7 sin3 Ia5-sou?  Lan2 na7 sin3 Ia5-sou chiu7 e7-thang kau3 thian-tong5 khi3, ti7 hia tak8-jit8 long2 u7 thiN-sai3 teh gim5-si o-lo2, hit e5 si7 chin khoai3-lok8 e5 sou2-chai7.  Am3-si5 lan2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chin-choe7 kng-chheN, in-ui7 chheN si7 thiN-sai3 e5 bak8-chiu, long2 teh khoaN3 lan2.¡¨
¡§Liap8-sat-lou7 ia7 si7 kho2-lin5 e5 lang5, in-ui7 long2 bo5 chhu3, bo5 lang5 thang khoaN3-kou3 i, chin kou-toaN.  I e5 sin-khu u7 siN tok8-liu5, hit e5 si7 chin thang3-thiaN3 e5 su7, khiok Liap8-sat-lou7 tak8-jit8 kiah8-bak8 ng3-thiN, sou2-i2 si2-liau2 u7 chin-choe7 chheng7 peh8-saN e5 thiN-sai3 lai5 chhoa7 i chiuN7 thiN-teng2 khi3.  Kau3 ti7 lau7-pe7 A-pek-liap8-han2 e5 heng-cheng5 khi3,ti7 hia Liap8-sat-lou7 bo5 koh siu7-khou2, bo5 iau-go7, bo5 kou-toaN, bo5 lau5 bak8-sai2, bo5 thang3-thiaN3, in-ui7 lau7-pe7 A-pek-liap8-han2 e5 heng-cheng5 u7 moa2-moa2 e5 an-ui3 kap hoaN-hi2.¡¨
¡§A-peh, li2 e5 bak8-chiu ti7 hia tek-khak oe7 khoaN3-kiN3, chhin-chhiuN7 Liap8-sat-lou7 chit8-iuN7.¡¨
¡§Liap8-sat-lou7 si7 toa7-lang5, chong2-si7 i ia7 hou7 lau7-pe7 pho7, hit e5 m7-si7 kan-taN gin2-na2 e5 su7, in-ui7 toa7-lang5 ia7 su-iau3 lau7-pe7 e5 thiaN3, hit e5 an-ui3 e5 sim-hoai5 tiong.¡¨
A-hoa kong2 kau3 chia chiu7 eng7 siang-chhiu2 lai5 lam2-oa2 i e5 sim.

Chong2-si7 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 bin7 na2-thiaN na2-kat, kau3-boe2 soa3 tong3 boe7-tiau5 chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5.
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, li2 tioh8 kin2-kin2 tng2-khi3 li2 lai5 e5 sou2-chai7!¡¨  I an2-ni kong2 chiu7 giah8 i e5 khim5, theh8 i e5 mih8-kiaN7 lai5 kin2-kin2 kiaN5-li7 hit e5 sou2-chai7. ¡§Hit e5 m7-si7 kan-taN gin2-na2 e5 su7, toa7-lang5 ia7 su-iau3 hit e5 an-ui3 e5 sim-hoai5 tiong.¡¨  A-hoa e5 oe7 iau2-ku2 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 teh chau2-seh8.
A-hoa iau2 kui7 ti7 hia, chin sit-bang7 teh khoaN3 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 au7-bin7.  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 chiam7-chiam7 li7-hng7 khi3 lah.  Siong-pi e5 ou-hun5 hut-jian5 ta3-oa2 ti7 A-hoa e5 sim, i e5 bak8-chiu u7 bak8-sai2 e5 iaN2 chhut-hian7.
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 tui3 toa7-kio5 tit8-tit8 kiaN5-khi3.  U7 chin-choe7 ong2-lai5 e5 lang5 chiong i e5 cheng5-iaN2 thun-biat8 khi3.  A-hoa kin2-kin2 khia7 khi2-lai5, ti7 chhiu7-piN lai5 beh chhoe7 hit e5 sit-loh8 e5 lang5 e5 iaN2, i e5 bak8-sai2 tui7-loh8 i e5 chhui3-phoe2.  A-hoa e5 sim chin tioh8-kip, chhin-chhiuN7 eng2-oan2 beh sit-loh8 chit e5 choe3 chhin-bit8 e5 peng5-iu2 chit8-iuN7.  I ke3-siok8 ti7 jin5-kun5 e5 lai7-bin7 lai5 chhoe7 A-peh e5 iaN2.
A-hoa hut-jian5 ti7 toa7-kio5 teng2 khoaN3 tioh8 A-peh teh kiaN5 e5 iaN2.  I e5 sim sui5-si5 hoaN-hi2 khi2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 hit e5 iaN2 iau2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 e5 si5 iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 ng3-bang7 ti7 in 2 lang5 e5 tiong-kan chit8-iuN7.  A-hoa chin chu3-sin5 teh khoaN3 i, kiaN-liau2 koh sit-loh8 i iaN2.  A-hoa hut-jian5 khoaN3-tioh8 chhiN-mi5 lang5 kiaN5 kau3 kio5 e5 tiong-cham7, chiu7 theng5-kha, lai5 oa2 ti7 kio5-lan5, bin7 ng3 ti7 chui2-lai7, i chiu7 toa7 hoaN-hi2 koaN2-kin2 lai5 chau2-khi3 beh chhoe7 i.
¡§A-peh ah, A-peh ah!¡¨  I chiu7 chau2 kau3 jin5-kun5 e5 lai7-bin7, oe-kheh cheng3-lang5 lai5 tah8-jip8 toa7-kio5 teng2, tit8-tit8 chau2 kau3 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 sou2-chai7.  ¡§A-peh ah, A-peh ah!¡¨  A-hoa chau2-oa2 khi3, chiu7 liah8 i e5 chhiu2.  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 tioh8-kiaN oat8-thau5 lai5 beh chai si7 sim2-mih8 lang5.
¡§A-peh ah, goa2 siuN7 goa2 oe7 chhoe7 li2 bo5, hou7 goa2 e5 sim chin kan-khou2 kau3 lau5 bak8-sai2, chong2-si7 kai-chai3 goa2 u7 chhoe7-tioh8 li2, goa2 chin hoaN-hi2!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 sui-jian5 beng5-pek8 si7 hit e5 sin5-pi3 e5 lu2-long5, iau2-ku2 i chin tioh8-kiaN.

¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-a2, li2 u7 sim2-mih8 su7?!  Li2 m7-thang lai5, chia chin gui5-hiam2!¡¨
¡§A-peh, li2 sim2-mih8 si5 beh koh lai5?  Goa2 beh tiam3 chia tan2-hau7 li2!  A-hoa khiN5-oa2 A-peh e5 chhiu2 lai5 eng7 pek-chhiat e5 sim mng7 i.
Chit-ku3 oe7 hou7 chhiN-mi5 lang5 kam2-kak chin kan-lan5.
¡§Chit e5 gin2-na2 u7 sim2-mih8 put-heng7!  Kiam2 u7 pat8-lang5 ko2-jian5 kap goa2 siang7-khoan2 bo5 i-oa2 mah?!¡¨  I ti7 sim-lai7 an2-ni siuN7.
¡§Goa2 tioh8 bin5-na2 cha2-khi2 chiah oe7 koh lai5, li2 tioh8 tng2-khi3!¡¨  I pak-khui gin2-na2 e5 chhiu2 lai5 beh li7-khui khi3.
¡§A-peh ah, goa2 beh tiam3 chia tan2-hau7 li2, li2 tioh8 u7-iaN2 koh lai5 haN5!¡¨  A-hoa e5 siaN-im chin pi-chhiat.
¡§Li2 tioh8 kin2-kin2 tng2-khi3!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 i2-keng koh ke3-siok8 chin3-cheng5 kiaN5-khi3.  I e5 sim chin kan-khou2, ¡§Che si7 sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3, i si7 beh lian5-lui7 goa2 mah, goa2 kiam2 u7 hoat-tou7 thang ka7 i cho3 sim2-mih8, goa2 ka-ki7 e5 su7-cheng5 kiam2 bo5 i2-keng chiam3-moa2 goa2 e5 it-chhe3 mah!¡¨  Chiah e5 su-siuN2 kau-chit ti7 i e5 sim-lai7, hou7 i chin lan5-koe3.
¡§A-peh ah, li2 tioh8 u7-iaN2 koh lai5 neh!¡¨
Tui3 hng7 e5 au7-bin7, ti7 choe7-choe7 chap8-im e5 lai7-bin7 i koh thiaN-kiN3 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 e5 siaN.  I kin2-kin2 tong3 tiam7 i e5 kha-pou7.  ¡§Hit e5 siaN si7 choat8-bang7, pi-chham2 tiong teh chhoe7 bo5 lou7 e5 siaN, hit e5 siaN kiam2 m7-si7 i chhin-sin sou2 the2-giam7 tioh8 khou2-chham2 e5 siaN mah!¡¨  Chong2-si7 goa2 oe7-thang ui7-tioh8 i cho3 
sim2-mih8, goa2 kiam2 m7-si7 ka-ki7 ti7 hit tiong-kan teh beh tim5-lek8 e5 lang5 mah!¡¨
¡§A-peh ah, A-peh ah, li2 tioh8 u7-iaN2 koh lai5 haN5!¡¨  A-hoa i2-keng koh chau2-oa2 lai5 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 lah.
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, goa2 chhoa7 li2 tng2-khi3 li2 e5 chhu3!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 khan A-hoa e5 chhiu2 khi2-lai5, A-hoa e5 hoaN-hi2 sui5-si5 koh hok8-to3.
¡§A-peh ah, li2 kiam2 chai goa2 e5 chhu3, goa2 m7-chai goa2 e5 chhu3 si7 ti7 to2-ui7?!¡¨
Iau2-ku2 chhiN-mi5 lang5 khan A-hoa e5 chhiu2, oat8 tng2-sin kiaN5 to3-tng2 e5 lou7.
¡§A-peh ah, goa2 chin hoaN-hi2!  Neh, A-peh, lin2 e5 chhu3 si7 ti7 to2-ui7?¡¨  A-hoa khiN5 ti7 i e5 saN lai5 mng7 i.  I kam2-kak chin pang3-sim, chin hoaN-hi2.
¡§Goa2 ia7 m7-chai goa2 e5 chhu3!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 chin pi-siong an2-ni in3 A-hoa.
¡§A-peh, Li7-li7 ia7 si7 m7-chai i e5 chhu3, i ka-ki7 chau2 lai5 thau5-ke niu5 e5 chhu3, i si7 bo5 lang5 ai3 e5 niau-a2.  Goa2 ia7 m7-si7 thau5-ke niu5 e5-, si7 tui3 A-long5 in keh-piah, ma-ma e5 chhu3 chhoa7 lai5 e5-.  Ma-ma tui3 chin hng7 e5 sou2-chai7 che7 chun5 chhoa7 goa2 lai5, koh khah i2-cheng5 e5 su7 goa2 long2 m7-chai-iaN2, in-ui7 hit e5 si5 goa2 si7 chin soe3-han3 e5 eN-a2.¡¨
¡§Li7-li7 ia7 si7 goa2 e5 eN-a2, i chin thian-thoh8 tak8-jit8 long2 teh choe3-sng2, u7-si5 tioh8 thiau3-bu2, u7-si5 tioh8 gim5-si.  Chong2-si7 thau5-ke niu5 na7 tng2-lai5 goa2 chiu7 bo5 thiau3-bu2, bo5 gim5-si, in-ui7 thau5-ke niu5 bo5 ai3 goa2 an2-ni choe3.  I ai3 goan2 choe3 kang, goan2 tak8-jit8 long2 tioh8 hou7 i phah.  I ia7 eng7 soh tiau3 ti7 chhu3-teng2 beh tiau3-si2 goan2.¡¨  A-hoa e5 bin7 kong2 kau3 chia chiu7 bo5 khoai3-lok8, chong2-si7 sui5-si5 koh pian3 chin hoaN-hi2.

¡§A-peh ah, li2 khoaN3 e7-bin7 e5 khoe-te2 u7 chin-choe7 chun5-a2 ti7 hia!¡¨  In nng7-lang5 chiu7 theng5-oa2 khi3 kio5-hoaN7.  Ti7 hit e5 chheng7-cheng7 e5 khoe-chui2 teng2 u7 saN si3 chiah phang5-chun5 teh kiaN5.
U7 hai2-hong chhoe ti7 in nng7-lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7.  Jit8-thau5 i2-keng beh loh8 hai2 lah.  ThiN-khi3 ia7 chin leng2.  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 tiam7-tiam7 khia7-oa2 ti7 kio5-lan5, i boe7-thang khoaN3-tioh8 sim2-mih8, chi2-u7 khia7 tit8-tit8, bin7 ng3 ti7 khoe-te2.  Khiok ti7 i e5 sim, i khai-si2 teh beng5-pek8 A-hoa e5 jin5-but8.  Ti7 A-hoa sou2 piau2-hian7 thian-chin, beng5-long2 e5 oe7-gu2, hou7 i ti7 gin2-a2 e5 lai7-bin7 hoat-hian7 tioh8 chit8-e5 chin-toa7 koh bi2-biau7 e5 se3-kai3.  In saN-kap khia7 ti7 kio5-teng2 lai5 hiong2-siu7 sin-sian2 e5 hai2-hong.  A-hoa ke3-siok8 teh kong2-oe7.  Ti7 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7 u7 siN-chhut chit8-chiong2 e5 boan2-chiok.  Chit e5 boan2-chiok chhin-chhiuN7 tui3 ti7 chit8 e5 pat8-e5 se3-kai3 sou2 pun hou7 chit8 e5 leng7-goa7 e5 se3-kai3 e5 boan2-chiok chit8-iuN7.  Chit e5 leng7-goa7 e5 se3-kai3 si7 ho5-teng2 e5 ou-am3, ho5-teng2 e5 choat8-bang7, chong2-si7 iau2 hit e5 si7 chit8 e5 thian-chin, oah8-phoat, kng-beng5 e5 se3-kai3, sui-jian5 piN5-piN5 u7 put-heng7, gek8-keng2 e5 pak-hong chhiong-heng5 ti7 hit teng2-bin7.
Chiong2-chiong2 e5 hoe5-kou3 kap su-siong2, chiaN5-cho3 chit8-phiN chap8-loan7 e5 chhiN-hun5 lai5 am-bat8 i hoan5-chap8 e5 thau5-nau2.  I chiu7 kam2-kak gong5-ngiah8, seh8-sin5, sou2-i2 kin2-kin2 lai5 beh thong2-it i e5 sim.
A-hoa e5 sim chin peng5-an, khoai3-lok8.  Chiah e5 kong-keng2 hou7 i e5 sim chin khui-khoah, i chiu7 ti7 chhui3-lai7 khai-si2 gim5-si.
¡§Kho2-lin5 bo5 chhu3 e5 sio2-niau, Li2 tui3 to2-ui7 chit8-e5 kok lai5, ChhiN-sin5 e5 teng2-bin7, chhai2-kheng7 e5 boe2-liu, Hng7-hng7 poaN5-koe3 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu.
Li2 e5 siang-kha tah8 ti7 ou-am3 e5 tin5-se3, Li2 e5 sim khiok bang7-siong2 bo5-soah, Sun5-chin si7 li2 e5 mia5, Chin-sit8 si7 li2 un2-bat8 e5 sit8-giau2.¡¨
A-hoa e5 siaN-im chin hiang2-liang7 khi2-lai5, lai5 pou3-moa2 ti7 hit e5 chheng-liang5 chui2-teng2 e5 khong-khi3, hou7 thiaN e5 lang5 ke-thiN chit8-chiong2 e5 thiam-cheng7.  A-hoa kap i sou2 piau2-hian7 chhut-lai5 long2-chong2 sin5-pi3 e5 ku2-tong7 i2-keng kau3-giah8 
tin2-tang7 chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 choan sim-sin5.  I eng7 i e5 chhiu2 lai5 gim7 A-hoa soe3-soe3 e5 chhiu2.
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, li2 chin gau5 gim5-si!¡¨
A-hoa e5 sim chin boan2-chiok, chiu7 kheh-oa2 ti7 i e5 sin-khu.
¡§Chit e5 si7 A-gi7 e5 ma-ma e5 io5-na5-si, ia7 si7 goa2 e5 io5-na5-si!¡¨
¡§Li2 chin gau5 gim5!¡¨  ChhiN-mi5 lang5 chin kam2-kek lai5 tit8-tit8 o-lo2 i.
¡§Sin5-pi3 e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2, i hou7 goa2 e5 sim toa7 ki5-koai3, i e5 chhut-hian7 si7 m7-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3!?¡¨  I ti7 sim-lai7 an2-ni siuN7, iau2-ku2 chhui3-lai7 chi2-u7 kong2 ¡§Li2 chin gau5 gim5-si!¡¨
ChhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 chhiu2 tang7-tang7 gim7-oa2 A-hoa e5 chhiu2.  A-hoa e5 huih, chit8-meh8 chit8-meh8 e5 kou2-tong7, chhin-chhiuN7 chiaN5-cho3 chin sin5-pi3 e5 lek8-liong7 lai5 thau3-jip8 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7, hou7 i na2 kam2-kak A-hoa e5 seN3-mia7 kap i e5 seN3-mia7 u7 chit8-chiong2 sin5-pi3 e5 lian5-lok8.
2 goeh8 e5 sek8-iong5 chiam7-chiam7 sit-loh8 i e5 kng-lat8, hian2-chhut chhiah-ang5 e5 iN5-hun5, koa3 ti7 hai2-teng2 e5 khong-tiong, lai5 hoan2-chio3 chu-ang5 e5 chhai2-sek ti7 hit e5 khoe-chui2 e5 teng2-bin7, kap ti7 in 2 lang5 saN khia7-oa2 e5 cheng5-iaN2 e5 teng2-bin7.
Tang-hong ti7 hit e5 kio5-e7 kap kio5-teng2 teh hiu7-hiu7 hau2, chhin-chhiuN7 siong-pi, ia7 chhin-chhiuN7 hoaN-hi2 chit8-iuN7.
4 BONG5-BOK8 GAK8-JIN5 E5 SIN-SE3
Chit e5 lou7-piN teh gim5-si kiu5-khit e5 chhiN-mi5 lang5 si7 sim2-mih8 lang5, taN lan2 tioh8 chiam7-si5 to2-tng2 khi3 khoaN3 i e5 su7-cheng5 kap keng-koe3.
Kin7 40 goa7-ni5 i2-cheng5 e5 su7, ti7 Tai5-lam5 e5 ¡Ñ ¡Ñ ke e5 tiong-cham7 u7 chit8-cho7 hoa5-bi2 e5 toa7 iuN5-lau5, chha-put-to si7 tong-si5 choe3 tong5-hong5 e5 kian3-tiok8.
Hit-e5 iuN5-lau5 e5 chu2-lang5 kio3-cho3 Chhoa3 Peng2-bun5, lang5 phou2-thong kio3 i Peng2-bun5-a2-sia3, si7 chit8-ui7 kek8-ki5 pu3-u7 e5 giap8-chu2.
I e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 u7 seN nng7 e5 hau7-siN kap chit8-e5 cha-bou2 kiaN2.
U7 chit8-pai2 te7 ji7-kiaN2 ti7 Jit8-pun2 teh thak8 tai7-hak8 e5 si5 soa3 tu2-tioh8 toa7-piN7.  Lau7-bu2, Chhoa3 hu7-jin5 chiap-tioh8 siau-sit chiu7 chhong2-chhong2 pong5-pong5 ta3-chun5 koe3 Jit8-pun2 khi3 khoaN3 i e5 kiaN2.
Ti7 hu7-jin5 lang5 chhut-goa7 chia5-ni5 e5 si5, chit e5 hong-liu5 e5 chu2-lang5 soa3 kap chit8-e5 chhu3-lai7 e5 lu2-pi7 hoat-seng koan-he7.
Pi-kek8 tui3 chia khai-si2.  Kau3 ti7 hu7-jin5 lang5 thiaN-kiN3 chit e5 su7-cheng5 tui3 Jit8-pun2 piaN3 tng2-lai5 e5 si5, chit-e5 lu2-pi7 i2-keng seN chit8-e5 ta7-pou eN-a2 lah.
Keng-koe3 geh8-goa7 jit8 au7, kho2-lin5 e5 bu2-kiaN2 chiu7 siu7 koaN2-chhut chit e5 oan3-than3 e5 toa7-lau5.
Lau7-bu2 lau5 bak8-sai2 pho7 i e5 eN-a2 khi3 oa2-kho3 toa3 ti7 soaN-lai7 chhang5-chng e5 a-hiaN.
Chit e5 soaN-lai7 e5 chhan5-chng chi2-u7 si7 pah goa7-hou7 chip8-hap8 khia7-khi2 e5 chit8-e5 sio2 pou7-lok8.
Khiok ti7 chia u7 chu7-jian5-kai3 sou2 oe7-thang hou7 lang5 long2-chong2 e5 bi2-sek kap khoai3-lok8 moa2-moa2, thang khoaN3-kiN3 se3-goa7 tho5-hng5 e5 peng5-an ti7 hia.  Ti7 chit e5 chng-sia7 e5 teng2-bin7, soaN-kha u7 chit8-keng Thian-chu2 kau3-tng5, toa7-pou7-hun7 e5 peh-seN3 na7 kau3 le2-pai3 jit8 chiu7 hioh-khun3 long2-chong2 e5 kang-chok, kau3 le2-pai3-tng5 khi3 choe3 le2-pai3, siu2 mi7-sat.

Chit e5 siu7-khou2 e5 lau7-bu2 khoaN3 chit e5 sou2-chai7 si7 choe3 thang hou7 in bu2-kiaN2 tit-tioh8 siam2-pi7 se3-jin5 e5 ki-chhi3 kap pai5-thek e5 toe7.  Bo5 gi5-gou7 in bu2-kiaN2 chit8-e5 tah8 jip8 chit e5 toe7, choan5-chng e5 peh-seN3 long2 saN-kap gi7-lun7.  ¡§In si7 sim2-mih8 lang5?¡¨  Chit e5 gi7-lun7 bo5-ku2 chiu7 seN-chhut kiat-lun7.
¡§U7 chit8-e5 hoan7-choe7 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5, pho7 i hoan7-choe7 e5 kiaN2 jip8 lai5 chit e5 chng-sia7!!¡¨  Chit e5 siau-sit u7 tin2-tang7 choan5-chng.  Su7-sit8 chit-khoan2 e5 su7 ti7 chit e5 chng-sia7 si7 chit8-e5 thang-kiaN thang-ui3 e5 tai7-chi3.
Ti7 khe-chui2 piN soe2-saN e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 chiong chit e5 kiaN-lang5 e5 toa7-su7 lai5 cho3 in e5 oe7-peN3, saN-kap kong2 lai5 chhio3.
Lau7 hu7-jin5 lang5 khoaN3-tioh8 chit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 lau7-bu2 tui3 in e5 sin-piN koe3-khi3, chiu7 phui3-noa7, giah8 keng-thau5, oe7 sip8-ji7 ti7 heng-cheng5 lai5 piau2-si7 iam3-ouN3.
¡§U3-oe3 mih8!¡¨  In e5 chhui3-lai7 an2-ni liam7, in bu2-kiaN2 chiaN5-choe3 choan5-chng e5 thah-gai7.  ¡§Chit e5 choe7-ok e5 kiaN2 tioh8 hiat-kak, m7-thang chhi7 chit e5, tek-khak oe7 in2 chai-lan7!¡¨
A-hiaN e5 ka-teng5 long2 bo5 hoaN-hi2 in ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7, siong5-siong5 eng7 oe7 lai5 kong-kek ki-chhi3 in.  Koh ia7 kiaN-liau2 u7 sim2-mih8 lian5-lui7.  Chit e5 kong-kek kap ki-chhi3 long2 bo5 leng2-cheng7, na2 ku2 na2 li7-hai7.
EN-a2 ti7 chit e5 khoan5-keng2 e5 lai7-bin7 chiam7-chiam7 toa7-han3 lah.  Lau7-bu2 chiu7 ka7 i ho7 mia5 choe3 Pek-jim2, chiu7-si7 pah-poaN e5 jim2-siu7.
Bu2-kiaN2 ham7-loh8 ti7 chin-toa7-e5 khun3-lan5.  Khiok ia7 kam2-kak long2 bo5 pat8 tiau5 lou7, chiu7 aiN7 chit e5 kho2-lin5 siu7 iam3-ouN3 e5 kiaN2 khioh chhiu7-hioh8 a2-si7 kut8 chhau2-thau5 chhut-lai5 boe7, lai5 i5-chhi5 in e5 seng-oah8.
U7-si5 lau7-bu2 siuN7-tioh8 bu2-kiaN2 e5 keng2-gu7 kap ou-am3 e5 chian5-tou5 lai5 che7 ti7 chhiu7-kha hau2.  Pek-jim2 kau3 ti7 chin toa7-han3 oe7-hiau2 in3-siong7 tioh8 khou2-mia7 lau7-bu2 e5 bak8-sai2 tih ti7 i chiah8-ni e5 bin7.
Ti7 chit e5 chham2-keng2 koe3 liau2 10 goa7-ni5, Pek-jim2 i2-keng kap pat8-e5 gin2-na2 jip8 ti7 soaN-e7 e5 sio2-oh8 teh thak8-chheh lah!
Chong2-si7 Pek-jim2 khai-si2 hoat-hian7 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7 u7 chin-toa7 e5 put-heng7 kap kou-toaN.
¡§Bo5-pe7 kiaN2 m7-si7 lang5!Pek-jim2 kho2-ou3 thang5!¡¨
Tong5-hak8 cho3 koa-khek lai5 ki-chhi3 pai5-thek i.  Lang5 na7 khoaN3-tioh8 i chiu7 chau2-siam2 khi3, ia7 bo5 lang5 beh kap i tang5-toh.
¡§Ma-ma, lang5 si7 an2-choaN2 kio3 goa2 bo5-pe7-kiaN2, kio2 goa2 kho2-ou3 thang5 ne3?!¡¨  Pek-jim2 khai-si2 chiong i e5 khou2-su7 lai5 chit-mng7 i e5 lau7-bu2.
¡§Pek-jim2, chhiaN2 li2 m7-thang mng7 goa2 sim2-mih8!  Long2 si7 ma-ma e5 choe7, chhiaN2 li2 tioh8 sia3-bian2 goa2, long2 si7 goa2 m7-tioh8!¡¨  Lau7-bu2 lam2-oa2 kiaN2-ji5 lai5 toa7-hau2.
Chong2-si7 kau3 Pek-jim2 pit-giap bo5-ku2, chit e5 siu7-khou2 e5 lau7-bu2 chiu7 tai3-piN7 soah koe3-sin.  Pek-jim2 chu7-jian5 kui-siok8 i e5 a-ku7, lai5 pang-chan7 chhan5-hng5 i2-kip long2-chong2 khun3-khou2 e5 kang-chok.  Pek-jim2 ti7 chit-e5 ka-teng5 e5 seng-oah8 si7 chin put-heng7.  A-ku7 khoaN3 i cho3 gu5-be2 lai5 khou2-chhou2 iam3-chian7 i.  I tak8-jit8 long2 ti7 soaN-ia2 teh kap thou5-be5 cho3-hoe2.  Ti7 ha7-thiN u7 jiat8-iam7 e5 jit8, ti7 koaN5-thiN u7 han5-leng2 e5 pak-hong teh khou2-chhou2 i e5 sin-khu.
U7-si5 khoaN3-tioh8 pat8-e5 ka-teng5 pe7-bu2 kiaN2-ji5 thoan5-lok8 e5 cheng5-heng5 lai5 thou2-khui3.  Ia7 u7 chin-choe7 chheng-lian5 lang5 cha2-am3 chhut-goa7 siong7-oh8 e5 cheng5-heng5, hou7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim seN-chhut chin-toa7 e5 sit-chi3 kap oan3-chheh.  I khai-si2 thong3-oan3 i e5 mia7-un7.  I e5 put-heng7 chiong-jit8 chhiong-moa2 i e5 sim, lai5 hou7 i si5-siong5 chin ut-chut.

I m7-bat kiaN5-kau3 le2-pai3-tng5 khi3, le2-pai3 jit8 choan5-chng e5 peh-siN3 long2 bo5 cho3-kang khi3 le2-pai3, khiok i ka-ki7 chau2-kau3 soaN-ia2 e5 chhau2-pou khi3 to2 ti7 chhiu7-kha.
¡§Li2 si7 choe7-ok e5 kiaN2, li2 e5 choan5-sin long2 u7 choe7-ok u3-oe3 e5 huih teh lau5, li2 eng3-kai tioh8 thong3-hoe2 iu-siong lai5 kiu5 Thian-chu2 sia3-bian2 li2 e5 choe7, na7 bo5 li2 tek-khak ti7 choe7-ok tiong tim5-lun5!¡¨  A-ku7 siong5-siong5 an2-ni tui3 i kong2.  Chong2-si7 i kou3-i3 hoan2-tui3 kau3 le2-pai3-tng5.  U7-si5 na7 kou-put-chiong lai5 tui3 hia keng-koe3, i chiu7 phui3-noa7 kong2, ¡§U7 sim2-mih8 Thian-chu2!  I si7 put-gi7 put-hoat e5 sin5 lah!¡¨
Lang5-lang5 iam3-ou3 i, i ia7 iam3-ou3 lang5, choan5 se3-kai3 pai5-thek i, i ia7 pai5-thek choan5 se3-kai3. 
Kau3 18 hoe3 e5 si5 Pek-jim2 chiu7 khai-si2 ka-ki7 ke3-siok8 thak8-chheh.  Tak8-mi5 long2 ti7 i e5 pang5-keng lai5 am3-chiN7 gian2-kiu3.  I e5 sin-the2 ia7 i2-keng chin seng5-sek8 kiat-sit8 lah.  Ti7 chit e5 chng-sia7 chha-put-to bo5 lang5 oe7-thang kap i pi2-pheng7.  I chiaN5-cho3 chit8-e5 han2-tit khoaN3-tioh8 e5 eng-chun3, chheng-siu3 e5 chheng-lian5.  I e5 iok8-bong7 ia7 khai-si2 sio-toh8 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.
¡§Goa2 tioh8 lou2-lek8, lai5 soe2 goa2 long2-chong2 e5 kian3-siau3.  Goa2 tioh8 tui3-khong3 choan5 se3-kai3, tioh8 cheng-hok8 i!¡¨
I siong5-siong5 chiuN7 kau3 soaN-nia2 teng2 khoaN3 loh8 peng5-iuN5 e5 tou-chhi7 lai5 an2-ni koat-sim.
Ko2-jian5 bo5-ku2 i u7 tit-tioh8 chit8-e5 ki-hoe7 thang li7-khui chit e5 hoan2-kam2 e5 chng-sia7, khi3 hok8-bu7 ti7 Tai5-lam5 chhi7-lai7 chit8-keng choe3-toa7 e5 pah-hoe3 kong-si.  I chit8 hong-bin7 kong-chok chit8 hong-bin7 khun5-khun5 thak8-chheh.  Au7-lai5 Pek-jim2 chiu7 chin3-jip8 ti7 chit8-keng chhi7-lip8 e5 ia7-hak8 thak8 tiong-hak8 e5 kho3-theng5.  I hui-siong5 jin7-chin khin5-bian2, ti3-kau3 long2 kap pat8-lang5 u7 chin toa7 e5 hun-piat.  4 ni5 au7 ia7-hak8 pit-giap8 e5 si5 i chiu7 tit-tioh8 chu-keh khi3 kho2-chhi3 Tai5-pak e5 ko-teng2 hak8-hau7.  I put-toan7 e5 lou2-lek8 kap jiat8-jiat8 e5 sim-chi3 pang-chan7 i, hou7 i chin ho2 e5 seng5-chek lai5 kip8-keh, koh soa3 oe7-thang tit-tioh8 kai-hau7 e5 chiong2-hak8-kim.
Pek-jim2 e5 lou2-lek8 chin-toa7 seng5-kong lah!  Khiok i bo5 liah8 chit e5 choe3 kau3-giah8 lai5 sit-loh8 kin2-sin7, si7 tit-tioh8 chhut-lat8 e5 te7-pou7 lai5 it-hoat ke-thiN lou2-lek8.  I lian5 khun3 e5 si5-kan ia7 kiam2-chio2, bo5-lun7 ti7 sim2-mih8 sou2-chai7, chheh long2 bo5 
li7-khui i e5 chhiu2.  I ia7 chhim-chhim po2-siu2 kou-toaN e5 seng-oah8.  Sou2-i2 i e5 seng-chek si7 tek8-piat chhut-kun5.  Sim7-chi3 i u7 chin tek8-piat bun5-nga2 e5 goa7-mau7 hou7 lang5 boe7-thang khoaN3-chhut u7 sim2-mih8 ou-am3 e5 cheng5-sin5.
Ti7 chiah e5 su7, chu7-jian5 hou7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim hoat-seng chin toa7 e5 iu-oat, kiau-ngou7.  I e5 iok8-bong7 it-hoat chi3-liat8 sio-toh.  Ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 u7 chin toa7 e5 chu7-sin3.
Chong2-si7 i thak8-kau3 te7-ji7 ni5 boe2 e5 si5 hut-jian5 hoat-kak u7 jiam2-tioh8 hi3-piN7.  Sin-the2 jit8-jit8 siau-san2 soe jiok8 khi3.
Chit e5 su7 tu2-tu2 si7 si2-heng5 e5 thih-thui5 kong3 ti7 i e5 thau5-khak chit8-iuN7, hou7 i it-chhe3 long2 toa7 io5-tang7.  I khai-si2 pang3-sak i e5 chheh lah.  I chhin-chhiuN7 tui3 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 poaN3-thiN koh siak-loh8 kau3 ti7 ou-am3 choat8-bang7 e5 chhim-ian.  Hit e5 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 poaN3-thiN si7 eng7 ho5-teng2 ke3-chiN5 lai5 tit-tioh8 e5-, hou7 i kam2-kak bo5 hoat-tou thang jim2-siu7 chit e5 su7-sit8.
¡§Goa2 long2-chong2 e5 lou2-lek8 kap siu7-khou2 ti7 to2-ui7?¡¨  I ti7 hak8-hau7 hu3-siat e5 peN7-iN lai7, chhin-chhiuN7 sit-sin5 bo5 leng5-hun5 e5 lang5 che7 tiam7-tiam7, long2 bo5 tin2-tang7.  I kui2-na7-jit8 long2 bo5 chiah8-png7, mi5-si5 ia7 m7-chai i u7 khun3-khi3.  Oan3-than3 kap choat8-bang7 e5 toa7-hun5 pau-bat8 i e5 choan5-sin.
¡§TaN beh an2-choaN2?!¡¨  I chin3-cheng5 siuN7 ia7 siuN7 bo5, to3-tng2 siuN7 ia7 siuN7 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8, it-chhe3 long2 si7 bong5-bong5 biau2-biau2.  Au7-lai5 i chiu7 chin chhiN-chhin3 e5 khoan2 lai5 ka-leng2-sun2 soa3 khia7 khi2-lai5 kiaN5-kau3 thang-a2 piN khi3.
¡§Choat8-keng2!  Choat8-keng2!¡¨  I chi2-u7 soe3-siaN lai5 an2-ni liam7 ti7 chhui3-lai7.
¡§I phah-hoai7, chhiuN2-toat8 goa2 e5 it-chhe3!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chhiN gin5-gin5 e5 bak8-chiu giah8 koaiN5 khoaN3 thiN.  ¡§It-chhe3 long2 liau2 lah!¡¨  I chiu7 koh kiaN5 kau3 i e5 chhng5 lai5 phak ti7 chhng5-teng2.

¡§Chai-lan7, goa2 kap li2 u7 sim2-mih8 koan-he7!¡¨  I ka-ge5, chhiat-chhi2, gim7 chhiu2 lai5 phah chim2-thau5.  Au7-lai5 chiu7 siang-chhiu2 lam2 i e5 thau5-khak lai5 hau2.
Keng-koe3 chit8-jit8, nng7-jit8, saN-jit8 e5 hoan2-bun7, siong-pi ti3-kau3 hou7 i e5 bak8-chiu chhut-huih lah.  Khiok Pek-jim2 bo5 koan2 it-chhe3, i chiong-jit8 koaiN-bat8 ti7 i e5 piN7-pang5, bo5 ai3 kiN3 lang5 e5 bin7.  I e5 sin-the2 oan5-choan5 soe-pai7 lah.  Bak8-chiu ia7 khai-si2 bong5-bu7 lah.
Kau3 ti7 chiaN5 le2-pai3 au7 u7 chiap-tioh8 hak8-hau7 the3-hak8 e5 soan-ko3 e5 si5, Pek-jim2 chiu7 thng3 i e5 piN7-saN, loah8 i e5 thau5-mng5, cheng2-li2 i e5 mih8-kiaN7, tan2-hau7 hong5-hun-am3 e5 si5 chiah am3-chiN7 chau2-chhut peN7-iN7.
I tit8 tit8 kiaN5 tui3 tong-si5 choe3 lau7-jiat8 e5 Eng2-lok8 ke loh8-khi3, au7-lai5 chiu7 oat tui3 Tai5-pak toa7-kio5 kiaN5-khi3.
Na7 siat-su2 u7 lang5 siong5-se3 khoa3-kiN3i e5 bin7-iong5 a2-si7 thai7-tou7, lang5 beh kam2-kak chin-toa7 e5 ki5-koai3 lai5 kong2:
¡§Chit-lang5 si7 tui3 bong7-lai7 chhut-lai5 e5 sin-si mah?!¡¨
Khiok tong-si5 e5 Tai5-pak si7 ti7 tai7-chian3 ui5-bat8 e5 e7-bin7 chin leng2-cheng7, hi-bi5.
Tai7 Tang-a-chian3 i2-keng ian2-pian3 kau3 ti7 se3-kai3 ji7-chhu3 tai7-chian3, chhu3-chhu3 chhiong-moa2 chian3-cheng e5 khi3-hun kap but8-chit seng-oah8 siong7 chiong2-chiong2 e5 thong2-che3.  Tai5-pak chiaN5-choe3 chit8-e5 im-tim5, am3-ut, kin2-tiuN e5 tou-chhi7.
Mi5-kan e5 tian7-teng siu7 koan2-che3 i2-lai5 ke-lou7 siong7 han2-han2 u7 lang5, chi2-u7 si7 kun-tui7 e5 oah8-tang7 put-chi2 hian2-jian5 na7-tiaN7.
Khiok Pek-jim2 e5 sim long2 thoat-li7 liau2 chiah e5 su7-cheng5.  I chit8-pou7 chit8-pou7 lai5 peh-chiuN7 hit e5 chhu-koaiN5 e5 toa7-kio5 teng2 khi3.  Kio5-teng2 ke-lou7 long2 chin chio2 lang5 teh ong2-lai5, na7 u7 ia7 si7 chin kin2-kip e5 khoan2.

Tong-si5 lang5 kiaN-liau2 siu7 hiam5-gi5, koh long2-chong2 e5 khong-khi3 hou7 lang5 chin kin2-tiuN.
¡§Goa2 iau2-u7 chit8-tiau5 tui3-khong3 e5 lou7,¡¨ i kiaN5-kau3 kio5 e5 tiong-cham7 chiu7 oa2 ti7 hit-e5 kio5-lan5, lai5 khoaN3 loh8 kio5-kha e5 chui2.  Tui3 Pang-kio5 hong-bin7 u7 chio3 thiN-teng2 e5 kng-soaN3 gou7 lak8 tiau5 ti7 hit e5 ou-am3 kiaN-hiaN5 e5 khong-tiong teh chau2-lai5 chau2-khi3.  Hit-e5 kng-soaN3 u7 hoan2-chio3 ti7 an-cheng7 seh-seh lau5 e5 tam7-chui2 khoe- bin7.  Han2-han2 u7 chhia kap lang5 ti7 au7-bin7 teh koe3.  Hiah e5 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu long2 tang5 chit8-iuN7 e5 ki5-koai3 teh kong2.
¡§Ti7 chit e5 si5-ki5 chit e5 lang5 tiam3 chia teh cho3 sim2-mih8?  Kiam2 u7 hit e5 pang3-sim mah?!¡¨
Khiok Pek-jim2 long2 bo5 teh koan2 in e5 su7.  I e5 bak8-chiu chi2-u7 ki-hai5-tek toe3 hit e5 ti7 chui2-bin7 teh io5-choah, siu5-lai5 siu5-khi3 e5 kng-soaN3.
¡§Put-heng7 e5 phaiN2-sin5, goa2 kiam2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang tui3-hu3 li2 mah?!  Kho2-ou3 siu7 chiu3-chou2 e5 mia7-un7, goa2 kiam2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang kai2-koat li2 e5 khu-sok mah?!  Goa2 siu7-chin7 li2 e5 gek8-thai7 lah!!  Goa2 su-iau3 kai2-koat lah!¡¨
Bak8-sai2 e5 chui2-choaN5 moa2-lau5 i e5 bin7.  Koe3-khi3 long2-chong2 e5 pi-chham2 long2 chhut-hian7 ti7 i e5 thau5-nau2 lai7.
¡§Goa2 tek-khak bo5 beh khut-hok8 li2!¡¨  I kin2-kin2 tong3-tiam7 bak8-sai2 lai5 gin5 bin7-cheng5 e5 thiN.
Tai5-pak chhi7 e5 ou-iaN2 phu5-chhut ti7 khoe e5 tang-peng5-hoaN7.  An-cheng7 bo5 choe3-siaN teh khun3.  Chong3-toa7 e5 Tai5-oan5 soaN-meh8 ia7 chiam3-moa2 khong-tiong e5 chit8-poaN3.
¡§Se3-kai3 ah, goa2 ai3-bou7 li2 e5 bi2-le7, li2 e5 ge7-sut8, li2 it-chhe3 e5 pu3-u7 kap khoai3-lok8, khiok kiat-kiok8 goa2 sit-loh8 li2, eng2-oan2 kap li2 sou-oan2 lah!  Goa2 lok8-ngou2 ti7 li2 e5 kha-e7......¡¨

Bak8-sai2 koh lau5 chhut, pi-siong koh tin2-tang7 i e5 choan5-sin.
¡§Kho2-ou3 e5 mia7-un7, li2 thai3 li7-hai7 lah!  Li2 toan7-choat8 goa2 e5 oah8-lou7!  Li2 chiaN5-cho3 goa2 e5 kiu5-siu5!¡¨
¡§Goa2 ia3-sian7 lah, goa2 su-iau3 an-hioh!¡¨  I ti7 chhui3-lai7 soe3-siaN lai5 thou3-lou7 moa2-pak e5 choat8-bang7 kap oan3-hun7.  I e5 bak8-sai2 tit8-tit8 lau5-chhut.
¡§Ti7 chit e5 chui2-te2 e5 se3-kai3 u7 eng2-kiu2 e5 an-cheng7 bong5-khiok¡]§Ñ«o¡^.  I beh tui3 goa2 e5 thau5-nau2 lai7 chhat-siau long2-chong2 put-heng7 e5 phaiN2-bang7.¡¨
¡§Hit e5 leng2-cheng7 chui2-te2 e5 se3-kai3 si7 tu2-tu2 hou7 pai7-pok chia2 thang eng2-oan2 siam2-bih e5 sou2-chai7.¡¨
¡§Put-heng7 e5 chhiu2 ah, li2 u7 sim2-mih8 hoat-tou7 thang khou2-chhou2 goa2!¡¨
¡§I e5 bak8-chiu khoaN3-loh8 hit e5 chui2-te2.  Koh khoaN3 hit e5 khong-tiong.  U7 hai2-hong chhin-chhiuN7 kui2-sin5 e5 siaN, hiu-hiu hau2.  Hiah e5 kng-soaN3 hou7 i e5 bak8-chiu ou-ng7, i chiu7 khiN5-oa2 ti7 hit e5 kio5-lan5, i kam2-kak i e5 i3-sek u7 chiam7-chiam7 beh chau2 bo5-khi3, iau2-ku2 i lou2-lek8 ban2-hoe5, lai5 poaN5-koe3 kio5-lan5, chiu7 chhut-lat8 chiong i loan2-jiok8 e5 sin-khu hiat tui3 hit e5 chhim-chhim e5 chui2-te2 loh8-khi3.  ¡§Ah!!¡¨  Leng2-cheng7 e5 chui2 chiong Pek-jim2 e5 sin-khu thun lok8-khi3.
5 PEK-JIM2 KHOAN3-KIN3 BI5-KNG
¡§Sin-khu u7 khah sio-lo7 lah!¡¨  U7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 siaN teh kong2.  ¡§I2-keng u7 chap8-tiam2 goa7-cheng ku2 e5 keng-koe3 lah, theng5 chit8-si5-a2 na7-bo5 chheN2 khi2-lai5 chiah koh chu3-sia7.¡¨  U7 ta7-pou lang5 e5 siaN teh kong2.
¡§Khia7 ti7 hit e5 kio5-teng2 iok-liok8 u7 30 hun, jian5-au7 chiu7 poaN5 hit e5 kio5-lan5 lai5 thiau3-loh8 khoe-te2, ou-am3 mi5 long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3, na7 m7-si7 tu2-tu2 u7 chun5-a2 ti7 khoe-teng2 teh hioh-mi5 chiu7 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang kiu3 i.¡¨  U7 chit8 e5 Jit8-pun2 chheng-lian5 teh kong2.
¡§Sin-the2 u7 piN7, tui3 an3-ni pi-koan chu7-sat e5 khoan2.¡¨  Ia7 u7 pat8 e5 lang5 an2-ni kong2.  I2-goa7 iau2-u7 chin-choe7 siaN-im, hiah-e5 u7-si5 tioh8 u7 thiaN-kiN3, u7-si5 tioh8 bo5 thiaN-kiN3.  Chiah e5 kong2-oe7 e5 siaN si7 te7-it pai2 hoe5-hok8 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 thau5-nau2 sou2 thiaN-kiN3 e5... khiok sui5-si5 koh m7-chai lang5 khi3.  Kau3 i koh chheN2 e5 si5, tak8-hang7 long2 chin an-cheng7, chi2-u7 thiaN-kiN3 si5-cheng teh khok! khok! e5 siaN na7-tiaN7.
 ¡§Hoe5-hok8 lai5 e5 khoan2 lah, sin-khu teh tin2-tang7 lah!¡¨  Keng-koe3 chin-ku2 u7 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 siaN lai5 kio3-chheN2 Pek-jim2, i chiah beng5-beng5 hok8-to3 i e5 i3-sek.  Si5-kan tu2-tu2 si7 koe3-jit8 e5 e7-pou si5 lah.
Pek-jim2 hoat-hian7 i to2 ti7 chit8-keng piN7-iN7 sek e5 lai7-bin7.  Ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 u7 chit8-ui7 tiong-lian5 e5 i-seng kap i-seng niu5, in oa2-kin7 ti7 i e5 sin-khu teh ka7 i u3-peng.  Pek-jim2 bak8-chiu khui e5 si5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 in nng7-lang5 hoaN-hi2 teh chhio3 e5 bin7, tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 pau ti7 hun5-bu7 e5 lai7-bin7 chit8-iuN7 chin bo5-beng5.
I thiap bak8-chiu beh khoaN3 khah-beng5, chong2-si7 hoat-kak tioh8 bak8-chiu i2-keng u7 sit-siong5.
¡§Siau3-lian5 lang5 ah, li2 chheN2 lah hoN3!  Chin kai-chai3!  Goan2 tui3 cha-mi5 chiu7 long2 bo5 khun3 teh khoaN3 li2 e5 cheng5-heng5.  TaN i2-keng bo5 iau3-kin2 lah!¡¨  I-seng chu5-pi e5 bin7 chin hoaN-hi2 chhio3-iong5 lai5 tui3 i an2-ni kong2.
¡§Chin-chiaN3 ho2 kai-chai3!  Chin kam2-sia7!  Na7 m7-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 pang-chan7, li2 chiu7 i2-keng sit-loh8 siN3-mia7 lah.  Chin thang kam2-sia7!  ChhiaN2 li2 tioh8 pang3-sim ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 hiu-iong2, long2 m7-thang koh siuN7 sim2-mih8.  Kiu5 Chu2 tam-tng li2 sou2 u7 e5 tang7-taN3 kap khun3-khou2.¡¨
