I-seng niu5 chin tong5-cheng5 e5 piau2-cheng5 lai5 tui3 i kong2.
¡§Lan2 m7-thang koh kiau2-jiau2 i, in-ui7 i tioh8 an-cheng7 hioh-khun3.¡¨  I-seng tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2 chiu7 koh oat8 koe3-lai5.
¡§ChhiaN2 li2 an-cheng7, na7 u7 ai3 sim2-mih8 chiah jih8 chit e5 tian7-leng5, tioh8 ai3 choat8-tui3 e5 an-cheng7 chiah oe7 eng7-tit.¡¨  I an2-ni hoan-hu3 chiu7 chhut-khi3.
Hu-hu7 li7-khui piN7-iN7-sek e5 si5 Pek-jim2 chiah beng5-pek8 i e5 siN3-mia7 u7 koh oah8-teh.  I eng7 chhiu2 lai5 bong i e5 thau5-khak kap sim-koaN.
¡§Goa2 bo5 si2 tioh8-m7?!¡¨  Bak8-sai2 hut-jian5 ong-moa2 i e5 bin7.¡¨  Goa2 e5 chhiN-chham2 iau2 tiN5-toe3 goa2!  PhaiN2-bang7 iau2 teh ke3-siok8!¡¨
Su7-sit8 chit e5 bek8-kiu3 ti7 i long2 bo5 hoaN-hi2, hoan2-tng2 si7 chai-lan7, toa7 sit-pai7.  I e5 cheng5-sin5 kek8-ki5 soe-jiok8 lah.
¡§Goa2 iau2-u7 sim2-mih8 ng3-bang7!¡¨  I chi2-u7 lau5 bak8-sai2 thi5-khau3 chiu7 koh khun3-khi3.
Pek-jim2 thiau3-chui2 liau2-au7, kio5-teng2 chhau3-kham2 u7 lang5 ti7 hia.  Koh ti7 kio5-e7 ia7 u7 tho2-hi5 e5 chun5 ti7 hia koe3-mi5.  Sou2-i2 sui5-si5 hou7 lang5 kiu3 kau3 ti7 hu7-kin7 e5 chit-keng goa7-kho piN7-iN7 khi3.
Chit-keng piN7-iN7 e5 chu2-lang5 Hoa5 sian-siN kap sian-siN niu5 si7 jiat8-sim keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3 e5 Ki-tok-kau3 tou5.  In siong5-siong5 in2-chhoa7 hoan7-chia2 lai5 bat Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3, ia7 choe7-choe7 pang-chan7 pin5-khun3 e5 lang5.  Beh khui-to chhiu2-sut8 e5 tai7-seng long2 ki5-to2 giong2-bong7 Siong7-te3 e5 pang-chan7.
In chih-tioh8 Pek-jim2 e5 si5 chiu7 kin2-kin2 ui7-tioh8 chit e5 put-heng7, siu7-khou2 e5 chheng-lian5 lai5 chau2-chong5, si-ioh8, chu3-sia7.  U7 Jit8-pun2 chheng-lian5 chiong it-chhe3 sou2 khoaN3-tioh8 e5 su7 lai5 soat-beng5 hou7 in chai.  Pek-jim2 kau3 ti7 poaN3-mi5 u7 kui2-na7-pai2 chhin-chhiuN7 beh hoe5-hun5 lai5, chong2-si7 tioh8 koh khun3-khi3.  Hit tiong-kan hiah e5 kiu3 i e5 lang5 long2 kun-sui5 ti7 sin-piN, kau3 thiN-kng cha2 tak8-lang5 chiah si3-soaN3 tng2-khi3.  Chi2-u7 Hoa5 sian-siN hu-hu7 ti7 i e5 sin-piN, teh siong5-se3 kam2-chhat i e5 cheng5-heng5.  In eng7 chhiu2 hoaN7 ti7 i e5 meh8, chong2-si7 ti7 in e5 sim-lai7 teh ui7-tioh8 chit e5 kho2-lin5 e5 lang5 pek-chhiat ki5-to2.  Kau3 hit e7-pou7 Pek-jim2 cheng5-sin5 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, in chiah pang3-sim hoaN-hi2 kam2-sia7 Siong7-te3 lai5 li7-khui khi3 hioh-khun3.
U7 pang-chan7 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 theh8 chiah8-mih8 hou7 Pek-jim2, ia7 u7 ke3-siok8 u3-peng, chu3-sia7, chiah8-ioh8.
Khiok Pek-jim2 chin oh-tit thong2-it i e5 i3-sek, bang7 kap hian7-sit8 long2 bo5 u7 kai3-han7 chin hun7-chap8 ti7 i e5 nau2-hai2.  I long2 teh khun3, u7-si5 chhiN2 e5 si5 chhin-chhiuN7 keng-koe3 kui2-na7 se3-tai7 e5 khoan2.  U7-si5 ia7 kam2-kak i si7 to2 ti7 hit e5 ou-am3, chhiN-chhin3, kiaN-hiaN5 e5 im-kan.  U7-si5 thi2-khui3 bak8-chiu e5 si5 sou2 khoaN3 e5 mih8 long2 bong5-bu7.  U7-si5 ia7 chai-iaN2 lang5 ti7 i e5 sin-piN teh cho3 sim2-mih8.  U7-si5 chiu7 hoat-hian7 i si7 kou-tok8 chit8-lang5 ti7 piN7-chhng5.  U7-si5 kam2-kak si7 jit8-si5, u7-si5 kam2-kak si7 mi5-kan.
Chiah e5 su7 hoan-hoan hok8-hok8 ti7 i e5 i3-sek e5 lai7-bin7.
Keng-koe3 kui2-jit8 Pek-jim2 e5 i3-sek u7 hoe5-hok8 lah.  Sin-the2 e5 khui3-lat8 ia7 hoe5-hok8 lai5.  I chiah kam2-kak i e5 bak8-chiu hou7 lang5 am khi2-lai5, ou-thiN toa7 am3 long2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8.
¡§Goa2 kiam2 oe7 chhiN-mi5 mah?!¡¨  I hut-jian5 siuN7-tioh8 chit e5 su7 lai5 tioh8-kiaN.
¡§Mia7-un7 ah, li2 kiam2 tioh8 hiah chan5-jim2!  Li2 khou2-chhou2 e5 chhiu2 iau2 bo5 theng5-chi2 mah?!¡¨  I e5 pi-siong thong3-khou2 ia7 hoe5-hok8 lim5-kau3 i e5 sim-lai7.
¡§Siau3-lian5 lang5 ah, li2 u7 khah ho2-se3 bo5?¡¨  U7 chit8-jit8 Hoa5 i-seng oaN7 i bak8-chiu e5 ioh8, khoaN3-kiN3 Pek-jim2 cheng-eng e5 khoan2-sit, chiu7 chhio3-chhio3 lai5 mng7 i.

¡§Sian-siN, hou7 li2 chin to-sia7!¡¨  Pek-jim2 an2-ni seh-sia7 i.
¡§M7-bian2 kheh-khi3, li2 tioh8 ai3 tau3 chhut-lat8 kap goan2 saN-kap chiau3-kou3 li2 e5 sin-the2, choat8-tui3 m7-thang khoa3-lu7, tioh8 pang3-sim, na7 bo5 li2 e5 bak8-chiu u7 gui5-hiam2!¡¨  Chit-ku3 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 to chhi3-jip8 Pek-jim2 e5 sim-lai7.
¡§Sian-siN ah, goa2 oe7 chhiN-mi5 tioh8-m7?!¡¨  Pek-jim2 khi2-sin khi2-lai5 beh mng7 i-seng.
¡§ChhiaN2 li2 choat8-tui3 an-cheng7, m7-thang tin2-tang7!¡¨  I-seng koh hou7 i to2 loh8-khi3.
¡§Na7 u7 pang3-sim chiu7 bo5 tai7-chi3.¡¨
¡§Goa2 beh an2-choaN2 pang3-sim neh?!¡¨  Pek-jim2, thou2 chit8-e5 toa7-khui3.
¡§Li2 si7 chit8-e5 chian5-tou5 liau5-oan2 e5 chheng-lian5 lang5, m7-thang ui7-tioh8 sio2-khoa2 e5 su7 lai5 chhoe7 si2-lou7, an2-ni si7 chin kian3-siau3 e5 su7.¡¨  I-seng e5 chhio3-iong5 chin kong-beng5.
¡§Sim2-mih8 lang5 chai goa2 e5 su7, na7 oe7 chai ia7 bo5 chit e5 tai7-chi3.¡¨  Pek-jim2, ti7 sim-lai7 an2-ni kong2.  I e5 bak8-chiu u7 bak8-sai2 e5 iaN2.
¡§Hi3-piN7, ti7 koe3-khi3 si7 chit8-chiong2 si2-piN7, lang5-lang5 chin kiaN, chong2-si7 hian7-chai7 chiu7 m7-si7 an2-ni.  Siong7-te3 hou7 lang5 u7 chin-toa7 e5 ti3-hui7, u7 chin-choe7 i-hoat kap tek8-hau7 ioh8 thang hou7 lan2 tui3-hu3 chit e5 piN7 lah.  Sit8-chai7 hi3-piN7 si7 bo5 bun7-te5 e5 su7.  Ui7-tioh8 an2-ni chiu7 lai5 chhoe7 si2-lou7, si7 chit8 e5 gu5-gong e5 su7.¡¨
I-seng soa3 chhio3 chhut-lai5.  Hit-si5 i-seng niu5 ia7 jip8 lai5 khia7 ti7 i e5 chhng5-piN.
¡§U7 khah ho2-se3 bo5?  M7-thang hoan5-lo2, tioh8 pang3-sim kau-thok Siong7-te3, in-ui7 ban7-hang7 su7 long2 si7 chhut ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 ho2 i3-su3.  Lan2 chi2-u7 tioh8 sun7-hok8 i.¡¨  Sian-siN niu5 e5 siaN chin nga2-khi3.

¡§Na7 u7 Siong7-te3, i si7 chit8-e5 chan-jim2, put-gi7 e5 Siong7-te3.¡¨  Pek-jim2 ti7 sim-lai7 an2-ni in3-tap, chong2-si7 chhui3-lai7 chi2-u7 soe3-siaN kong2. 
¡§Goa2 bo5 sin3 Siong7-te3, goa2 m7-si7 Ki-tok-tou5!¡¨
¡§Sin3 Siong7-te3 m7-si7 han7 ti7 chit8-pou7-hun7 e5 lang5 na7-tiaN7, si7 tak8-lang5 tek-khak tioh8 sin3 e5 su7, in-ui7 lan2 long2 si7 I e5 chu2-bin5, I e5 peh-siN3.¡¨  I-seng niu5 soa3-chiap koh kong2.
¡§Siong7-te3 bo5 su-iau3 goa2.  I ia7 bo5 su-iau3 goa2 chun5-chai7.¡¨  Pek-jim2 e5 siaN kap bin7 long2 chin hun3-khai3.
¡§Siong7-te3 chin su-iau3 li2!  I tek8-piat koan-sim ti7 li2, in-ui7 si7 chit8-e5 gek8-keng2 siu7-khou2 e5 lang5.  Li2 eng3-kai tioh8 jin7-bat hit e5 koan-sim li2 e5 Siong7-te3.¡¨  I-seng niu5 e5 siaN koh-khah jiat8-chhiat.
¡§Lan2 lang5 long2 u7 choe7, long2 si7 pai7-hoai7, sou2-i2 su-iau3 Siong7-te3 e5 kiu3-un, tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 i-seng su-iau3 hoan7-chia2, hoan7-chia2 su-iau3 i-seng chit8-iuN7.¡¨  Hoa5 i-seng an2-ni kong2 lai5 khah8-khah8 chhio3, chong2-si7 hut-jian5 koh piN3 giam5-siok e5 bin7.
¡§Khiok u7 hoan7-chia2 si7 chit-khoan2 e5_, ka-ki7 u7 tang7-piN7 khiok m7-chai i e5 piN7-cheng3.  Hit khoan2 e5 hoan7-chia2 si7 choe3 hou7 i-seng ma5-hoan5.¡¨  I-seng kong2 liau2 chiu7 koh chhio3.
Pek-jim2 kat-bak8 boe7 beng5-pek8 hiah e5 i3-su3.
¡§Lan2 lang5 long2 si7 chit8-e5 choat8-bang7 bo5 chin2-kiu3 e5 choe7-jin5.  Choe7-ok pai7-hoai7 chit e5 se3-kan i2-lai5, lang5 bo5 u7 chin-sit8 e5 peng5-an, bo5 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 ng3-bang7, bo5 u7 chin-li2 e5 lou7.  Goan5-lai5 e5 lok8-hng5 hian7-si5 si7 chiaN5-choe3 pai7-hoai7 si2-hiat e5 se3-kai3.  Choe7-ok m7-si7 tiam3 ti7 goa7-khau2, si7 ti7 lang5 e sim-lai7.¡¨  I-seng niu5 eng7 chhiu2 pi2 i e5 sim.
¡§Se3-kai3 sou2-u7 e5 put-heng7, pi-chham2, thong3-khou2, iu-siong long2 si7 choe7-ok sou2 san2-seng e5 mih8.  Lan2 long2 si7 choat8-bang7 e5 choe7-jin5, in-ui7 u7 choe7-ok e5 kun hoat-seng ti7 lan2 e5 sim-lai7.¡¨
I-seng niu5 e5 bin7 chin jin7-chin.

¡§Tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 gam5-hoe e5 kun ti7 lang5 e5 sin-the2 siN-thoaN3, kau3-boe2 chiu7 pai7-hoai7 lang5 e5 siN3-mia7 chit8-iuN7.¡¨  Hoa5 i-seng soa3-chiap sian-siN niuN5 an2-ni kong2.
¡§Goa2 e5 keng2-gu7 chin tek8-piat, se3-kan bo5 u7 lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 goa2, goa2 chu7-jian5 bo5 u7 ki-hoe7 thang hong3 chhiong3 su-iok8 chhin-chhiuN7 se3-kan it-poaN e5 khoan2-sit.¡¨  Pek-jim2 e5 sim chin kan-khou2, i e5 in3-tap chin thiu-siong7-tek, chong2-si7 Hoa5 i-seng kap i-seng niu5 long2 beng5-pek8 i e5 sim-su.
¡§Choe7-ok long2 bo5 hun-piat sim2-mih8 khoan2 lang5, a2-si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2 seng-oah8.  Choe7-ek ia7 oe7 hou7 lang5 e5 iok8-bong7 oai-chhoah8 khi3, lang5 iok8-bong7 Siong7-te3 e5 iok8-bong7 piN3-chiaN5 kau3 ti7 iok8-bong7 se3-kan khi3, chit e5 chiu7-si7 choe7-ok pai7-hoai7 e5 kang-chok.¡¨  I-seng niu5 khoaN3-kiN3 Pek-jim2 u7 beng5-pek8 chit e5 chiu7 sim-lai7 hoaN-hi2 lai5 bi5-chhio3.  Khiok Pek-jim2 e5 sim kam2-kak toa7 e5 ap-pek lai5 kan-khou2.
¡§Goa2 si7 chit8-e5 se3-kai3 e5 pai7-pok-chia2, goa2 sit-loh8 se3-kai3 it-chhe3 e5 khoai3-lok8 kap heng7-hok.¡¨
¡§Tham-ai3 se3-kai3 e5 kiat-kiok8 siong5-siong5 si7 tioh8 si2 ti7 se3-kai3 e5 e7-bin7, chhin-chhiuN7 iong2-su7 teh loan5-bou7 bi2-jin5, siong5-siong5 long2 si7 in-ui7 bi2-jin5 lai5 si2 ti7 bi2-jin5 e5 kha-e7.¡¨  Hoa5 i-seng koh chhap-chhui3.
Chiah e5 oe7 tak8-ku3 long2 chhi3-chhak8 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim hou7 i kam2-kak chin lan5-koe3, i chiu7 bo5 ai3 koh thiaN chit-khoan2 e5 oe7, chhin-chhiuN7 jim2-siu7 boe7-tiau5 e5 khoan2 lai5 tin2-tang7 i e5 thau5-khak.
I-seng, i-seng niu5 sui-jian5 khoaN3-chhut chit e5 su7, iau2-ku2 tit8-tit8 ai3 beh in2-chhoa7 i bat chin-li2.  ¡§Siong7-te3 tek-khak bo5 pai7-hoai7 I ka-ki7 e5 kang-chok, bo5 leng5-jiok8 ka-ki7 e5 sou2-choe3.  Long2 si7 lang5 e5 poe7-gek8, choe7-ok e5 ham7-hai7.¡¨
¡§Iau2-ku2 Siong7-te3 bo5 choat8-bang7, sui-jian5 choan5 se3-kai3 long2 poe7-gek8 I, I iau2-ku2 si7 teh thiaN3 lan2.  I u7 chiong I tok8-siN-kiaN2 Ia5-sou2 siuN2-su3 se3-kan, lai5 beh kiu3-siok8 lan2 u7 choe7 e5 lang5.¡¨
¡§Ia5-sou e5 chhiu2 put-si5 chhun tng5-tng5 teh tan2-hau7 lan2, kong2, hoan7-choe7 e5 
lang5 ah, tng2-lai5 ouh!  Chi2-u7 lan2 na7 hoaN-hi2 chun lan2 e5 chhiu2 lai5 chiap-lap8 I e5 chhiu2, lan2 chiu7 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 ng3-bang7.¡¨
¡§Siong7-te3 e5 kiu3-un chiu7-si7 an2-ni, m7-si7 ti7 lan2 u7 sim2-mih8 ho2 thang tit-kau3 tit-kiu3, si7 chhim-chai ka-ki7 si7 chit8-e5 bo5 ng3-bang7 pai7-hoai7 e5 choe7-jin5 ti7 choe7-tiong giah8 thau5 beh giong2-bong7 I e5 lang5 oe7-thang peh8-peh8 tit-tioh8 I e5 kiu3-un.¡¨
¡§Sou2-i2 lang5 tioh8 ti7 Ia5-sou lai5 chai ka-ki7 si7 choe7-jin5, lai5 hoan2-hoe2, jin7-choe7, na7 bo5 hoan2-hoe2 chiu7 bo5 u7 chin2-kiu3, na7 bo5 jin7-bat ka-ki7 e5 cheng5-heng5, chiu7 bo5 u7 sin3-sim giong2-bong7, na7 bo5 giong2-bong7 chiu7 bo5 u7 kiu3-un.¡¨
¡§Siong7-te3 m7-bat hai7 lan2 lang5 chhiN-chham2, a2-si7 hoaN-hi2 lang5 put-heng7.  Long2 si7 choe7-ok e5 ham7-hai7.  Sou2-i2 ti7 chit e5 se3-kai3 long2 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 pat8 e5 ng3-bang7, tu5-liau2 Chu2 Ia5-sou beh hou7 lan2 e5 ng3-bang7 i2-goa7.¡¨
¡§Lang5 tioh8 khoaN3 bo5 it-chhe3, lai5 tui-kiu5 Ia5-sou kap I sou2 eng3-un2 e5 kok.  Chiu7-si7 chin-sit8 peng5-an, khoai3-lok8 e5 kok.  In-ui7 ti7 hit e5 kok chi2-u7 THIAN3 si7 in e5 tiong-sim, in e5 goan5-thau5.¡¨
¡§Tu5-khi3 chit e5 su7, ti7 se3-kan lang5 long2 piN5-piN5 tioh8 hiong2-siu7 choe7-ok e5 koe2-chi2, chiu7-si7 choat8-bang7, thong3-khou2, si2-sit.¡¨
¡§Lang5 na7 bo5 ti7 Ia5-sou lai5 hoan2-hoe2 teng5-thau5-siN, tek-khak si7 kap chit e5 se3-kai3 piN5-piN5 biat8-bong5.¡¨
¡§In-ui7 CHOE7-OK e5 kang-chiN5 chiu7-si7 SI2!  Lang5 chi2-u7 chit e5 tong5-it e5 mia7-un7, hit e5 mia7-un7 kio3-choe3 SI2!¡¨
¡§Ti7 si2 e5 lai7-bin7 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 heng7-hok put-heng7, sun7-keng2 gek8-keng2, long2 si7 piN5-piN5 siu7 thun-biat8, kau3 ti7 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 chha-piat.¡¨
¡§Ki-tok-tou5 liah8 sip8-ji7-ke3 choe3 i e5 eng5-iau7 khoa-khau2.  Sim2-mih8 kio3-choe3 sip8-ji7-ke3, chiu7-si7 hi-seng, leng5-jiok8, siu7-khou2.¡¨
¡§In-ui7 ti7 hit e5 eng3-un2 e5 kok, lan2 lang5 e5 siu7-khou2 beh piN3-chiaN5 lan2 e5 eng5-iau7.  Siong7-te3 e5 thiaN3 beh am-moa2 it-chhe3 e5 put-heng7, ti7 hia u7 moa2-moa2 e5 an-ui3.¡¨
Tui3 i-seng niu5 e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 chhut-lai5 chiah e5 oe7, chhin-chhiuN7 chheng3-chhut e5 chui2-choaN5, tit8-tit8 koan3-jip8 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim-lai7, hou7 i siN-chhut chin-toa7 e5 hoan2-bun7 kap pe2-pak.
I kau3-boe2 soa3 eng7 siang-chhiu2 lai5 lam2 i e5 thau5-khak, piau2-beng5 sim-lai7 e5 toa7 io5-tang7.
I-seng niu5 e5 oe7 long2 bo5 lun2-neh, chit8-ku3 chit8-ku3 chhi3-jip8 i e5 sim lai5 phoa3-khui i e5 i3-liam7.
¡§Sou2-thiaN3 e5 hiaN-ti7 ah, li2 tioh8 sin3 Ia5-sou kap i e5 chin2-kiu3!  In-ui7 li2 tek8-piat su-iau3 kiu3-un.  Siong7-te3 ia7 tek8-piat su-iau3 li2, li2 tioh8 chiap-siu7 Ia5-sou cho3 li2 e5 Kiu3-chu2 lai5 kai2-pian3 li2 it-chhe3 e5 sim-su liam7-thau5, chiu7-si7 oan3-than3, choat8-bang7, pi-siong e5 sim, chiah e5 si7 ti7 li2 e5 lai7-bin7 oe7 ti3-kau3 li2 si2 e5....
Li2 na7 chiap-siu7, li2 e5 hok-khi3 tek-khak chin-chiaN3 toa7 ti7 thiN-nih8!¡¨
I-seng niu5 e5 siaN-im in-ui7 koe3-thau5 e5 pek-chhiat kap heng7-hun3 chiaN5-choe3 chin-koan5.  Sit8-chai7 i e5 sim moa2-moa2 lin5-bin2 tong5-cheng5 chit e5 chheng-lian5 lang5 e5 leng5-hun5.  I chhun i e5 siang-chhiu2 lai5 khiN5-oa2 Pek-jim2 e5 chhiu2, tit8-tit8 chhui-pek i tioh8 chiap-siu7, i ka-ki7 e5 bak8-chiu ia7 u7 bak8-sai2 teh sui5-loh8.
Pek-jim2 e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 beh piak-lih8 chit8-iuN7 e5 thong3-khou2, i e5 bak8-chiu tit8-tit8 chhoe7 tang chhoe7 sai, i e5 chhui3 ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, kau3 boe2 soa3 pang3-siaN toa7-hau2.  I chin7 i long2-chong2 e5 siaN-liong7 lai5 toa7-hau2, ti3-kau3 i chham2-chheh e5 khau3-siaN long2 tin2-tang7 peN7-iN7 lai7.

¡§Choan5 se3-kai3 ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN!¡¨
Cheng3 thiN ah, li2 tioh8 thiaN goa2 e5 siaN!  I e5 khau3 tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 chit e5 khoan2-sit, toa7-toa7 kai2-hong3.
I-seng tit8-tit8 kiong5-pek i an-cheng7, khiok i-seng niu5 khia7 ti7 piN-a2 lai5 khai-si2 ui7-tioh8 i ki5-to2.
¡§Siong7-te3 ah, li2 kho2-lin5 chit e5 lang5!  Siong7-te3 ah, li2 tioh8 eng7 li2 bin7 e5 kng lai5 kng-chio3 i, hou7 i cha2 chit8-jit8 tit-tioh8 Li2 e5 lin5-bin2, in-ui7 i si7 tek8-piat su-iau3 Chu2 li2 e5 lang5.¡¨  I-seng niu5 e5 bak8-sai2 hou7 i bo5 hoat-tou7 thang koh ke3-siok8 ki5-to2, i chi2-u7 theh8 i e5 chhiu2-kin khi2-lai5 chhit i e5 bak8-sai2.
Pek-jim2 e5 thi5-khau3 chiam7-chiam7 soe-bi5 khi3.  I-seng niu5 hut-jian5 gim5-si chhut-lai5, hit e5 an-cheng7 e5 siaN-im hou7 Pek-jim2 e5 siaN long2 tiam7-khi3.
¡§Siong7-te3 chai li2 e5 iu-siong,KhoaN3-kiN3 li2 e5 bak8-sai2.Soe3-siaN kong2, Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh, Li2 boh8-tit sit-bang7.
I chai-iaN2 li2 e5 kou-toaN, Kap li2 saN-kap siu7-khou2, I tam-tng li2 e5 tang7-taN3, I tek-khak khoaN3-kou3 li2. 
Siong7-te3 chai li2 e5 sim siong, Chai li2 sin-chiuN7 khou2-thang3, Ti7 ou-am3 tiong giah8-bak8 khoaN3 I, I bo5 pang3-sak li2.¡¨
I-seng niu5 e5 siaN-im chhin-chhiuN7 hian5 e5 hiang2-liang7 thang3-kau3 piN7-iN7 sek e5 mui2 chit8-e5 kak-thau5, sim7-chi3 chhin-chhiuN7 thang3-kau3 ti7 lang5 sim-leng5 e5 lai7-bin7.

Pek-jim2 kin2-kin2 eng7 siang-chhiu2 lai5 am-bat8 i e5 hi7-khang, i e5 bin7 chhin-chhiuN7 gin2-na2 beh hau2, hau2 boe7 chhut-lai5 e5 bin7, ti7 kek8-ki5 khun3-lan5 thong3-khou2 e5 si5 sou2 hoat-chhut e5 piau2-cheng5.  I chiu7 phak-to2 ti7 hit e5 thou5-teng2.
¡§Lang5 chi2-u7 u7 chit8-e5 tong5-it e5 mia7-un7, hit e5 mia7-un7 kio3-cho3 si2!  Ti7 hit e5 si2 e5 lai7-bin7 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 heng7-hok a2-si7 put-heng7, sun7-keng2 a2-si7 gek8-keng2, long2 si7 piN5-piN5 siu7 thun-biat8, kau3 ti7 long2 bo5 u7 sim2-mih8 chha-piat!¡¨
Hoa5 i-seng niu5 e5 oe7 chit8-ku3 chit8-ku3 koh hian2-chhut ti7 i e5 sim-lai7, i thau5 giah8 khi2-lai5, chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 teh thiaN sim2-mih8 oe7 e5 khoan2.
¡§Lan2 lang5 long2 si7 chit8-e5 choat8-bang7 bo5 chin2-kiu3 e5 choe7-jin5.  Choe7-ok pai7-hoai7 chit e5 se3-kan i2-lai5, lang5 bo5 u7 chin-sit8 e5 peng5-an, bo5 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 ng3-bang7, bo5 u7 chin-li2 e5 lou7.  Goan5-lai5 e5 lok8-hng5 hian7-si5 si7 chiaN5-cho3 pai7-hoai7, si2-hiat8 e5 se3-kai3!¡¨  I chhin-chhiuN7 tui3 chiah e5 oe7 lai5 tit-tioh8 chin-toa7 e5 kai2-tap chit8-iuN7.
¡§Siong7-te3 chin su-iau3 li2, I tek8-piat koan-sim ti7 li2, in-ui7 li2 si7 chit8-e5 gek8-keng2, siu7-khou2 e5 lang5, li2 eng3-kai tioh8 jin7-bat hit e5 koan-sim li2 e5 Siong7-te3!¡¨
¡§Siong7-te3 e5 chhiu2 put-si5 tioh8 chhun tng5-tng5 teh tan2-hau7 lan2, kong2 u7-choe7 e5 lang5 ah, tng2-lai5 ouh.  Chi2-u7 lan2 na7 hoaN-hi2 chhun lan2 e5 chhiu2 lai5 chiap-lap8 I e5 chhiu2, lan2 chiu7 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 ng3-bang7.¡¨

¡§Lang5 tioh8 khoaN3 bo5 it-chhe3 lai5 tui-kiu5 Ia5-sou kap sou2 eng3-un2 e5 kok, chiu7-si7 chin-sit8 peng5-an, khoai3-lok8 e5 kok.  In-ui7 ti7 hit e5 kok chi2-u7 thiaN3 si7 in e5 tiong-sim.¡¨
¡§Tu5-khi3 chit e5 su7, ti7 se3-kan lang5, long2 tioh8 piN5-piN5 hiong2-siu7 choe7-ok e5 koe2-chi2, chiu7-si7 choat8-bang7, thong3-khou2, si2-sit!¡¨
¡§Sou2 thiaN3 e5 hiaN-ti7 ah, li2 tioh8 sin3 Ia5-sou kap i e5 chin2-kiu3!  In-ui7 li2 tek8-piat su-iau3 kiu3-un, Siong7-te3 ia7 tek8-piat su-iau3 li2, li2 tioh8 chiap-siu7 Ia5-sou cho3 li2 e5 Kiu3-chu2 lai5 kai2-pian3 li2 it-chhe3 e5 sim-su liam7-thau5.¡¨
Hoa5 i-seng niu5 e5 bin7 ia7 hian2-chhut ti7 i e5 bak8-cheng5, siang-chhiu2 khui-khui, eng7 khun2-chhiat e5 siaN lai5 koh teh khou2-khng3 i tioh8 sin3 Ia5-sou.
Pek-jim2 e5 bin7 phak-loh8 ti7 toe7-bin7 lai5 pang3 -siaN toa7-khau3.

7 SIOu2 THIN-SAI3 E5 CHHUT-HIAN7
Chit e5 su7 koe3 bo5 ku2 Jit8-pun2 kun chiu7 hang5-hok8 pai7-chian3.  Tui3 an2-ni chiaN5 chap8-ni5 lai5 e5 chian3-su7 kap khun3-khou2 ou-am3 e5 seng-oah8 chiu7 kiat-sok.
Jit8-pun2 e5 kun-bin5 chiu7 chun2-pi7 hoe5-kok, ke-thau5 hang7-boe2 long2 chhiong-moa2 li7-piat e5 ai-siu5.
Hiah e5 hong-hoe3 pha-hng e5 khi3-siong7 ke-thiN chit8-chiong2 bu5-han7 e5 kam2-siong2.
Soa3-chiap kok-kun lim5 Tai5, chhu3-chhu3 u7 hoan-geng5 e5 hou-siaN kap koa-im, khiok hiah e5 hoan-geng5 e5 siaN iau2 boe7 soah e5 si5, Tai5-oan5 chiu7 ham7-loh8 ti7 chit8 e5 koh-khah giam5-tiong7 e5 keng-che3 gui5-ki.
Choat8-bang7 kap ou-am3 khai-si2 pou3-moa2 choan5 Tai5.  Tui3 an2-ni u7 siN-chhut ji7-ji7-pat su7-kiaN7.

Au7-lai5 chiu7 chiaN5-cho3 kiong7-san2 chu2-gi7 e5 ui7-hat kap chhim-hoan7.  Soan2-tek8 chu7-iu5 lai5 to5-thoat chhia-hoa e5 Tai7-liok8 e5 peh-siN3, liok8-siok chau2 kau3 Tai5-oan5.
Hiah e5 kun-koaN bin5-chiong3 toa3-tioh8 chu7-iu5 Tiong-kok tok8-chu7 e5 bin5-chu2 hong-khi3 lai5 Tai5-oan5 tiong5-sin khai-si2, Tai5-oan5 tui3 an2-ni chiu7 pou7-jip8 ti7 chit8 e5 oan5-choan5 kng-beng5, chu7-iu5, hoan-eng5 e5 sin se3-tai7.
Hiah e5 siu7-siong phoa3-hai7 long2 koh siu-cheng2, tit8-tit8 hiong3 kian3-siat sin ki5-oe7(´Á¹º¡^e5 Tai5-oan5 lai5 teh chin3-heng5.  Tou-hoe7 e5 hoan-hoa, kau-thong e5 pou7-siat, seng-san2 e5 keng3-cheng, seng-oah8 e5 hiong2-siu7 long2 si7 chiam7-chiam7 teh to3-tat8(¨ì¹F¡^ti7 chit8-e5 oan5-seng5 e5 ng5-kim si5-tai7.
Sui-jian5 ti7 goa7-tek u7 chiah e5 hian2-jian5 e5 hoat-tat8, chong2-si7 lai7-tek u7 hok8-chap8 e5 pian3-chhian, i2-kip8 koe3-khi3 hiah e5 chian3-cheng kap koe3-tou7 si5-ki5 ou-am3 khun3-khou2 e5 si5-tai7 sou2 siu7 e5 siong-hun5 iau2 lau5 ti7 lang5 e5 sim-lai7 teh thang3-thiaN3.
Pek-jim2 ti7 chit e5 pian3-hoa3 to-toan e5 si5-ki5, i ia7 sui5 sia7-hoe7 tiau5-liu5 lai5 ke3-siok8 i liu5-long5 phiau-liu5 e5 hong-tin5 seng-oah8.
Lan2 koh khoaN3-kiN3 i e5 si5 si7 i2-keng keng-koe3 kong-hok8 chap8-goa7 ni5 e5 si5-kan lah.  I hut-jian5 chhut-hian7 ti7 hit-e5 hoan-hoa¡]ÁcµØ¡^bu5-siong5 e5 Tai5-pak chhi7.  Lan2 khoaN3-kiN3 i chha-put-to beh koh jin7 boe7-chhut i.  Ti7 Tai5-lam5 hit-e5 chham2-tam7 leng2-loh8 e5 Pek-jim2 long2 kap hit-e5 si5-tai7 koe3 liau2 lah.  Hian7-chai7 e5 Pek-jim2 si7 chit8-e5 chhou-lau7 e5 sin5-su7, i-hok8 cheng2-che5, khoan2-sit bun5-nga2 e5 lang5.  I e5 thau5-mng5 khai-si2 teh tng5-peh8 lah, i e5 bin7-mau7 chin chong3-giam5, put-heng7 siong5-siong5 oe7 hou7 lang5 ham7-loh8 ti7 chit-chiong2 bu5-gian5 e5 giam5-siok.  Khoah-toa7 e5 thau5-hiah8 u7 hian2-chhut eng-chun3, kui3-khi3.  Koan5-tit8 e5 phiN7 piau2-beng5 kiong5-ngiN7 e5 i3-chi3.  Thap-thap e5 bak8-chiu u7 am3-si7 chhim-o3 e5 su-siuN2.
I e5 hong-chhai2 na7 it-khoaN3 put-chi2 u7 chin3-pou7, khiok na7 khoaN3 khah ku2 chiu7 chai ki5-sit8 u7 toa3 tioh8 chin tang7 e5 kou-tok8 kap soe-pai7 ti7-teh.  U7-si5 lang5 e5 goa7-mau7 oe7 kap lai7-sim tu2-tu2 tui3-hoan2, Pek-jim2 si7 it-le7.  Lang5 ti7 kek8-ki5 kou-toaN, soe-pai7 e5 
si5, i oe7 eng7 goa7-mau7 e5 chng-thaN7 lai5 am-moa5 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu.
Kong-hok8 tong-chhou i u7 tui3 hoe5-kok e5 Jit8-pun2 lang5 lai5 tit-tioh8 chit8-ki chhiu2-the5-khim5.  Chit-ki khim5 si7 i sou2 u7 e5 it-chhe3.  Chit-ki khim5 ia7 hou7 i e5 seng-oah8 u7 chit8-e5 sek-chhai2 kap chhu3-bi7.  I eng7 choan5 cheng-sin5 koan3-jip8 ti7 i e5 khim5.  I ti7 i e5 seng-oah8 chhoe7-chhut chit8-e5 i3-gi7.  I kong2 chit-ki khim5 si7 goa2 e5 leng5-hun5, in-ui7 i thoe3 goa2 kong2 chhut choe7-choe7 sim-lai7 e5 gian5-gu2.  Pek-jim2 kio3 chit-ki khim5 cho3 Ni-na2.  I toa3 Ni-na2 kau3 ti7 lou7-piN lai5 gim5-si.  I chiong i e5 bo7-a2 khng3 ti7 kha-cheng5 lai5 kiu5-khit tam7-poh8 chiN5 cho3 i e5 seng-oah8.
Sui-jian5 hoan2-kong Tai7-liok8 e5 siaN tit8-tit8 han2-hoah, iau2-ku2 sia7-hoe7 jit8-jit8 hoat-tat8, chin3-tian2.  Jin5-khau2 e5 cheng7-ka oe7 hou7 lang5 siN-chhut put-an e5 theng5-tou7 teh chheng3-koan5, khiok ti7 seng-oah8 siong7 ia7 khoaN3-kiN3 chin han2-tit u7 heng7-ju7, an-tiaN7.  Tui3 an2-ni lang5-lang5 tui-kiu5 hiong2-lok8 e5 hong-khi3 chin ong7-seng7.
Pek-jim2 ti7 chit e5 sin si5-tai7 e5 khoan5-keng2 u7 put-chi2 khah chin3-pou7.  I e5 goa7-tek seng-oah8 u7 sui5 chit e5 sia7-hoe7 e5 hoat-tian2 khah ho2-se3, khiok ti7 i e5 sim-lai7, hiah e5 koe3-khi3 chhiN-chham2 pai7-loh8 e5 cho7-gu7, chhin-chhiuN7 si2-piN7 e5 pai5-hoe5 chiaN5-cho3 phaiN2-bang7 tiong e5 phaiN2-bang7, hou7 i siu7 chin-toa7 e5 koan2-hat chi-phoe3.
Hit e5 kou-toaN, iu-chhiu5 e5 iaN2 long2 bo5 li7-khui i e5 sin-chiuN7, hoan2-tng2 ke-thiN sin e5 heng5-the2, na2 hian2-beng5 chhut-lai5.
Na7-si7 i e5 oan3-than3 pi2 i2-cheng5 u7 khah leng2-loh8, i e5 iok8-kiu5 bang7-siong2 chha-put-to long2 siau-biat8 bo5 iaN2 lah.  I e5 hian7-sit8 chi2-u7 beh an2-choaN2 lai5 tui3-hu3 kou-tok8 kap pi-ai chiu7 i2-keng kau3-giah8 lah.  Ti7 chit e5 si5 Ni-na2 si7 i choe3-toa7 e5 an-ui3, i u7-si5 kap i kong2-oe7, u7-si5 ia7 chim i.
Pek-jim2 boe7 kau3 Tai5-pak e5 i2-cheng5 long2 si7 phiau-iu5 ti7 tiong-pou7 e5 kok toe7-hng, toa7-pou7-hun7 si7 Tai5-tiong, Chiong-hoa3 choe3 kin-ku3-toe7 lai5 khai-si2 i e5 iu5-gim5 seng-oah8.  Ti7 hit e5 tiong-kan, i u7 ng3-bang7 oe7-thang koh kau3 ku2-ku2 li7-piat8 e5 Tai5-pak khi3.  Tui3 ti7 Tai5-pak kio5-teng2 si2 bo5 seng5 i2-lai5 i2-keng u7 keng-koe3 chap8-goa7 ni5 e5 jit8-chi2 lah.  Hoa5 i-seng, i-seng niu5 ti7 hit-jit8 tui3 i kong2 hiah e5 oe7 
long2 chhin-chhiuN7 in3-siong7 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.
Hit-si5 kau3 chit-si5, na7 hoe5-kou3 lai5 khoaN3, u7 ho5-teng2 e5 pian3-hoa3 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.  Ki-tok-tou5 tui3 i si7 chit8-chiong2 ki5-biau7, oh-tit li2-kai2 e5 lang5.  Sui-jian5 si7 an2-ni i kam2-kak i su-iau3 in e5 oe7.  In-ui7 in u7 ki5-biau7 e5 gan2-kong, ki5-biau7 e5 thau3-thiat, sim7-chi3 u7 ki5-biau7 e5 ng3-bang7.  In e5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 liang7-kng hou7 i beng5-pek8 ka-ki7 e5 toe7-ui7, kong-keng2(¥ú´º¡^.  I e5 li2-ti3, i3-chi3, long2 ti7 chiah e5 ki5-biau7 e5 leng5-lat8 e5 bin7-cheng5 the3-pai7 lah, i chu7-sin3 e5 kin-goan5 u7 toa7 io5-tang7.  I kam2-kak i tioh8 khut-hok8 ti7 hit e5 sin5-pi3 e5 e7-bin7, chiu7-si7 Ki-tok-tou5 sou2 chhim-sin3 hit e5 to7-li2 e5 e7-bin7.
I am3-chiN7 siuN7 ai3 koh khi3 chhoe7 Hoa5 i-seng, i-seng niu5.  Tai5-pak i2-keng chiaN5-cho3 chit8-e5 jiat8-khai e5 kok-che3 tou-chhi7!  Pek-jim2 kau3 Tai5-pak e5 si5 khoaN3-tioh8 Tai5-pak e5 toa7 pian3-oaN7 lai5 tioh8-kiaN.  I ti7 ke-lou7 u7 tu2-tioh8 kui2-na7 pai2 hiam2-hiam2 hou7 chhia kauh-si2.  Ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 i e5 sim kam2-kak koh khah toa7 e5 kou-tok8, hiah e5 jiat8-kun2 e5 siaN-im hou7 i siN-chhut kiaN-hiaN5 kap chhiN-sou.  Keng-koe3 kui2-jit8 e5 un2-bat8 i chiah chhut-lai5 tham3-mng7 Hoa5 i-iN7.
Tai5-pak e5 chhi7-iong5 long2 toa7 kai2-pian3 lah.  Tak8-hang7 long2 pian3-chhian, hou7 i chhoe7 long2 bo5.
¡§Hoa5 i-seng!  Goan2 m7-bat i!¡¨  I khia7 ti7 jin5-ke tiam3-thau5 lai5 mng7 lang5, in long2 an2-ni in3 lai5 cho3 in jip8-khi3.  I kui cha2-khi2 lai5 chhoe7 mng7 Hoa5 i-iN7, khiok u7 lang5 kong2 sou-khai khi3 Hoa-lian5-kang2 chiu7 long2 bo5 koh tng2 lai5 lah.
Pek-jim2 thiaN-tioh8 chit e5 siau-sit sim-lai7 chin siong-pi, choat8-bang7 lai5 li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7.
I sun7 hit tiau5-lou7 lai5 kiaN5 kau3 oa2 ti7 Tam5-chui2 khoe-piN e5 chui2-mng5 lou7 khi3.  Sui-jian5 si7 ji7-geh8 thiN, chong2-si7 hit-jit8 tek8-piat sio-joah8.  Lang5-lang5 long2 chhut-lai5 ti7 khoe-piN teh phak8-sio, chhut-goa7 ong2-lai5 e5 lang5 ti7 chit e5 sou2-chai7 iu5-goan5 chhin-chhiuN7 teh sio-kheh, chin nau7-jiat8.  Thai3-iong5 e5 kng hoan2-sia7 ti7 
khoe-chui2 e5 bin7, hoat-chhut chin peh8-kng.  Hng7-hng7 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Tai5-pak toa7-kio5.  Kio5-teng2 u7 bu5-sou3 e5 lang5 kap chhia teh kau-ong2.
Pek-jim2 kiaN5 kau3 chit8-ui7 khah khoah koh an-cheng7 e5 sou2-chai7, chiu7 khai-si2 beh cho3 i e5 kang.
I chiu7 thoat bo7-a2, khng3 ti7 kha-cheng5, pi7-pan7 i e5 khim5, chiu7 oe-khim5 chhut-lai5.  Au7-lai5 chiu7 soa3 soe3-siaN lai5 gim5-si.  U7 ke-lou7 e5 lang5 theng5-tiam7 in e5 kha-pou7 lai5 kiaN5-oa2 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Chit8-e5..., nng7-e5..., bo5 loa7-ku2 chiu7 chin-choe7 lang5 ui5-lui5 ti7 i e5 sin-piN.
Hit-si5 A-hoa tu2-tu2 kiaN5 kau3 hit sou2-chai7.  I chiu7 kheh lang5 e5 kha-phang7 lai5 chiN3 kau3 siang7 thau5-cheng5 khi3.  Pek-jim2 oe-khim5 gim5-si e5 khoan2-sit, ti7 chit e5 sia7-hoe7 siong7 put-chi2 si7 iN7-chhai2 hi-ki5.
I gim5-si liau2 e5 si5 chiu7 ng3 lang5 tam3-thau5, piau2-si7 oan5-pit kap kiu5-khit.  U7 kui2-lang5 sui5-si5 lim5 chiN5 lai5 hiat ti7 bo7-a2 lai7.
Au7-lai5 lang5 long2 si3-soaN3, Pek-jim2 chiu7 khut-sin lai5 siu i e5 chiN5.
A-hoa long2 bo5 li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7, lai5 ke3-siok8 khoaN3 Pek-jim2 e5 heng5-tong7, in-ui7 ti7 i soe3-soe3 e5 sim u7 kam2-kak chit8-chiong2 hi-ki5, chhin-bit8 ti7 chit e5 lang5 e5 sin-chiuN7.  A-hoa u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chit8-e5 gun5-a2 ka-lauh8 ti7 toe7-nih8, chiu7 kin2-kin2 khioh khi2-lai5 heng5 hit e5 kap i pun2-sin u7 chit8-chiong2 lian5-he5 e5 lang5.
¡§Ia5-sou kap thiN-sai3 long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3, in bo5 ai3 lang5 u7 am3-sam3 bo5 kng-beng5 e5 sim.¡¨
Pek-jim2 kau3 taN m7-bat tu2-tioh8 gin2-na2 seng5-sit8 beh khioh chiN5 heng5 i, hoan2-tng2 long2 si7 tui3 bo7-a2 lai5 thau-theh8 khi3, chong2-si7 A-hoa e5 sou2 choe3 kap in3-tap hou7 Pek-jim2 chin ki5-koai3.
¡§Chit e5 gin2-na2 si7 Ki-tok-tou5 mah?  Chi2 u7 Ki-tok-tou5 chiah u7 chit-chiong2 sin5-pi3 e5 heng5-tong7.¡¨

I li7-khui A-hoa e5 si5, koh siuN7-tioh8 Hoa5 i-seng, i-seng niu5 sou2 tui3 i kong2 hiah e5 oe7.  I ia7 beng5-pek8 tui3 hit-si5 kau3 taN ti7 i e5 lai7-bin7 u7 chin-toa7 e5 kai2-kek lah.  I ng3-bang7 Ki-tok-tou5 oe7-thang hou7 i ta-so3 iau-go7 e5 sim tit-tioh8 pa2-chiok.  Ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 sou2 khat-bong7 e5 Ki-tok-tou5 tek-khak u7....  I e5 sim khai-si2 ai3 beh chhoe7-kiu5 hian7-se3 i2-goa7 e5, jin5-seng bun7-toe5.  Chiu7-si7 chin-li2, oah8-mia7.
I kam2-kak lang5 khia7-khi2 ti7 chit e5 bo5 chin-li2 bo5 oah8-mia7 e5 se3-kai3 si7 ho5-teng2 e5 pi-chham2.
Chong2-si7 Ki-tok-tou5 tui3 chiah e5 bun7-toe5 u7 chin-toa7 pa2-ak kap sin3-sim.  Ki-tok-tou5 oe7-thang kai2-tap hian7-se3 e5 khun3-lan5 soa3 chi2-ng3 chit8-e5 heng7-hok e5 lai5-se3, i2-kip8 beh chin3-jip8 hit-e5 lai5-se3 e5 hoat-tou7.
Pek-jim2 ti7 sim-lai7 kam2-kak i su-iau3 Hoa5 i-seng,i-seng niu5.  Khiok i2-keng bo5 ng3-bang7 thang koh kiN3 in e5 bin7 lah.  Na7 si7 ti7 hit e5 sit-bang7 tiong i u7 koh tu2-tioh8 leng7-goa7 chit8-chiong2 e5 Ki-tok-tou5.  I chiu7 koh siuN7 hit-e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 tui3 i sou kong2 e5 oe7.
¡§Long2 si7 chin sin5-pi3!  Tek-khak ti7 sin5-pi3 tiong u7 chin-li!¡¨
¡§Hit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 si7 sim2-mih8 khoan2 e5 Ki-tok-tou5, in-ui7 i ia7 chai-iaN2 i si7 Ki-tok-tou5 a2 m7-si7.¡¨  I kau3 ti7 chhiu7-kha, che7 loh8-khi3, chiah8 tiong-sit8 e5 si5 iau2-ku2 teh siuN7 chit e5 su7 bo5 soah.  Hut-jian5 thiaN-kiN3 u7 gin2-na2 teh hau2 e5 siaN.  ¡§Kiam2 si7 hit e5 gin2-na2?¡¨  I sui5-si5 siuN7 an2-ni lai5 mng7 i.
Tui3 A-hoa e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 kap khoaN3 i e5 cheng5-heng5 hou7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim it-hoat hi-ki5 chit-e5 gin2-na2.  I chai-iaN2 ti7 chit-e5 gin2-na2 e5 sin-chiuN7 u7 chin-toa7 e5 put-heng7, si7 tu2-tu2 oe7-thang kap i tang5-liat8 saN-pi2 e5 , chong2-si7 gin2-na2 long2 bo5 hou7 put-heng7 lai5 thun-biat8 i.  I u7 kong2 koh chit8-e5 put-heng7 e5 kou3-su7, chiu7-si7 Liap8-sat-lou7 pi-chham2 e5 it-seng.
Pek-jim2 chhoe7-tioh8 leng7-goa7 nng7 lang5 si7 thang pi2-kau3 i pun2-sin e5 e5 su7.  Ti7 
chiah e5 choat8-bang7 pi-chham2 e5 lai7-bin7 put-heng7 e5 tong5-chi3 teh giah8-bak8 ng3 thiN.  Ia7 u7 tong5-chi3 teh him-soan7 i e5 put-heng7.  Ti7 in e5 sim-lai7 u7 chit8-e5 li2-siong2 sim-su e5 kok, si7 oe7-thang kau3-giah8 an-ui3, tu5-siau in long2-chong2 e5 put-heng7 e5__.  Chit e5 ng3-bang7 e5 kng i2-keng khai-si2 chio3 ti7 in e5 sim.  Sou2-i2 ti7 in e5 sim-lai7 u7 hoaN-hi2.  Che si7 m7-si7, choat8-bang7 chia2 e5 chu7-ui3?!
Pek-jim2 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang jim2-siu7 chiah e5 su-siuN2 lai5 hoan2-bun7.  I chiu7 li7-khui cha-bou2 gin2-na2 khi3.
Pek-jim2 pho7-tioh8 choat8-bang7 khou2-thang3 e5 cheng5 lai5 chit8-pou7 chit8-pou7 kiaN5 kau3 Tai5-pak toa7-kio5 hong-bin7 khi3.
Siong-pi, ou-am3 ta3-oa2 i e5 sim.
¡§Eng2 boe7-thang boe7 ki3-tit e5 toa7-kio5!¡¨  I e5 kha tah8-jip8 kio5-teng2 e5 si5, i chin kam2-hun3.  Koe3-khi3 e5 hoe5-siong2 hou7 i kam2-kak oh-tit thun-lun2, i bo5 ai3 koh siuN7 hiah e5 su7, lai5 io5-thau5 koaN2-chau2 hiah e5 i3-liam7.  Sit8-chai7 i bo5 khui3-lat8 thang koh tui3-hu3 hiah e5 pi-chham2, khou2-thang3 e5 jit8-chi2.  ¡§PhaiN2-bang7!  PhaiN2-bang7!¡¨  I chu2-u7 io5-thau5 lai5 an2-ni kong2.  I kiaN5 kau3 hit e5 kio5-teng2, chiu7-si7 ti7 chap8-goa7 ni5 cheng5 i sou2 khia7 e5 sou2-chai7, i chiu7 tong3-tiam7 i e5 kha.  I kiaN-oa2 ti7 hit e5 kio5-lan5.  I e5 siong-pi ti3-kau3 beh hou7 i ou-am3-hin5 e5 khoan2.
¡§Tu2-tu2 si7 chap8-saN ni5 cheng5!¡¨  I an2-ni liam7 lai5 khiN5-oa2 kio5-lan5.  ¡§Khiok phaiN2-bang7 iau2-teh ke3-siok8!¡¨  U7 hai2-hong lai5 chhoe i e5 thau5-mng5.  Choe7-choe7 lai5-ong2 e5 chhia kap lang5 ti7 hit e5 kio5-teng2 bo5 si5-tiaN7 teh hoat-chhut chit8-chiong2 phaiN2-thiaN, tho2-iam3 e5 chap8-hiang2.
¡§I2-cheng5 hit e5 iong2-kam2, chu7-sin3 e5 Pek-jim2 ti7 to-loh?!  Lian5 hit e5 iaN2 ia7 bo5-thang koh chhoe7-tioh8!¡¨
I giah8 i e5 keng-thau5 lai5 ka-leng2-sun2.

¡§Pek-jim2 sit8-chai7 si2 khi3 lah!  Hian7-chai7 sou2 u7 e5 Pek-jim2 si7 chit8-e5 oan5-choan5 phoa3-chhui3 pai7-loh8 e5 lang5!  TaN iau2 u7 sim2-mih8 thang ban2-hoe5 chit e5 to2-hoai7!¡¨  I lau5 bak8-sai2 chhut-lai5.
¡§Goa2 e5 loan2-jiok8, khang-hi u7 sim2-mih8 thang koh saN pi2!
Goa2 e5 hian7-sit8 khiam2 m7-si7 hou7 iu-siong, kou-toaN saN-chiap khou2-chhou2 kau3 ti7 chiam7-chiam7 teh tim5-biat8 e5 lang5 mah!  Ah, goa2 su-iau3 an-ui3!  Chong2-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 oe7-thang sit8-chai7 an-ui3 lang5, koh sit-loh8 an-ui3 e5 lang5 beh ti7 ta2-loh8 lai5 chhoe7 u7 oah8-mia7 e lou7!  Long2-si7 choat8-bang7!¡¨  U7 khou2-nau2 e5 sek hian2-chhut ti7 i e5 thau5-hiah8.
¡§Chong2-si7 sui-jian5 an2-ni, goa2 iau2-ku2 su-iau3 sim2-mih8!  Na7 bo5 goa2 e5 oah8 hou7 goa2 tam-tng boe7-khi2.¡¨
Pek-jim2 tui3 i e5 thau5-nau2 lai5 io5-khui hiah e5 mi5-bat e5 su-siuN2.  I koh siuN7 hit e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2 e5 oe7.
Pek-jim2 han-jian5 siuN7 kau3 m7-chai7 lang5 khi3.
¡§A-peh ah, A-peh ah!¡¨  A-hoa e5 siaN hut-jian5 u7 kio3 chhiN2 i.
¡§A-peh ah, li2 sim2-mih8 si5 beh koh lai5?  Goa2 beh tiam3 chia tan2-hau7 li2!¡¨
I u7 koh thiaN-tioh8 leng7-goa7 chit8 e5 choat8-bang7 put-heng7 e5 lang5 e5 siaN-im.  Hiah e5 oe7 tai-seng hou7 i kiaN, chhin-chhiuN7 koh-chai3 tu2-tioh8 chit8-e5 sin e5 chai-lan7 chit8-iuN7.  I kin2-kin2 beh lai5 thoat-li7 hit e5, chong2-si7 A-hoa koh chit8-pai2 e5 siaN hou7 i m7-kaN2 chau2-khi3.  ¡§Chhin-chhiuN7 goa2 su-iau3 sim2-mih8, chit e5 oah8-mia7 su-iau3 goa2.  Goa2 kiam2 thang to5-thoat i mah?¡¨
A-hoa e5 sim khui-khoah khi2-lai5, i e5 sim u7 tian2-khui chit e5 ki5-biau7 e5 se3-kai3 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Sun5-chin, kng-beng5, bi2-biau7 e5 se3-kai3.

I ti7 A-hoa e5 lai7-bin7 u7 hoat-kian3 tioh8 chit8-e5 chin-toa7 e5 tui3-chio3, si7 i2-cheng5 m7-bat kam2-kak, m7-bat siuN7-tioh8 e5 tui3-chio3.  Chit8 e5 si7 siok8 thiN kng-beng5 khoai3-lok8, chit8 e5 si7 siok8 toe7, ou-am3 choat8-bang7.
Tek8-piat A-hoa sou2 gim5 chhut-lai5 e5 si, hou7 i chin kam2-tong7.  I khai-si2 kho2-chhat A-hoa e5 su7-cheng5, u7 i3-su3 beh toa3 A-hoa kap i khi3.  I ka-ki7 e5 put-heng7 ti7 choan5-sin e5 tiong-kan i2-keng the3 kau3 thiN-piN hai2-kak khi3 lah.
Pek-jim2 chiam7-chiam7 chin3-jip8 ti7 chit e5 ki5-biau7 e5 sio2-lu2 sou2 toa3 lai5 e5 se3-kai3 jip8-khi3.
In nng7-lang5 e5 hoe7-gu7 sit8-chai7 si7 thiN-nih8 ki5-biau e5 chi2-i3.  Chit8 e5 si7 siu7-chin7 liau2 put-heng7 e5 tiong-lian5 lang5, phau7-tioh8 choat8-bang7 oan3-than3, chit8 e5 si7 ti7 gek8-keng2 tiong m7-chai7 gek8-keng2, thian-chin oah8-phoat e5 sio2 kou-lu2.
Chit nng7-e5 se3-kai3 e5 ti2-chhiok sou2 beh hoat-seng e5 im-hiang2 na7 m7-si7 in nng7-lang5 ia7 tek-khak boe7-thang beng5-pek8 hit e5 bi2-biau7.
8 U7 CHIT8-E5 SE3-KAI3 OAN5-CHOAN5 KNG-BENG5
Tui3 Tai5-pak toa7-kio5 teng2 ki5-biau7 e5 hoe7-hap8 liau2-au7 keng-koe3 chiaN5-geh8 jit8, lan2 beh koh chit8-pai2 hoat-kian3 Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa chhut-hian7 ti7 kang2-tou Ki-lun5 e5 lou7-piN, chui2-gin5-teng kah teh gim5-si.  Gim5-si e5 siaN-im m7-si7 Pek-jim2, si7 A-hoa.
A-hoa iu3-eN kou2-chui e5 siaN u7 khip-in2 choe7-choe7 kang2-tou e5 peh-siN3 kap kun-jin5 lai5 ui5-oa2 ti7 in e5 sin-piN.
Kho2-lin5 bo5-chhu3 e5 sio2-niau, Li2 tui3 to2-ui7 chit8-e5 kok lai5,
A-hoa e5 siaN-im chin hiang2-liang7 beng5-liau5.  Pek-jim2 ngeh8 i e5 khim5 ti7 am7-kun2 e5 sou2-chai7, bak8-chiu kheh-kheh lai5 teh toe3 A-hoa e5 tiau7.  Pek-jim2 e5 bin7 u7 chit8-chiong2 e5 hoaN-hi2 boan2-chiok chhiong-moa2.

ThiN-sin5 e5 teng2-bin7, chhai2-kheng7 e5 boe2-liu, Hng7-hng7 poaN5-koe3 lang5 e5 bak8-chiu.
A-hoa long2 bo5 lun2-neh, chin chu7-jian5 chin khui-sim lai5 gim5-si.  I e5 thau5-mng5 u7 koe3 cheng2-li2 kau3 chin ho2-khoaN3, ti7 i e5 sin-khu ia7 u7 chit8-nia2 sin koh sui2 e5 iuN5-chong, ti7 i e5 kha ia7 u7 oe5.
A-hoa na2 gim5-si na2 eng7 chhiu2 lai5 bong i e5 saN, khiok i e5 bak8-chiu hoaN-hoaN hi2-hi2 teh khoaN3 lang5 e5 bin7.  Hiah e5 ui5-lui5 e5 lang5 khi2-chhou long2 teh khoaN3 A-hoa.  Au7-lai5 chiu7 hoat-hian7 tioh8 hit e5 chhiN-mi5 oe-khim5 e5 sin5-su7 si7 ka3-tit lai5 koan-chhat e5 lang5.
¡§Chit nng7-lang5 si7 sim2-mih8 teng2-ho7 e5 lang5?¡¨  Lang5-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu long2 chin ki5-koai3.
¡§Li2 e5 siang-kha tah8 ti7 ou-am3 e5 tin5-se3, Li2 e5 sim khiok bong7-siong2 bo5-soah.¡¨  
¡§Chit nng7-lang5 si7 pe7-kiaN2 e5 khoan2.¡¨
¡§Phah-sng3 si7 ho2-giah8 lang5 e5 pian3-sin, chian3-cheng e5 hi-seng-chia2.¡¨  U7 lang5 khai-si2 teh gi7-lun7 in.
¡§Sun7-chin si7 li2 e5 mia5, Chin-sit8 si7 li2 un2-bat8 e5 sit8-giau2.¡¨
A-hoa gim5-si liau2 e5 si5 in nng7-lang5 chiu7 che5-che5 hiong3 cheng5-lang5 tham3-thau5, ti7 in e5 kha-e7 u7 peng2-phak e5 bo7-a2.
Hiah e5 peng-teng, tek8-piat si7 chui2-peng, long2 toa7 hoaN-hi2 A-hoa e5 siaN, chiu7 chhut-siaN hoah koh phah-chhiu2 lai5 chheng-chan3 i, u7 lang5 i2-keng teh hiat chiN5 ti7 bo7-a2 lai7.  A-hoa chin hoaN-hi2, chiu7 khiu2 Pek-jim2 e5 chhiu2, siong5-siong5 giah8-bak8 lai5 khoaN3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7.
¡§Cha-bou2 gin2-na2, li2 chin gau5 gim5-si, li2 pat8-jit8 oe7 piN3-chiaN5 chin sui2 e5 sio2-chia2!¡¨
¡§Hiah-nih8 soe3-han3 chiu7 hiah-nih8 gau5 gim5-si, sit8-chai7 chhi7-tioh8 chin gau5 e5 kiaN2.¡¨

U7 nng7, saN e5 peng-teng thoa A-hoa oa2-khi3 lai5 bong i e5 chhui3-phoe2.
¡§Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 chin hok-khi3, u7 li2 chit-khoan2 e5 gin2-na2!¡¨  U7 chui2-peng kong2 an2-ni, chiong gou7-khou-gun5 hou7 A-hoa.  Pek-jim2 e5 bin7 u7 hoaN-hi2, chhin-chhiuN7 kng-beng5, ng3-bang7 e5 soaN3 teh chau2.
Au7-lai5 lang5 si3-soaN3 liau2-au7, Pek-jim2 chiu7 khut-oa2 ti7 A-hoa e5 hiN7-khang piN lai5 kong2.
¡§Li2 kim e7-pou gim5-liau2 chin ho2, li2 e5 siaN-im bo5 m7-tioh8!  Goa2 ia7 bo5 siuN7 li2 thau5 chit8-pai2 oe7 gim5 chiah ho2!¡¨
A-hoa chin phaiN2 i3-su3 e5 khoan2, chiong i e5 sin-khu the-oa2 Pek-jim2.
¡§A-peh ah, goa2 chit nia2 saN tui3 taN khi2 beh tak8-jit8 chheng7 tioh8 m7?!¡¨  A-hoa e5 sim chi2-u7 hoaN-hi2 i e5 sin-saN kap sin-oe5.
¡§Li2 hoaN-hi2 chit nia2 saN tioh8 m7?  Ho2, goa2 leng7-jit8 chiah koh boe2 chit8-nia2 hou7 li2.  Li2 khoaN3 lan2 kin-a2-jit8 e5 seng5-chek chiah-nih8 ho2!¡¨
Pek-jim2 chiu7 khai-si2 chip8-chiN5, A-hoa ia7 pang-chan7 i.
Au7-lai5 Pek-jim2 chiu7 toa3 A-hoa ti7 chhiu7-kha e5 chioh8-liau5 lai5 saN-kap che7, him-siong2 kang2-tou sui2 e5 chui2-sek.  Si5-kan i2-keng si7 hong5-hun-am3 lah.
Pek-jim2 e5 sim chin heng-hun3, tek8-piat thiaN-tioh8 hiah e5 lang5 e5 oe7, hou7 i chin boan2-chiok.  Ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 khai-si2 chit e5 bang7-siong2 si7 ku2-ku2 toan7-choat8 iaN2 e5....
¡§A-peh ah, hia u7 chit8-chiah chin toa7-chiah e5 toa7-chun5, ia7 u7 chit8-chiah chin soe3-chiah e5 sio2-chun5, in saN-kap tui3 hai2-nih teh jip8-lai5.  Hit-chiah toa7-chun5 phah-sng3 si7 pa-pa chun5, soe3-chiah e5 si7 kiaN2-chun5, saN-kap kheh-oa2 teh kiaN5.¡¨
Tu2-tu2 tui3 goa7-hai2 u7 nng7-chiah chun5 saN-chhoa7 teh jip8-lai5.  Ti7 kang2-khau2 
i2-keng u7 chin-choe7 kun-lam7 kap goa7-kok chun5 theng5 ti7 hia.  Chhia-thau5 e5 kng-toe7 u7 bu5-sou3 e5 lang5 kap chhia ti7 hia bo5-theng5 teh kau-chit, in chhin-chhiuN7 teh koaN2-kin2 beh tng2-khi3 in sio-lo7 un-loan2 e5 ka-teng5.  Hong i2-keng chiam7-chiam7 teh leng2 lah.  Pek-jim2 u7 lam2-oa2 A-hoa ti7 i e5 sin-piN, lai5 beh hou7 i bo5 tioh8 liang5.
Hit-si5 ti7 au7-bin7 toa7-lau5 e5 chit8-keng lu2-koan2 e5 pang5-keng u7 chit8-e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 bo5-liau5 che7 ti7 lau5-teng2 e5 thang-a2 khau2 teh khoaN3 Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa e5 heng5-tong7.
I u7 khoaN3-kiN3 chhiN-mi5 lang5 tiam7-tiam7 aN3-oa2 gin2-na2, chong2-si7 gin2-na2 u7 teh kong2-oe7 e5 khoan2, u7-si5 gin2-na2 ia7 teh pi2-tang pi2-sai.  Au7-lai5 chhiN-mi5 lang5 kap gin2-na2 chiu7 khai-si2 beh li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7.
Gin2-na2 u7 khan chhiN-mi5 lang5 e5 chhiu2, cho3-cheng5, in kiaN5 kau3 toa7-lou7 e5 si5 u7 tu2-tioh8 kui2-na7 tiuN chhia chau2-siam2 in e5 bin7-cheng5, chhiN-mi5 lang5 chiu7 cho3-cheng5 khan gin2-na2 lai5 iap ti7 i e5 au7-bin7.  In nng7-lang5 saN kheh-oa2 lai5 kiaN5-kau3 chit8-keng sit8-tng5, chiu7 jip8-khi3, theng5 beh poaN3-tiam2 cheng ku2 chiu7 koh khoaN3-kiN3 in saN-kap chhut-lai5.
Gin2-na2 cho3-cheng5, chong2-si7 kau3 toa7-lou7 e5 si5 chhiN-mi5 lang5 chiu7 koh hou7 gin2-na2 cho3 i e5 au7-bin7 lai5 khan gin2-na2 koe3 toa7-lou7.  In nng7-lang5 chin heng7-hok khoai3-lok8 e5 khoan2.  In oat8-jip8 ke-chhi7 e5 lai7-bin7 khi3, chiu7 khoaN3 boe7-tioh8 lah.
Pek-jim2 sou2 hioh e5 lu2-khoan2 si7 ti7 chhi7-tiong e5 chit8-keng ha7-teng2 e5 tiam3.  Tui3 peng5-keng e5 thang oe7-thang khoaN3-kiN3 chit8 pou7-hun7 pin5-bin5 e5 chhu3-teng2, ia7 koh chit8-e5 thang oe7-thang khoaN3-tioh8 soaN-teng2 e5 chhu3 kap goa7-hai2.
Hit e5 pang5-keng u7 nng7-teng2 khun3-chhng5 kap chit8-te3 toh.  Pang5-ok i2-keng chin ku7, chin phoa3-sun2, khiok cheng2-li2 chin chheng-khi3.  Pang5-keng e5 goa7-bin7 u7 chau2-long5, u7 tam7-poh8 toh-i2 ti7 hia beh hou7 lang5 che7.  Ti7 hit e5 chau2-long5 e5 e7-bin7 u7 chit8-tiau5 hang7-lou7 thang3 kau3 toa7-lou7.
Pek-jim2 tui3 gu7-tioh8 A-hoa, koh siuN7 beh khng3 A-hoa ti7 i e5 sin-piN liau2-au7, i chiu7 sui5-si5 chau2 kau3 Ki-lun5 lai5.  In-ui7 kiaN-liau2 oe7 hou7 lang5 hoat-kian3 tioh8 A-hoa.  

Ti7 i e5 liong5-sim lai7 u7 chit8-chiong2 e5 put-an kap kiaN-hiaN5.  ¡§Chit e5 gin2-na2 si7 m7-si7 u7 lang5 teh chhoe7?  U7-si5 siuN7-tioh8 chit e5 su7, ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 u7 chit8-chiong2 e5 ut-bun7.
Sou2-i2 ti7 lou7-piN gim5-si e5 si5 chit-chiong2 e5 kiaN-hiaN5 long2 bo5 li7-khui i e5 sim.  Tek8-piat ti7 chit kui2-jit8 e5 seng-oah8, hou7 i na2 kam2-kak i chin su-iau3 A-hoa.
Sit8-chai7 A-hoa e5 cheng5-iaN2 chin-kin2 e5 hoat-tian2 lai5 teh chiam3-moa2 Pek-jim2 khang-hi kou-tok8 e5 sim.
Hit chit8-mi5 in to2-chhng5 beh khun3 e5 si5, A-hoa hut-jian5 tu3 Pek-jim2 kong2-oe7.
¡§A-peh ah, li2 kiam2 si7 goa2 e5 pa-pa?  In-ui7 tak8-lang5 e5 gin2-na2 long2 u7 pa-pa, i2-cheng5 goa2 ia7 u7 lang5 cho3 goa2 e5 pa-pa, chit-tiap li2 beh cho3 goa2 e5 pa-pa tioh8 m7?  Goa2 kiam2 m7-si7 tioh8 kio3 li2 pa-pa!?¡¨
Pek-jim2 long2 bo5 in3 sim2-mih8, ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 chi2-u7 hoat-seng chit8-chiong2 e5 boan2-chiok kap hoaN-hi2.
¡§Chit nng7-lang5 si7 pe7-kiaN2 e5 khoan2.¡¨
¡§Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 tek-khak chin heng7-hok!¡¨
I koh siuN7-tioh8 ti7 lou7-piN sou2 thiaN-tioh8 e5 oe7.
¡§Chhut-chai7 li2 kio3, long2 oe7 eng7-tit!¡¨  Pek-jim2 an2-ni in3 A-hoa.
¡§An2-ni goa2 beh kio3 li2 pa-pa!¡¨  A-hoa chin hoaN-hi2, khi2-sin khi2-lai5 phak ti7 chhng5-teng2.
¡§Pa-pa, li2 m7-thang koh hou7 lang5 chhoa7 goa2 khi3 pat8-e5 sou2-chai7, in-ui7 goa2 ai3 kap li2 cho3-hoe2.¡¨  A-hoa e5 siaN hut-jian5 sit-loh8 chu7-jian5 oah8-khi3.
¡§Ti7 chia goa2 oe7-thang gim5-si, oe7-thang chheng7 saN, chheng7 oe5, koh ia7 oe7-thang chhut-lai5 ke-lou7 khoaN3-lang5.¡¨  A-hoa sou2 kio3 chhut-lai5 e5 oe7 u7 phah-tioh8  Pek-jim2 e5 sim.  I long2 bo5 in3-tap sim2-mih8, chi2-u7 tui3 i e5 chhng5 khi2-lai5, ti7 hit e5 piah-kak kiaN5-lai5 kiaN5-khi3, au7-lai5 chiu7 kiaN5 kau3 A-hoa e5 chhng5.
¡§Goa2 beh ka7 li2 ho7 chit8-e5 mia5, cho3 Li7-li7.¡¨  A-hoa e5 bak8-chiu chin toa7-khui.
¡§Li7-li7 si7 bo5 chhu3 e5 sio2-niau, ia7 si7 goa2 e5 eN-a2!  I ka-ki7 lai5 jip8 thau5-ke niu5 e5 chhu3!¡¨
¡§Si7..., Li7-li7 tu2-tu2 si7 li2!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chhun i e5 chhiu2 lai5 bong A-hoa e5 thau5-khak.
¡§Pa-pa, goa2 ti7 chia mia5 cho3 Li7-li7, au7-lai5 m7-chai beh koh pian3 sim2-mih8 mia5?¡¨
¡§Li7-li7, li2 e5 mia5 taN eng2-oan2 si7 Li7-li7, tek-khak bo5 koh pian3-oaN7.¡¨
A-hoa chin hoaN-hi2 chiu7 koh to2 ho2-se3, i e5 bin7 chhio3-chhio3, khiok bak8-chiu khai-si2 teh ai3 khun3 lah.
¡§Li7-li7, bak8-chiu khoeh-khoeh, kin2-kin2 khun3, lan2 bin5-a2-jit8 iau2-ku2 u7 kang-chok.¡¨  Pek-jim2 pang-chan7 i kah-phoe7 hou7 ho2-se3.
¡§Pa-pa, an-bin5!¡¨  A-hoa chiu7 choan2 i e5 sin-khu beh jip8-bin5, chong2-si7 hut-jian5 koh peng2 khi2-lai5.
¡§Pa-pa, beh khun3 e5 si5 lang5 tioh8 ai3 ki5-to2, goa2 chin ku2 long2 boe7 ki3-tit lah.  A-long5 e5 a-ma2 tak8-mi5 long2 chhoa7 A-long5 ki5-to2.  Pa-pa, li2 oe7-hiau2 ki5-to2 boe7?¡¨
¡§Goa2 boe7 hiau2-tit!¡¨  Pek-jim2 io5 i e5 thau5, 
¡§Li7-li7, li2 ki5-to2 hou7 goa2 khoaN3.¡¨  A-hoa chiu7 koh chit8-pai2 khi2-lai5, kui7 ti7 
chhng5-teng2, siang-chhiu2 hap8-hap8, bak8-chiu khoeh-khoeh lai5 ki5-to2.
¡§ThiN-teng2 e5 Siong7-te3, kiu5 Li2 chiau3-kou3 goa2 kap pa-pa peng5-an keng-koe3 chit e5 ou-am3 mi5.  Oa2-kho3 Chu2 Ia5-sou e5 mia5, A-men!¡¨  A-hoa chin hoaN-hi2, chiu7 koh jip8 chhng5 to2-teh.
¡§ThiN-teng2 e5 Siong7-te3 long2 chai-iaN2 lan2 e5 tai7-chi3, tak8-si5 long2 teh khoaN3-kou3 lan2, thiN-teng2 si7 Siong7-te3 kap thiN-sai3 sou2 toa3 e5 sou2-chai7, hit si7 chin khoai3-lok8, eng5-kng e5 sou2-chai7, tak8-jit8 long2 oe7-thang thiaN toaN5-khim5, chau3-gak8 e5 siaN, lang5 na7 sin3 Ia5-sou chiu7 si2-liau2 oe7-thang kau3 hit e5 sou2-chai7 khi3.  Pa-pa, li2 kiam2 chai-iaN2 hit e5 sou2-chai7?¡¨  A-hoa chiong keng3-khian5 e5 lau7 hu-jin5 lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7 lai5 koh teng5-sut8 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Pek-jim2 long2 bo5 chhut-siaN.  A-hoa chiu7 jip8-bin5 khun3-khi3.
Pek-jim2 thiaN A-hoa theng5-ku2 bo5 koh kong2-oe7 chiu7 chai-iaN2 si7 khun3-khi3.  I koh chit8-pai2 eng7 chhiu2 thoa-phoe7 lai5 ka7 A-hoa kah, soa3 bong i e5 thau5-khak, chiu7 aN3-chhui3 chim i e5 thau5-hiah8.
¡§An-bin5 kho2-lin5 bo5 chhu3 e5 sio2-niau!¡¨
Pek-jim2 chiu7 chiam7-si5 kiaN5-tah8 ti7 pang5-keng lai7, au7-lai5 chiu7 jip8 chhng5 beh khi3 khun3.
¡§Pa-pa, beh khun3 e5 si5 lang5 tioh8 ai3 ki5-to2!¡¨  Hut-jian5 A-hoa e5 oe7 koh phu5-chhut ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.
¡§ThiN-teng2 e5 Siong7-te3, kiu5 li2 chiau3-kou3 goa2 kap pa-pa!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chiu7 theng5-sin, lai5 kui7 ti7 chhng5-teng2.
¡§ThiN-teng2 e5 Siong7-te3 long2 chai-iaN2 lan2 e5 tai7-chi3, tak8-si5 long2 teh khoaN3-kou3 lan2, thiN-teng2 si7 Siong7-te3 kap thiN-sai3 sou2 teh toa3 e5 sou2-chai7.¡¨
Pek-jim2 chiu7 ban7-ban7 chiong i e5 bin7 ng3 ti7 hit e5 koaiN5-koaiN5 e5 thiN-teng2 khi3.

¡§Hia si7 chin khoai3-lok8, eng5-kng e5 sou2-chai7, tak8-jit8 long2 oe7-thang thiaN toaN5-khim5 chau3 gak8 e5 siaN, lan2 na7 sin3 Ia5-sou chiu7 si2-liau2 oe7-thang kau3 hit e5 sou2-chai7 khi3.¡¨  Hiah e5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 chau2-be2-teng e5 iaN2 lai5 kek-khi2 Pek-jim2 e5 sim.
¡§Siong7-te3 ah!  Siong7-te3 ah!¡¨  Pek-jim2 khui-siaN lai5 ki5-to2 Siong7-te3, chong2-si7 i hoat-kian3 i bo5 koh u7 pat8-mih8 oe7 thang koh ke3-siok8.
I chi2-u7 tiam7-tiam7 ti7 hia kui7, au7-lai5 thou2 chit8-e5 khui3 chiu7 jip8 chhng5 khi3 khun3.
Ke3-jit8, piN5-piN5 ti7 hit e7-pou, ti7 tui3-hoaN7 e5 kheh-koan2 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 u7 khoaN3-kiN3 Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa saN-chhoa7 kau3 ti7 hit e5 hai2-hoaN7 e5 chui2-gin5-teng kha lai5.
In sui5-si5 chun2-pi7 khai-si2 kang-chok.  Pek-jim2 seng gim5-si, au7-lai5 lang5 chiam7-chiam7 oa2-lai5 e5 si5 chiah hou7 A-hoa gim5.  I2-keng u7 chin-choe7 lang5 oa2-lai5 ui5-lui5 in, ti3-kau3 u7 thiaN-kiN3 siaN, bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 iaN2.
A-hoa gim5-si liau2 u7 chin-choe7 lang5 hoaN-hi2, lai5 phah-chhiu2, ia7 u7 lang5 teh hiat-chiN5.  Khiok Pek-jim2 koh ke3-siok8 lai5 gim5-si.  I e5 siaN-im put-chi2 u7 oah8-khi3, ti3-kau3 lau5-teng2 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 oe7-thang thiaN-tioh8 hiah e5 gian5-su5.
Ti7 chit e5 toa7-seh chhiong3-heng5 e5 phaiN2-mi5, Goa2 u7 bang7-kiN3 chit8-e5 phaiN2-bang7, Hit e5 phaiN2-bang7 phah-chhui3 goa2 e5 sun5-cheng5, I e5 iaN2 chiong-jit8 toe3-tiau5 goa2 e5 sim.
Goa2 e5 phaiN2-bang7 ka7-tiau5 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7, Hou7 goa2 ti7 i lai7-bin7 iu-chhiu5 pi-ai, I ti7 goa2 e5 sim-lai7 khia7 ong5-ki5, Goa2 e5 kou2-tong7 lian5-hap8 ti7 i e5 chong7-hu2.
Goa2 e5 phaiN2-bang7, li2 si7 goa2 e5 siN3-mia7, Li7-khui li2 goa2 bo5 u7 pat8 e5 ng3-bang7, In-ui7 li2 chhoa7 goa2 jin7-bat li2 e5 o3-pi3, Hou7 goa2 beng5-pek8 li2 e5 pu3-u7.

Ti7 li2 e5 chhau2--tiuN5 u7 hoan-lok8 e5 siaN, Si7 oah8-mia7 khoai3-lok8 e5 hoan-hou, Li2 e5 soaN-thau5 u7 kng-beng5 e5 ian-hoe2, SoaN-kok si7 li2 ban7-u7 e5 po2-khou3.
Goa2 e5 sim beh khoai3-lok8 gim5-si, In-ui7 hit e5 toa7-seh phaiN2-mi5 e5 bang7, Chhoa7 goa2 jip8 chit8 e5 bi2-biau7 e5 se3-kai3.Si7 tu5-khi3 tui3 chit8 e5 phaiN2-bang7 hou7 lang5 oe7 chai e5....
Pek-jim2 gim5-si liau2, A-hoa chiu7 koh soa3-chiap gim5.  In e5 siaN-im u7 khip-in2 kang2-tou e5 chiong3-lang5, chha-put-to chhin-chhiuN7 ou-soaN e5 lang5 ui5-lai5 in.
U7 choe7-choe7 lang5 tui3 hng7-hng7 lai5 hiat-chiN5 hou7 in.
Lang5 si3-soaN3 liau2-au7, A-hoa u7 pang-chan7 Pek-jim2 lai5 ti7 hit e5 si3-ui5 chhoe7 chiN5.
Chit-pai2 e5 kang-chok tek8-piat seng-kong, in sou2 tit-tioh8 e5 chiN5 chin-choe7.  Pek-jim2 chin boan2-chiok hoaN-hi2.  Nng7-lang5 chiam7-si5 ti7 chioh8-liau5 che7, liau2-au7 chiu7 saN-chhoa7 koe3 toa7-lou7, lai5 jip8 hit-keng sit8-tng5.
¡§Li7-li7, kin-a2-jit8 lan2 oe7-thang chiah8 khah ho2 e5 mih8!¡¨  Beh jip8 tiam3 e5 si5 Pek-jim2 chiu7 an2-ni kong2.  In saN-kap che7 ti7 phou2-thong in teh che7 khah lai7-bin7 e5 toh.  Pek-jim2 chiu7 kio3 su-hau7 e5 gin2-na2 lai5.  ¡§ChhiaN2 li2 chit-tng3 ka7 goan2 ke-thiN chit8-boe2 hi5 hou7 goan2.¡¨
Bo5-ku2 chiu7 phang5 sou2 beh chiah8 e5 png7-chhai3 chhut-lai5.  Pek-jim2 u7 tek8-piat e5 chap8-chhai3 png7, A-hoa u7 i e5 chhai3, koh ke-thiN chit8-boe2 hi5.
A-hoa chin hoaN-hi2, in-ui7 m7-bat khoaN3-tioh8 chit-khoan2 e5 hi5.
¡§Li7-li7, chit-boe2 hi5 si7 li2 e5 hun7!¡¨  Pek-jim2 sak-oa2 hi5 ti7 A-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.
¡§Pa-pa, li2 ia7 tioh8 saN-kap chiah8!¡¨  A-hoa koh sak kau3 tiong-ng.
¡§Pa-pa bo5 ai3 chiah8 hi5, sou2-i2 chhiaN2 li2 chiah8.¡¨  Pek-jim2 koh sak-oa2 khi3.  I e5 bin7 chin chhio3.  Chong2-si7 A-hoa kam2-kak chin khou2-sim.
¡§Pa-pa, chiah-nih8 ho2-chiah8 e5 hi5, li2 na7 bo5 chiah8 goa2 ka-ki7 chiah8 u7 sim2-mih8 ho2-chiah8?¡¨  Pek-jim2 e5 bin7 koh chhio3-chhio3, chiu7 chiong hi5 sak kau3 tiong-ng.
¡§Na7-si7 an2-ni pa-pa ia7 chiah8, chong2-si7 Li7-li7 tioh8 chiah8 hou7 khah ho2-khoaN3 leh!¡¨
In chin hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8 lai5 beh khai-si2 chiah8, khiok A-hoa hut-jian5 koh siuN7-tioh8 chit8-e5 su7.
¡§Pa-pa, lan2 beh chiah8-png7 e5 si5 ia7 bo5 ki5-to2?!  A-long5 na7 beh chiah8 ho2-chiah8 e5 mih8-kiaN7 tioh8 kam2-sia7.  Chit-boe2 hi5 ti7 lan2 si7 ho2-chiah8 e5 mih8-kiaN7, lan2 tioh8 kam2-sia7, na7 u7 kam2-sia7 Siong7-te3 chiah beh koh siuN2-su3 ti7 au7-pai2!¡¨
Pek-jim2 khai-si2 beh chiah8 e5 chhiu2 koh pang3-loh8 khi3.  ¡§Li7-li7, li2 chhoa7 pa-pa kam2-sia7 ki5-to2.¡¨  A-hoa kin2-kin2 lai5 siuN7 ki5-to2 e5 oe7, chiu7 khai-si2 aN3-thau5 lai5 kam2-sia7.  ¡§ThiN-teng2 e5 Siong7-te3, goan2 kam2-sia7 Li2 siuN2-su3 goan2 chiah8-mih8.  Goan2 ia7 kam2-sia7 Li2 hou7 goan2 chit-boe2 ho2-chiah8 e5 hi5, kho3 Ia5-sou e5 mia5, A-meh.¡¨  In chiu7 khai-si2 lai5 chiah8.  Pek-jim2 pang-chan7 A-hoa lai5 chiah8 hit-boe2 hi5, kiaN-liau2 u7 chhi3.
¡§Hi5, bah kap chhai3 long2-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 mih8, kin-chio ia7 si7 Siong7-te3 e5...  Siong7-te3 sit8-chai7 chin thiaN3 lan2, tak8-jit8 long2 hou7 lan2 u7 thang chiah8.¡¨  A-hoa ke3-siok8 kong2-oe7.
Chong2-si7 Pek-jim2 chin eng7 sim teh chi2-to7 A-hoa tioh8 lim-thng, tioh8 pe-png7, tioh8 phui3-chhi3, chhit8-chhiu2, chiong2-chiong2 e5 su7.
Chit chiong2 e5 seng-oah8 keng-ke3 bo5 ku2, A-hoa i2-keng u7 koh pian3 chit8-chiong2 e5 lang5 chhut-lai5 lah.  I pian3-chiaN5 chit8-e5 chin-sui2, chin ho2-khoaN3 e5 gin2-na2.  Koe3-khi3 hit e5 chiau-chui7, phaiN2-khoaN3 e5 iuN7-siuN3 long2 jin7 boe7 chhut-lai5.  I e5 bin7 u7 hoat-chhut kng-chhai2 oah8-khi3.

Pek-jim2 sui-jian5 ti7 bo5 chu7-iu5 e5 ou-am3 tiong, iau2-ku2 chin hoaN-hi2 lai5 khoan2-thai7 A-hoa, soe2 sin-khu, cheng2-li2 thau5-mng5, chheng7 saN, si7 ai3 hou7 A-hoa chiaN5-cho3 chit8-e5 put-chi2 kho2-ai3 kou2-chui e5 cha-bou2 gin2-na2.
U7 chit8-pai2 in teh kang-chok e5 si5, Pek-jim2 u7 thiaN-tioh8 chit8 e5 hu7-jin5 lang5 an2-ni kong2, 
¡§Chit e5 gin2-na2 chin-chiaN3 sui2, chin kho2-ai3, chhin-chhiuN7 thiN-sai3 e5 khoan2!¡¨
Hit chit8-mi5 saN-kap ki5-to2 liau2, A-hoa jip8 bin5 e5 si5 Pek-jim2 chiu7 pang-chan7 A-hoa kah phoe7, i che7 ti7 A-hoa e5 chhng5, thiaN A-hoa teh khun3 pang5-an e5 hoaN5-siaN, lai5 siuN7-tioh8 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 sou2 kong2 e5 oe7.  I chiu7 chhun-chhiu2 bong A-hoa e5 thau5-khak.  ¡§Siat-su2 goa2 na7 u7 bak8-chiu, goa2 chiu7 oe7-thang khoaN3 li2 e5 bin7!¡¨  I e5 chhiu2 chiu7 bong i e5 bin7, phiN7, bak8-chiu kap chhui3-phoe2.  ¡§Li7-li7, li2 sit8-chai7 chin kho2-ai3!  Li2 si7 goa2 e5 sio2 thiN-sai3!  Li2 si7 goa2 bang7-siong2 tiong e5 thiN-sai3!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chim i e5 thau5-hiah8.  I e5 bak8-chiu u7 bak8-sai2.
¡§Goa2 it-chhe3 e5 phaiN2-bang7 long2 soah lah!  M7-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 se3-kan e5 toa7-su7, chi2-u7 li2 e5 chhut-hian7 hou7 goa2 e5 it-chhe3 long2 toa7 pian3-oaN7.¡¨
Pek-jim2 e5 bak8-sai2 tit8-tit8 lau5-chhut.  I gim7-oa2 A-hoa e5 chhiu2 ti7 i heng5-cheng5.  I e5 bin7 ng3 ti7 thiN.
¡§Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 tioh8 kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 u7 siuN2-su3 goa2 chit e5 sio2 thiN-sai3.  Li2 chai goa2 e5 pi-chham2, goa2 e5 kou-toaN!¡¨
U7 chit8-mi5 Pek-jim2 bang7-kiN3 u7 chit8-e5 io5-na5.  Chhut-si3 bo5 ku2, iu3-eN e5 A-hoa to2 ti7 hit lai7-bin7.  Hit e5 io5-na5 ia7 si7 hoe-na5, in-ui7 u7 chin-choe7 chhau2-hoe am-moa2 A-hoa e5 sin-khu.
Chi2-u7 A-hoa e5 kha-boe2, si7 chheng7 chit8-siang peh8-sek e5 oe5..., kap ti3 chit8-teng2 chhau2 bo7-a2 e5 thau5-khak u7 khoaN3-kiN3 na7-tiaN7.

A-hoa e5 bin7 chin sui2 ti7 hit e5 am-bat8 e5 bo7-a2 e7.  I e5 bak8-chiu kheh-kheh.  Ti7 io5-na5 e5 si3-piN long2 u7 san3-moa2 e5 chhau2-hoe.
Au7-lai5 u7 chit8-e5 chheng7 ou-sek e5 le2-hok8 e5 bok8-su chhut-hian7 lai5 beh lam2 hit e5 io5-na5 khi3.  Pek-jim2 u7 mng7 bok8-su beh lam2 io5-na5 khi3 to2-ui7.  Bok8-su kong2 eN-a2 i2-keng si2-khi3, beh ti7 hoe2-lou5 lai7 sio i e5 sin-si.  Pek-jim2 toa7 kiaN-hiaN5, m7-sin3 u7 chit-e5 su7.  I chiu7 beh chhiuN2 A-hoa.  Khiok bok8-su u7 chiong Pek-jim2 oe-chau2, chiu7 chiong io5-na5 e5 sin-si he7 ti7 chit8 e5 iam7-jiat8 e5 hoe2-lou5 lai7.
Iam7-hoe2 u7 sio hit e5 io5-na5 kap lai7-bin7 e5 eN-a2 A-hoa.  I e5 thau5-khak, bo7-a2, thau5-mng5 long2 sio-loh8 khi3. 
Au7-lai5 sio i e5 kha, i e5 oe5....  Bo5 loa7-ku2 A-hoa chiu7 ti7 hit e5 iam7-hoe2 e5 lai7-bin7 siau-biat8 khi3.
Pek-jim2 khui-siaN toa7-khau3.  I chhiN2 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, hoat-hian7 i iau2 teh hau2, khiok i bo5 kim3-chi2 i e5 bak8-sai2 lai5 ke3-siok8 hau2.
I kin2-kin2 khi2-sin khi2-lai5, chau2-kau3 A-hoa e5 chhng5 lai5 bong A-hoa.  I e5 chhiu2 liah8-tioh8 A-hoa e5 chhiu2 e5 si5 i chiah pang3-sim, theng5-chi2 i e5 bak8-sai2.
I chiam7-si5 chin gong5-ngiah8, khia7 ti7 A-hoa e5 chhng5-piN.
¡§I kiam2 oe7 li7-khui goa2 khi3?!  Kiam2-chhai2 u7 i e5 chhin-lang5 beh chhoe7-tioh8 i lai5 chhoa7 i khi3.  A2-si7 hit e5 thau5-ke niu5 beh chhoe7 tioh8 i.¡¨
Pek-jim2 siuN7 kau3 chia, chiu7 m7-kaN2 koh siuN7.  I e5 sim ka-leng2-sun2 chit8-e5, in-ui7 hiah e5 su-siuN2 hou7 i e5 sim chin put-an, khoa3-lu7.
Pek-jim2 koh lau5 bak8-sai2 chhut-lai5.  I chiu7 kui7 ti7 A-hoa e5 chhng5-cheng5 lai5 khan A-hoa e5 chhiu2 lai5 hap8-oa2 ti7 i e5 siang-chhiu2 lai5 ki5-to2.
¡§Siong7-te3 ah, goa2 su-iau3 goa2 e5 thiN-sai3, si7 li2 sou2 siuN2-su3 hou7 goa2 e5..., kiu5 Li2 m7-thang koh tui3 goa2 chhiuN2-khi3 goa2 e5 thiN-sai3, chhin-chhiuN7 i2-cheng5 e5 khoan2.¡¨
Pek-jim2 e5 ki5-to2 i2-keng pian3-cho3 teh hau2 lah.  Khou2-mia7 e5 Pek-jim2, ti7 chit e5 put-heng7 e5 gin2-na2 e5 sin-chiuN7 ka7-tiau5 i e5 siN3-mia7.  I e5 bak8-sai2 moa2-lau5 ti7 i e5 bin7.
Hit chit8-me5 Pek-jim2 long2 boe7 khun3-tit.  I ti7 sim-lai7 teh siuN7 kiam2-chhai2 tioh8 chhoa7 A-hoa li7-khui chit e5 sou2-chai7, kau3 Tai5-lam5 khi3.  Si7 kiaN-liau2 chit e5 kang2-tou u7 chin-choe7 lang5 teh chhut-jip8.
Iau2-ku2 beh kau3 ti7 Tai5-lam5, chit e5 su7 hou7 Pek-jim2 e5 sin piN5-piN5 chin oh tam-tng tit.  Tai5-lam5 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim si7 chit8 e5 thang chiu3-chou2, kho2-ouN3 e5 toe7-hng.  Sim7-chi3 pok8-kek si5-tai7 ti7 Tai5-lam5 sou2 tu2-tioh8 hiah e5 kek8-ki5 pi-chham2 e5 jit8 iau2-ku2 chhin-chhiuN7 siong-hun5 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim teh thang3-thiaN3.  Sou2-i2 chit nng7 e5 i3-liam7 ti7 i e5 sim saN-kap chhiong-tut8, hoan2-hok8 bu5-siong5 teh tui-pek i.
Kau3 ti7 thiN-kng e5 si5, i iau2 boe7-thang tit-tioh8 kai2-koat.  Kiat-kiok8 in chiu7 chiau3-siong5 koh toa3 ti7 Ki-lun5.
U7 chit8-pai2 in chiau3-siong5 ti7 chui2-piN e5 chui2-gun5-teng kha teh cho3 kang e5 si5, hit-si5 tu2-tu2 A-hoa teh gim5-si.  Pek-jim2 u7 thiaN-tioh8 nng7-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 saN-kap teh chheng-chan3 A-hoa e5 gau5.
¡§Chit e5 gin2-na2 kap A-nga2 chin sio-siang5.  Hit e5 bak8-chiu, chhui3, thau5-mng5 long2 oan5-choan5 siang5-khoan2!¡¨  U7 chit8-e5 an2-ni kong2.
¡§U7-iaN2 to tioh8, kiam2-chhai2 si7 A-nga2 e5 chhin-lang5!¡¨  Koh leng7-goa7 chit8-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 an2-ni soa3-chiap.  Chong2-si7 chiah-e5 oe7 jip8 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim e5 si5, i peng5-cheng7 e5 sim chiu7 khi2 toa7 hong-eng2 khi2-lai5.  I e5 chhiu2 ia7 m7-chai-iaN2 si7 teh oe sim2-mih8, i e5 sim chhiong-moa2 tioh8 put-an.
Sou2-i2 kau3 A-hoa gim5-si liau2, chiu7 kin2-kin2 lai5 li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7.
Koe3-jit8 Pek-jim2 chiu7 bo5 chhut-lai5 kang-chok lah.  Hit e5 lau5-teng2 bo5-liau5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 u7 hoat-hian7 tioh8 Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa si3, gou7-jit8 bo5 koh chhut-lai5 ti7 chui2-piN cho3-kang.  I phah-sng3 in si7 phoa3-piN7, a2-si7 chhut-goa7 khi3.
Ko2-jian5 tui3 an2-ni liau2-au7 lan2 long2 boe7-thang koh ti7 Ki-lun5 e5 lou7-piN chhoe7-tioh8 Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa.
Han5-leng2, ta-so3 e5 koaN5-thiN i2-keng koe3-liau2 lah.  ThiN-toe7 chiam7-chiam7 choan2-jip8 ti7 oah8-mia7 hoan3-loan7 e5 chhun-thiN lah.  To3-chhu3 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 hoaN-hi2 kap khoai3-lok8 chhiong-moa2.  Lek8-sek e5 tai7-toe7 moa2-moa2 u7 seng e5 kou2-tong7 kap hoan-hou.  Chhiu7-bak8 chhau2-hoe long2 koh hok8-oah8.  ThiN-teng2 e5 pah-chiau2 ia7 long2 tng2-lai5 lah.  Lang5-lang5 e5 bin7 hoan2-chio3 chhun-thiN e5 kng-liang7 kap oah8-khi3.
Chit e5 si5 lan2 beh chhoe7-tioh8 Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa ti7 pah-hoe e5 soaN-nia2 Pak-tau5.  In nng7-lang5 saN khan-chhiu2 ti7 Pak-tau5 e5 ke-lou7 teh kiaN5-iu5.
Pek-jim2 long2 theng5-chi2 in e5 kang-chok, bo5 ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 lou7-bin7.  Koh iah8 chin7-liong7 siam2-pi7 khah choe7 lang5 teh chhut-jip8 e5 sou2-chai7.
Chhin-chhiuN7 kong-hng5, chhia-cham7, teng2-teng2.
In e5 si5-kan long2 si7 ti7 sek-lai7, a2-si7 ti7 khah an-cheng7 e5 au7-soaN.
Pek-jim2 in sou2 toa3 e5 lu2-koan2 e5 au7-bin7 u7 chit8-e5 khoah-toa7 koh sui2 e5 au7 tiaN5.  Tui3 chit e5 au7-tiaN5 oe7-thang khoaN3-kiN3 chin-hng7 soaN-ia2 e5 kong-keng2.  Ti7 hia ia7 u7 chin sui2 e5 chhiu7-bak8, hoe-chhau2 moa2-moa2 si7.  A-hoa chin ai3 chit e5 sou2-chai7, sou2-i2 cha2-am3 in nng7-lang5 siong5-siong5 chhoa7 kau3 chit e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 thit-tho5, iu5-siuN2 soaN-keng2 e5 bi2-sek.  Kiok-hoe i2-keng sia7 liau2 lah.  Moe5-hoe kap tho5-hoe khui-moa2 soaN-phiaN5 soaN-nia2.  Chhau2-hoe ia7 long2 che5-che5 teh giah8-thau5 hong3-chhai2 lah.

Ti7 chhiu7-teng2 u7 pah-chiau2 e5 siaN-im teh hou7 chit8 e5 chhun-thiN e5 bi2-biau7 ke-thiN eng5-iau7, nau7-jiat8.
¡§Chhun-thiN koh tng2-lai5 lah!  ThiN-toe7 u7 hoaN-hi2 e5 hoan-hou!  U7 oah8-mia7 e5 hoan2-lan7!¡¨
Pek-jim2 e5 sim ia7 tit-tioh8 chin toa7 e5 kek-tong7.  I sui-jian5 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 sim2-mih8, chong2-si7 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7 chhiong-moa2 tioh8 chhun-thiN e5 kng-beng5 oah8-khi3.
In keng-koe3 chit e5 moe5-hoe hng5 lai5 kau3 chit8-e5 chhiN-chhui3 e5 chhau2-pou, chiu7 saN-kap che7 ti7 hit-e5 un-loan2 e5 chhau2-teng2.  A-hoa khoaN3-tioh8 chit8-kun5 e5 hoe, chiu7 chau2-loh8 e7-bin7 e5 soaN-phiaN5 lai5 beh ban2-hoe.  ¡§Pa-pa, hia u7 chin-choe7 chin sui2 e5 hoe!!¡¨  Pek-jim2 u7 kio3 A-hoa tioh8 m7-thang khi3 siuN7 hng7, chong2-si7 A-hoa kam2-than3 bo5 soah teh soat-beng5 hoe e5 sui2, kap soaN-keng2 e5 bi2-biau7.
Au7-lai5 A-hoa ko2-jian5 u7 ban2 chit8 toa7-pe2 e5 hoe tng2-lai5.
¡§Pa-pa, li2 khoaN3 chiah-nih8 kah sui2 e5 hoe!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chhun-chhiu2 lai5 bong-hoe, koh phiN7 hoe e5 bi7.  ¡§U7-iaN2, chin sui2, chin phang e5 hoe!¡¨
¡§Chiah e5 hoe, goa2 beh sang3 pa-pa!¡¨  A-hoa an2-ni kong2.  Pek-jim2 chiu7 chiap hiah e5 hoe.
¡§Li7-li7, chin to-sia7!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chiu7 chiap8-chiap8 lai5 phiN7 hoe.  A-hoa ti7 i e5 sim-piN teh khai-si2 thit-tho5 pat8-mih8 su7.  In nng7-lang5 e5 sim long2 chin hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.
Hut-jian5 A-hoa u7 hoat-chhut ki5-koai3 e5 chhio3-siaN chhut-lai5.  ¡§Li7-li7, li2 teh chhio3 sim2-mih8?!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chiu7 mng7 i.  ¡§Pa-pa, li2 e5 thau5-khak u7 chhah sim2-mih8 li2 kiam2-chai?¡¨  A-hoa ke3-siok8 teh chhio3.  Pek-jim2 chhun-chhiu2 bong-tioh8 u7 chit8-lui2 hoe chhah ti7 thau5-khak.  ¡§Li7-li7, li2 ia7 oe7 chok-giat8!¡¨  Pek-jim2 ia7 chin hoaN-hi2.

¡§Pa-pa, li2 liah8 goa2 boe7-tioh8!¡¨  A-hoa u7 chau2 li7-khui Pek-jim2.  ¡§Pa-pa, chhiaN2 li2 liah8 goa2 khoaN3 oe7-tioh8 a2-boe7?¡¨
¡§Ho2, na7 liah8-tioh8 li2 chiu7 ai3 gim5-si.¡¨  Pek-jim2 chiu7 khi2-sin beh lai5 liah8 A-hoa.  A-hoa chin hoaN-hi2, chiu7 gi-gi chhio3 lai5 chau2.  Pek-jim2 siang-chhiu2 khui-khui lai5 beh liah8 A-hoa.
Ti7 hia choan2-seh bo5-ku2 Pek-jim2 soa3 tak-tioh8 mih8-kiaN7 lai5 poah8-to2 ti7 thou5-bin7.  ¡§Ah!¡¨  I e5 sin-khu u7 ko7 tui3 hit e5 soaN-pheN5 lok8-khi3, kau3 e7-bin7 e5 chhau2-pou.  A-hoa khoaN3-kiN3 Pek-jim2 tak-to2, koh lin3-loh8 e7-bin7, soa3 long2 boe7 tin2-tang7, chiu7 bin7 pian3-sek kiaN-hiaN5, kin2-kin2 chau2-kau3 Pek-jim2 e5 sou2-chai7 lai5 beh lam2 Pek-jim2 khi2-lai5.
¡§Pa-pa!  Pa-pa!  Pa-pa!¡¨  A-hoa i2-keng kiaN kau3 soa3 lau5 bak8-sai2 lah.  Chong2-si7 Pek-jim2 hut-jian5 chhio3 chhut-lai5, chiu7 khi2-lai5 pho7 A-hoa ti7 i e5 heng-cheng5.
¡§Li7-li7, pa-pa bo5 an2-choaN2 lah, li2 m7-bian2 kiaN!¡¨  Pek-jim2 chhio3 bo5-soat.
¡§Pa-pa, Pa-pa!¡¨  A-hoa chiu7 eng7 i e5 chhiu2 lai5 bong Pek-jim2 e5 bin7, chhin-chhiuN7 ai3 beh khak-sit8 i bo5 an2-choaN2 e5 khoan2.  Au7-lai5 in saN-kap lam2-oa2 lai5 khui-siaN toa7-chhio3.  Khiok in e5 bak8-chiu long2 u7 bak8-sai2.
In e5 heng7-hok thang kong2 si7 kau3 ti7 choat8-teng2.  Ti7 in tiong-kan sou2-u7 e5 thiaN3-sim si7 siok8 thiN e5 thiaN3, si7 han2-tit u7 lang5 oe7-thang keng-giam7 tioh8, oe7-thang li2-kai2 e5 thiaN3.  Ti7 chit e5 thiaN3 e5 lai7-bin7 Pek-jim2 u7 kam2-kak i si7 se3-kai3 siong7 choe7 heng7-hok e5 lang5.  Khiok i ia7 khak-sit8 i e5 se3-kai3 long2 oan5-choan5 pian3-oaN7 lah.  Chit e5 se3-kai3 ia7 thang kio3-cho3 thiaN3 e5 se3-kai3.  ThiaN3 i2-goa7 ti7 i e5 lai7-bin7 long2 boe7-thang chhoe7-tioh8 pat8-hang7 mih8.
9 TUI3 THIN-TENG2 LAI5 E5 SIAN-IM
Tui3 Pek-jim2, Tam5-chui2 choan2-seh8 kau3 Tang-pou7 iok-liok8 u7 nng7-geh8-jit8 ku2, kau3 ti7 lak8-geh8 chhe, he7-thiN pek-kin7, lang5-lang5 long2 lou7-chhut peh8-sek e5 kan2-i chhiu2 giah8 jit8-soaN3 e5 si5, hit e5 lau5-teng2 bo5-liau5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, u7 chit8-jit8 hut-jian5 koh khoaN3-kiN3 Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa koh chhut-lian7 ti7 Ki-lun5, goan5-lai5 hit e5 teng-kha teh cho3-kang.
A-hoa u7 pian3 chin ho2-khoaN3, chin kou2-chui e5 lak8-hoe3 gin2-na2 lah.  I e5 bin7, bak8-chiu long2 u7 hi2-lok8 e5 kng-chhai2 hoat-chhut.  I e5 sin-the2 ia7 hian2-beng5 iu-siu3 e5 hoat-iok8.  I u7 chheng7 chit8-nia2 lek8-sek bo5 chhiu2-ng2 e5 kan2-i.  Ou-kim-kim e5 thau5-mng5 chin-tng5, soe5 kau3 ti7 keng-thau5.  Na7-si7 Pek-jim2 ia7 u7 chin-toa7 e5 pian3-oaN7 lah.  Ku2-ku2 sou2 tiN5-tiau5 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7 hit e5 kou-toaN, iu-chhiu5 e5 iaN2, taN long2 bo5 khi3 lah.  I choan-sin long2 si7 peh8-sek.  Chhau2-bo7-a2, hun-saN, e7-hok8, oe5 long2 hou7 lang5 oe7 kam2-kak to2-kok he7-thiN e5 hong-cheng5.  I e5 bin7 u7 ng3-bang7 kap hoaN-hi2 chin-toa7.
U7 khoaN3-kiN3 in e5 lang5 e5 sim beh chit e5 sio-siang5 e5 in3-siong7, chiu7-si7, ¡§Heng7-hok, khoai3-lok8 e5 pe7-kiaN2!¡¨
Pek-jim2 kiat-kiok8 u7 chhoa7 A-hoa koh tng2-lai5 Ki-lun5, in cha2 sou2-toa3 e5 sou2-chai7.  Ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim-lai7 hit e5 put-an ia7 chiam7-chiam7 siau-bo5 khi3 lah.  In ke3-siok8 ti7 hit e5 toe7-tiam2 cho3-kang.
U7 chit8-jit8 in cho3-kang liau2, ti7 ke-lou7 teh kiaN5-iu5 e5 si5, u7 tu2-tioh8 chit8-tai5 Ki-tok-kau3 pou3-to7-hoe7 e5 soan-thoan5 chhia.  Hit tiuN chhia e5 kong2-seng-ki bo5-si5-theng5 teh chio-hou chhi7-bin5 tioh8 khi3 hu3 pou3-to7-hoe7.  Pek-jim2 chiu7 theng5-kha lai5 beh thiaN hit e5 siong5-se3.
¡§Chhin-ai3 e5 kok-ui7 hiaN-che2, goan2 si7 pun2-chhi7 ¡Ñ ¡Ñ Ki-tok kau3-hoe7 pou3-to7-hoe7 e5 soan-thoan5-tui7, ai3 beh hiong3 kok-ui7 po3 chit8 e5 ho2 siau7-sit.  Chiu7-si7 tui3 kim-mi5 peh tiam2 khi2 u7 Bi2-kok chhut-mia5 e5 pou3-to7-ka ¡Ñ ¡Ñ bok8-su beh ti7 pun2 kau3-hoe7 pou3-to7 saN-mi5.  ChhiaN2 kok-ui7 m7-thang sit-loh8 chit e5 ho2 e5 ki-hoe7 lai5 
khi3 chham-ka.  Ia5-sou kong2, kiN3-na7 lo5-khou2 tioh8-boa5 poe7 tang7-taN3 e5 tioh8 lai5 chiu7-kun7 goa2, goa2 beh ho7 li2 tit-tioh8 an-hioh.  Koh kong2, Goa2 si7 lou7, si7 chin-li2, si7 oah8-mia7, sou2-i2 kiN3-na7 sim-lai7 bo5 peng5-an e5 lang5, chhoe7 bo5 oah8-mia7 kap chin-li2 e5 lang5, chhiaN2 lin2 long2 tioh8 lai5 thiaN, Ia5-sou beh hou7 lin2 peng5-an, oah8-mia7, chin-li2.¡¨  Soan-thoan5 chhia chiam7-chiam7 hng7-khi3, i e5 siaN ia7 bo5 thiaN-kiN3 lah.
Hiah e5 oe7 khak-sit8 liah8-tioh8 Pek-jim2 e5 sim.
¡§Li7-li7, lan2 kim-me5-hng lai5 khi3 thiaN to7-li2, li2 u7 ai3 khi3 bo5?¡¨  I na2 liam7 e5 khoan2 lai5 mng7 an2-ni.  ¡§Pa-pa, goa2 chin ai3!¡¨  Na7-si7 A-hoa toa7 hoaN-hi2.
Chiah8 am3-tng3 liau2-au7, pun2-lai5 in saN-chhoa7 beh khi3 le2-pai3-tng5, chong2-si7 ti7 poaN3-lou7 Pek-jim2 hut-jian5 koh choan2 hong-hiong3, chhoa7 A-hoa koh tng2-lai5 lu2-koan2.  A-hoa e5 sim u7 tam7-poh8 ki5-koai3.
Chong2-si7 kau3 ti7 pang5-keng Pek-jim2 u7 ka7 A-hoa soe2 kha-chhiu2, soa3 oaN7-saN, hit-si5 A-hoa e5 hoaN-hi2 koh to3-tng2 lai5.  Pek-jim2 ia7 jip8 ek8-keng, koh soa3 oaN7 saN-khou3, liau2-au7 in chiah koh khai-si2 chhut-hoat.
Kau3 pai3-tng5 e5 si5 chu7-hoe7 i2-keng teh khai-si2 lah.  U7 chin chong3-giam5 e5 si-koa tui3 lai7-bin7 teh lau5 chhut-lai5, ti3-kau3 hou7 Pek-jim2 thiaN-tioh8 e5 si5 soa3 m7-kaN2 jip8-khi3.  I thoat i e5 bo7-a2, aN3-thau5 lai5 khia7 ti7 hng7-hng7 e5 mng5-khau2.  Ti7 i e5 sim u7 chin-choe7 kong2 boe7 chhut-lai5 e5 toa7-khui3.
Chong2-si7 sui5-si5 u7 an3-lai7 e5 lang5 chhut-lai5 kau3 in e5 bin7-cheng5 beh chhoa7 in jip8 lai7-bin7 khi3.
¡§Goan2 tiam3 chia tioh8 ho2!¡¨  Pek-jim2 kheh-khi3 khiok hit-ui7 sin3-tou5 u7 jiat8-khun2 lai5 chhiaN2 in tioh8 jip8-khi3.  Pek-jim2 toe3 i tah8-jip8 pai3-tng5-lai7 e5 si5 gim5-si e5 siaN it-hoat hiang2-liang7 lai5 pau-ui5 in.  I kam2-kak si7 jip8 ti7 thian-kai3 e5 keng2-lai7.  A-hoa u7 khiN5-oa2 ti7 Pek-jim2, lai5 chin3-cheng5 kau3 ti7 thau5-cheng5-bin7 e5 ui7 khi3.  Hiah e5 gim5-si e5 siaN-im chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-eng2, hoa-hoa hau2.  I kiong-kiong keng3-keng3 kau3 ti7 lai5 khia7 ti7 cheng3-lang5 e5 tiong-kan, tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 khia7 ti7 po2-cho7 kap cheng3 thiN-sai3, seng3-tou5 e5 bin7-cheng5 chit8-iuN7.
I long2 m7-kaN2 tin2-tang7, chhiu2 ia7 m7-kaN2 bong tioh8 i2.  In-ui7 i kam2-kak lai7-bin7 e5 it-chhe3 long2 si7 seng3-kiat, chun-kui3.
Gim5-si liau2 bok8-su u7 kong2 beh saN-kap ki5-to2, Pek-jim2 thiaN-tioh8 chit-ku3 oe7, siuN7 kong2 i tioh8 kui7 loh8-khi3, i beh kui7 loh8-khi3 e5 si5 piN-thau5 e5 chit8-ui7 hiaN-ti7 u7 tui3 i kong2 m7-bian2 an2-ni choe3.  Ti7 ki5-to2 e5 tiong-kan i kam2-kak chin ngong5-gniah, chin bo5 chu7-jian5.  Ki5-to2 liau2, che7 ho2-se3 e5 si5, ke3-siok8 u7 thak8 Seng3-keng Iok-han7 saN-chiuN chap8-lak8 chat.  Liau2-au7 u7 gim5-si-pan e5 hian3-si, u7 koh ki5-to2, jian5-au7 chiu7 u7 chit8-ui7 leng7-goa7 e5 bok8-su khi2-lai5 khai-si2 kang2-to7.
A-hoa tit8-tit8 khiN5 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sin-khu, m7-kaN2 pang3-li7 i.  I e5 bak8-chiu chu3-sin5 khoaN3 tai5-teng2 e5 lang5, au7-lai5 chiah khoaN3 si3-ui5 e5 cheng5-lang5 koh chiam7-chiam7 soa2-bak8 lai5 khoaN3 hiah e5 teh chau2-chong5 e5 hu7-chek-jin5.  Na7-si7 Pek-jim2, chi2-u7 aN3-thau5 lai5 tui3 siaN-im teh chhat-giam7 lai7-bin7 e5 chong7-hong2.
Bok8-su khui-siaN kang2-to7 e5 si5, lang5-lang5 e5 sim long2 chu3-sin5 ti7 i e5 oe7.  I chhou-toa7 e5 siaN-im chin-beng5, ku3-ku3 long2 jip8 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 sim.
¡§In-ui7 Siong7-te3 chiong tok8-siN e5 KiaN2 siuN2-su3 se3-kan, hou7 kiN3-na7 sin3 I e5 lang5 boe7 tim5-lun5, oe7 tit-tioh8 eng2-oah8; I thiaN3 se3-kan kau3 an2-ni.¡¨
¡§Goa2 beh tai7-seng tui3 chit-chat e5 lai7-bin7 e5 oe7 ¡¥Siong7-te3¡¦ lai5 soat-beng5.¡¨
¡§Siong7-te3 chiu7-si7 chhong3-cho7 e5 chu2-chaiN2.  Se3-kan e5 ban7-mih8 long2 si7 tui3 I lai5 cho7-chiaN5 e5.  I si7 choan5 u2-tiu7 e5 i5-it chu2-lang5, ban7-mih8 long2 si7 siok8 ti7 I e5 sou2-iu2.  I eng7 toa7 koan5-leng5 e5 khui3-lat8 lai5 tui3 bo5 chhong3-cho7 ban7-u7, koh tui3 I e5 ti3-hui7 lai5 cho3-chiaN5 long2-chong2 e5 tiat8-su5 kui-lut8.  Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 e5 kiat-chok chiu7-si7 ¡¥lang5¡¦.  Lang5 si7 chiau3 Siong7-te3 e5 siong7 lai5 chhong3-cho7 e5.  In-ui7 chhong3-cho7 long2-chong2 e5 bok8-tek si7 ti7 lang5, chhong3-cho7 e5 tiong-sim si7 ti7 lang5.  In-ui7 lang5 si7 
beh lai5 tai7-piau2 Siong7-te3, si7 beh lai5 eng5-iau7 Siong7-te3.  Siong7-te3 chiong ban7-mih8 su3 hou7 lang5, ui7-tioh8 lang5 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 ban7-mih8.  In-ui7 Siong7-te3 ai3 lang5 kap I kau-poe5, keng3-pai3 I, o-lo2 I, kam2-sia7 I, eng5-iau7 I.  Ti7 ban7-mih8 e5 tiong-kan bo5 u7 pat8 e5 pi7-cho7-mih8 kap lang5 sio-siang5, u7 Siong7-te3 long2-chong2 e5 tek-seng3 kap u7 chit8-chiong2 tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 heng5-thong.  Tu5-khi3 lang5 bo5 pat8-mih8 oe7-hiau2 o-lo2, keng3-pai3, kam2-sia7.¡¨
¡§Lang5 e5 li2-te3, to7-tek-seng3, ge7-sut8-seng3 long2 si7 tui3 Siong7-te3 e5 heng5-siong7 sou2 seng5-chiap lai5 e5....¡¨
¡§Koe3-khi3 beh kong2 ¡¥se3-kan¡¦¡¨
¡§Chit e5 se3-kan goan5-lai5 si7 chit8 e5 lok8-hng5.  Ti7 chit e5 se3-kan tak8-hang7 long2 si7 chin bi2-moa2, khoai3-lok8.  U7 un5-chong5 Siong7-te3 e5 toa7 koan5-leng5 kap ban7 pu3-u7.  Lang5-lang5 long2 oe7 thang ti7 chit e5 se3-kan lai5 hiong2-siu7 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 e5 bi2-biau7.  Khiok choe7-ok chin3-jip8 se3-kan i2-lai5, chit e5 khoai3-lok8, peng5-an e5 lok8-hng5 soa3 chiaN5-choe3 ou-am3, thong3-khou2 e5 toe7-gek8, Chhu2-chhu2 u7 pai7-hoai7, si2-hiat e5 siong-jiah.  Ti7 chit se3-kan bo5 koh u7 oah8-mia7 e5 ng3-bang7, ia7 bo5 u7 chin-li2 e5 kng, si7 in-ui7 chit e5 se3-kan tui3 poe7-gek8 Siong7-te3 liau2-au7 chiu7 li7-khui Siong7-te3 e5 koan2-kai3 lah.  Se3-kan bo5-khi3 Siong7-te3, chiu7 ka-ki7 cho3-seng5 i e5 siong7-te3, liah8 ban7-mih8 cho3 i e5 siong7-te3, lai5 ke-thiN i e5 choe7-ok kap gu5-gong7.
Bo5-khi3 Siong7-te3 liau2, chit e5 se3-kan long2 chhiong-moa2 put-heng7 kap pi-chham2.  Ti7 chit e5 choe7-ok pai7-hoai7 e5 se3-kan sou2 u7 e5 mia7-un7, chiu7-si7 si2-hiat na7-tiaN7.¡¨
¡§Goa2 beh koh kong2 ¡¥Lang5¡¦.¡¨
¡§Lang5 si7 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 ban7-mih8 e5 tiong-sim bok8-tek.  Lang5 u7 toa3 tioh8 Siong7-te3 eng5-iau7 e5 siong7.  So2-i2 lang5 u7 tek8-piat e5 chek-jim7.
Lang5 tioh8 keng3-pai3, o-lo2, eng5-kng Siong7-te3.

In-ui7 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 lang5 si7 beh tai7-piua2 I.  Koh Siong7-te3 ai3 lang5 kap I tang5-sim, chhin-chhiuN7 I e5 khoan2-sit, soa3 hok8-chiong5 I.
Khiok lang5 chiong Siong7-te3 chiah e5 un-su3, lai5 pian3-oaN7 choe3 ka-ki7 e5 eng5-iau7, soa3 poe7-poan7 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3.  Lang5 chhin-chhiuN7 iuN5 kiaN5 be5-lou7, tek8-lang5 kiaN5 ka-ki7 e5 phian-lou7, ki3-jian5 song3-sit liong5-sim, chiu7 hong3-chhiong3 su-iok8 ti7 tak8-iuN7 e5 phaiN2-tai7, seng-seng si7 ka-ki7 chhu2 sun2-phoaN3 ti7 biat8-bong5 e5 sou2-chai7.¡¨
¡§Choe7-jin5, che si7 lang5 tui3 tui7-loh8 liau2-au7 e5 leng7-goa7 chit8-e5 beng5-chheng.
Siong7-te3 bo5 teng7 pat8 e5 pi7-chhong3-cho7 mih8 e5 choe7, in-ui7 in m7-bat poe7-poan7, ia7 bo5 u7 toa3-tioh8 Siong7-te3 tek8-piat e5 su2-beng7.
Chi2-u7 lang5 si7 choe7-jin5, in-ui7 lang5 u7 phoa3-hai7 Siong7-te3 long2-chong2 e5 ke3-ek8, u7 pai7-hoai7 chit e5 lok8-hng5.  Choe7-ok e5 kang-chiN5 chiu7-si7 si2.  Lang5 e5 kiat-kiok8 chiu7 si7 biat-bong5, si2-sit.  (Chham-kho2 Lo5-ma2 jin5-su, 1 chiuN kau3 3 chiuN.)¡¨
¡§Lang5 ti7 chit e5 si2 e5 mia7-un7 e5 e7-bin7 chhoe7 bo5 oah8-mia7, chin-li2, lai5 put-an, choat8-bang7.¡¨
¡§Goa2 beh koh lai5 kong2 ¡¥tok-siN KiaN2¡¦.¡¨
¡§Sui-jian5 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 e5 tai7-ke3 u7 tu2-tioh8 chiat8-chih8, I e5 chi2-i3 u7 siu7 poe7-poan7, lang5 kap se3-kai3 u7 ka-ki7 chhu2 biat8-bong5, pai7-hoai7 e5 lou7, khiok Siong7-te3 m7-kam I e5 sou2 thiaN3 e5 lang5 tim5-lun5, a2-si7 I sou2 chhong3-cho7 e5 se3-kan lai5 biat8-bong5.¡¨
I iau2 ng3-bang7 u7 sim2-mih8 pan7-hoat thang ban2-hoe5, thang kiu3-siok8, hou7 I e5 chhong3-cho7 m7-bian2 tu2-tioh8 leng5-jiok8, phoa3-hai7.  Sou2-i2 I u7 chiong sim-hoai5 tiong e5 tok8-siN KiaN2 chhe-khian2 kau3 se3-kan, lai5 khui chit tiau5 kiu3-siok8 e5 lou7.  Chiu7-si7 hou7 
kiN3-na7 sin3 I e5 lang5, oe7-thang thoat-li7 chit e5 biat8-bong5 lai5 koh seng-chiap eng2-oah8 e5 kok.  Ui7-tioh8 an2-ni tok8-siN KiaN2 Ia5-sou u7 ng3 tak8-lang5 teh au5-kio3, lin2 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2 to3-tng2 lai5 kui-ng3 Siong7-te3.  Siong7-te3 ti7 I e5 koh u7 koh siat-hoat, kian3-ti3 chit8 e5 kok-tou7 beh hou7 kiN3-na7 sin3 KiaN2 e5 lang5 thang ti7 hia ke3-siok8 hiong2-siu7 chhong3-cho7 e5 khoai3-lok8, lai5 oan5-seng5 chhong3-cho7 e5 tai7-ke3.  Chi2-u7 sin3 KiaN2 e5 lang5 oe7-thang thoat-li7 chit se3-tai7 e5 biat8-bong5 lai5 jip8 hit e5 sou2-chai7.  Beh jip8 hit e5 sin kok-tou7 e5 hoat-tou7 chin kan2-tan, chiu7-si7 sin3 tok8-siN KiaN2 kap I sou2 kong2 long2-chong2 e5 oe7, sou2 kian3-cheng3 long2-chong2 e5 su7, sou2 eng3-un2 long2-chong2 e5 tai7-chi3.  Siong7-te3 bo5 beh koh tui3 lang5 iau-kiu5 sim2-mih8 tek-heng7, a2-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 kui-lut8(³W«ß¡^, chi2-u7 na7 sin3 I, chiu7 peh8-peh8 thang tit-tioh8 hun-piat, kap kiu3-siok8 e5 un-tian2.  Chit e5 sin3 ia7 si7 li2 hian7-chai7 sui5-si5 oe7-thang ti7 li2 e5 sim-lai7 lai5 koat-teng7 e5....¡¨
¡§Koh lai5 goa2 beh kong2, ¡¥I thiaN3 se3-kan kau3 an2-ni¡¦.¡¨
¡§Siong7-te3 eng2-oan2 e5 chi2-i3 ti7 chiit e5 se3-kan u7 sit-pai7, khiok ti7 hit e5 sin-thiN sin-toe7 beh tit-tioh8 tat8-seng5.  Kiu3-siok8 e5 lang5 beh ti7 hia, in-ui7 hiong2-siu7 e5 khoai3-lok8 lai5 toa7 chheng-chan3 tok8-it cho7-hoa3 e5 Chu2-chaiN2.  Hit e5 ong5-kok beh kio3-cho3 thiaN3.
In-ui7 Siong7-te3 si7 thiaN3, koh chhiat-chhiat su-iau3 thiaN3 e5....
