In-ui7 chi2-u7 ti7 chit e5 thiaN3 e5 lai7-bin7 chiah u7 chin-sit8 e5 heng7-hok kap khoai3-lok8.¡¨
¡§Hit e5 thiaN3 e5 ong5-kok si7 lan2 se3-kan lang5 tioh8 chhiat-chhiat him-bou7 e5..., in-ui7 chit e5 se3-kan i2-keng bo5 u7 chin-sit8 e5 oah8-mia7, moa2-moa2 si7 toa3 tioh8 si2-hiat, pai7-hoai7 e5 siong-hun5.  Ti7 chia u7 put-heng7 khou2-thang3 pi-chham2.  Siat-su2 na7 u7 thang kio3-choe3 heng7-hok, hit e5 si7 hu-ke2 koh si7 chiam7-si5, ngou2-jian5 e5 na7-tiaN7.¡¨
¡§Se3-kan lang5 ah, lin2 tioh8 ng3-bang7, tioh8 lai5 sin3 tok8-siN KiaN2 Ia5-sou!¡¨

¡§Sin3 Ia5-sou si7 beh kau3 hit e5 ong5-kok i5-it e5 lou7.¡¨  Bok8-su u7 ke3-siok8 eng7 chin jiat8-cheng5 teh kong2, khiok Pek-jim2 i2-keng chin beng5-pek8 lah.  Hiah e5 oe7 tu2-tu2 si7 chit8-ki so2-si5 lai5 khui ti7 i sin-chiuN7 sou2 tu2-tioh8 hiah e5 put-heng7 e5 keng2-gu7.
Hiah e5 oe7 chhin-chhiuN7 kng2-le5 hong, tit8-tit8 kng2 seh8 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7, hou7 i ti3-kau3 long2 bo5 koh thiaN-kiN3 i2-au7 e5 oe7.  I chhin-chhiuN7 ka-ki7 chin3-jip8 ti7 hit e5 eng5-kng e5 ong5-kok lai5 the2-giam7 tioh8 hit e5 thiaN3 sou2 u7 long2-chong2 ki5-biau7 e5 heng7-hok chit8-iuN7.  I e5 chhiu2 u7 khan-oa2 A-hoa ti7 i e5 sin-piN, u7-si5 eng7 i e5 e7-hoai5 lai5 so-seh8 A-hoa e5 thau5-mng5.  I kam2-kak chin boan2-chiok, chin heng7-hok.  Khiok hut-jian5 bok8-su u7 eng7 chin kiong5-toa7 e5 siaN, ng3 tui3 Pek-jim2 e5 hong-hiong3 lai5.
¡§Se3-kan lang5 ah, lin2 e5 heng7-hok, lin2 e5 khoai3-lok8 long2 si7 hu-ki2, hit e5 si7 chiam7-si5, ngou2-jian5 e5 chho3-kak na7-tiaN7, lin2 e5 heng7-hok, lin2 e5 khoai3-lok8 tek-khak oe7 cham2-tng7.  Lin2 tham-loan5 chit e5 biat8-bong5 e5 se3-kan beh kau3 sim2-mih8 si5?!  Tui3 se3-kan toa3-tioh8 si2-hiat e5 mia7-un7 i2-lai5, kiN3-na7 khi2-cho7 heng7-hok e5 toe7-ki ti7 i e5 teng2-bin7 e5, bo5 lang5 oe7 thang thoat-li7 i e5 oah8-tauh, chiu7-si7 choat8-bang7, oan3-than3 e5 oah8-tauh!  ¡§Lin2 e5 heng7-hok, lin2 e5 khoai3-lok8 tek-khak oe7 cham2-tng7!
Chiah e5 oe7 u7 chhiok-tong7 Pek-jim2 chin-toa7.
I e5 bin7 khai-si2 hian2-chhut toa7 io5-tang7 kap chhiN-chhin3.
¡§Lin2 e5 heng7-hok, lin2 e5 khoai3-lok8 tek-khak oe7 cham2-tng7!¡¨  Chit ku3 oe7 si7 chin-li2, khiok chit e5 chin-li2 si7 hou7 Pek-jim2 sou2 jim2-siu7 boe7 tiau5 e5, in-ui7 i beng5-pek8 i e5 oah8-mia7 oa2-kho3 ti7 i e5 heng7-hok.  I chhin-chhiuN7 koh ham7-loh8 ti7 ou-am3 sit-bang7 e5 chhim-khiN lai5 iu-bun7 kat-bak8.
Bok8-su u7 ke3-siok8 teh tui-pek8 lang5 tioh8 hoan2-hoe2 lai5 sin3 Ia5-sou, koh u7 chhiaN2 hiah e5 hoaN-hi2 chiap-siu7 e5 lang5 kiaN5 kau3 tai5-cheng5 lai5.
Hoe7-tiuN5 chiu7 khai-si2 nau7-tong7 lah.  U7 lang5 teh kiaN5-kau3 tai5-cheng5, u7 Seng3-koh-tui7 teh gim5-si, u7 hiah e5 hu7-chek e5 hiaN-che2 teh pang-chan7 lang5 ho2-taN2 chhut-lah.
Pek-jim2 e5 sim-su chin tim5-bun7, hun-loan7.  Kau3-boe2 soa3 kam2-kak gong5-ngiah8 seh8-sin5.  I chiu7 toe3 hiah e5 khi2-sin beh thoe3-tiuN5 e5 lang5 lai5 kin2-kin2 li7-khui hit e5 sou2-chai7, chhut-lai5 goa7-bin7.
I e5 sim kam2-kak chin bo5 peng5-an.
¡§Pa-pa, lan2 an2-choaN2 bo5 kau3 ti7 tai5-cheng5 khi3, lan2 kiam2 m7-si7 sin3 Ia5-sou e5 lang5 mah?¡¨  Hit chit8-mi5 tng2-lai5 ti7 lu2-koan2, beh to2-chhng5 e5 si5 A-hoa chiah khui-chhui3 lai5 an2-ni mng7 i.
Pek-jim2 long2 bo5 in3-tap sim2-mih8, chi2-u7 theng5-chi2 i e5 tong7-chok lai5 che7-tiam7 ti7 chhng5-teng2.
¡§Li7-li7, chhiaN2 li2 kin2-khun3, bin5-na2-jit8 chiah lai5 kong2, an-bin5!¡¨  Pek-jim2 kong2 an2-ni lai5 beh to5-chau2 A-hoa e5 chit-mng7.
¡§Goa2 si7 chit8-e5 eng2-oan2 e5 lok8-ngou2-chia2 mah?¡¨  I pho7 i e5 thau5-khak lai5 ka-ki7 hoan2-bun7.
Pek-jim2 kau3 chin-am3 long2 khun3 boe7 loh8-bin5.  U7 chit8-e5 ap-pek e5 khui3-lat8 ta3-oa2 ti7 i e5 sim.  Bok8-su e5 oe7, A-hoa e5 bin7, i2-kip8 koe3-khi3 long2-chong2 e5 cheng5-heng5 long2 koh khai-si2 chio3-iaN2 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.  Kin2-kin2 li7-choat8 e5 au2-nau2 koh tng2-lai5, hou7 i thong-mi5 long2 bo5 u7 peng5-an.
¡§Pa-pa!  Pa-pa!¡¨  Hut-jian5 ti7 poaN3-mi5-koe3 e5 si5, Pek-jim2 u7 thiaN-tioh8 A-hoa e5 siaN teh jiong2.
I kin2-kin2 chau2-kau3 A-hoa e5 chhng5-piN khi3.
¡§Li7-li7, goa2 ti7-chia, li2 an2-choaN2?¡¨  Chong2-si7 A-hoa goan5-lai5 si7 teh cho3-bang7.
Pek-jim2 u7 khan A-hoa e5 chhiu2, chiam7-si5 che7 ti7 i e5 chhng5.  Sim-sin5 iu5-goan5 kam2-kak chin ut-chut, ou-am3.
Keh cha2-khi2, in saN-kap chiah8 moe5 e5 si5, A-hoa hut-jian5 siuN7-tioh8 i cha7-mi5 e5 bang7.
¡§Pa-pa, goa2 cha7-mi5 u7 bang7-kiN3 chit8-e5 chin ki5-biau7 e5 bang7!¡¨  Tui3 A-hoa e5 chhui3 sou2 kong2 chhut-lai5 e5 bang7 si7 chhin-chhiuN7 e7-bin7.
Pek-jim2 u7 chhoa7 A-hoa che7 ti7 pai3-tng5 e5 lai7-bin7 teh thiaN kang2-to7.  U7 chin-choe7 lang5 khoeh-moa2 pai3-tng5.  Lian5 tai5-teng2 kap thang-a2 goa7 ia7 si7 long2 moa2-moa2 e5 jin5-kun5.  Bok8-su kang2-to7 liau2 u7 kio3 lang5 lai5 kau3 tai5-cheng5, khiok long2 bo5 lang5 beh khi3.  Bok8-su kap cheng3-lang5 e5 bak8-chiu long2 teh chhoe7, teh tan2-hau7, u7 lang5 thang chhut-lai5.  A-hoa chiu7 khan Pek-jim2 e5 chhiu2 kong2, chiah e5 lang5 long2 teh tan2-hau7 lan2 chhut-khi3.  A-hoa chiu7 kiong5-kiong5 thoa Pek-jim2 chhut-lai5.  Pai3-tng5 lai7 e5 cheng3-lang5 khoaN3-tioh8 in nng7-lang5 chhut-lai5 e5 si5 chiu7 toa7 hoaN-hi2 lai5 phah-chhiu2.  In chiu7 saN-kap kiaN5 hit tiau5 thang3 tai5-cheng5 e5 lou7 khi3, jin5-kun5 long2 ng3 in khui siaN gim5-si o-lo2, in ti7 hit e5 tiong-kan chhin-chhiuN7 khai3-soan5 e5 chiong-kun chit8-iuN7.  A-hoa u7 khan Pek-jim2 lai5 chin3-cheng5.  Chong2-si7 hit tiau5 tai5-cheng5 e5 lou7 na2 kiaN5 na2 piN3 chin hng7.  Pai3-tng5 ia7 long2 piN3 cho3 si7 chit8-e5 toa7 khong-tiong, hiah e5 jin5-kun5 long2 si7 thiN-sai3.  Tai5-cheng5 pian3-choe3 chit8-e5 kek8-ki5 eng5-kng, chhan3-lan7 e5 po2-cho7.  U7 chheng-chheng ban7-ban7 e5 thiN-sai3 teh hoan-hou, o-lo2.
A-hoa chiu7 toa7 hoaN-hi2 lai5 khan Pek-jim2 poaN3-kiaN5, poaN3-poe lai5 tit8-tit8 ng3 hit e5 po2-cho7 chin3-cheng5.  Ti7 po2-cho7 cheng5 u7 chit8-e5 toa7 chui2-ti5.
Bok8-su u7 kio3 Pek-jim2 tioh8 thng3-saN loh8 ti7 chui2-ti5 lai7, khiok Pek-jim2 long2 chin tiu5-tu5, A-hoa u7 pang-chan7 i thng3-saN, au7-lai5 chhoa7 i loh8 hit e5 chheN-lek8-lek8 e5 chui2-lai7.  Pek-jim2 tui3 chui2-lai7 khi2-lai5 e5 si5, thiN-sai3 thian-kun e5 siaN na2-toa7, chhin-chhiuN7 hai2-eng2 hang2-hoah long2 bo5 soah.

U7 thiN-sai3 eng7 chit8-nia2 peh8-saN theh8-kau3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  A-hoa u7 pang-chan7 i chheng7.
Hiah e5 thiN-sai3 koh teh khai-si2 gim5-si, hit te3 si7 tak8-lang5 long2 chin-sek8 e5, chiu7-si7 ¡§Siu7-siong e5 iuN5-ko.¡¨
Au7-lai5 thiN-sai3 chin bo5-eng5 lai5 teh chun2-pi7 ian5-siah.  A-hoa u7 khan-tiau5 Pek-jim2 e5 chhiu2.
¡§Pa-pa, pa-pa, li2 khoaN3 hiah e5 thiN-sai3 sou2 pi7-pan7 e5 chiah8-mih8 long2 gia5 ti7 thau5-khak teng2, tui3 thiN-teng2 pai5-liat8 poe loh8-lai5!¡¨
Hit e5 cheng5-keng2 toa7 kam2-tong7 A-hoa.  Kau3 ti7 keh cha2-khi2 A-hoa teh kong2 e5 si5 hit e5 kam2-hun3 iau2-ku2 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.
Khiok Pek-jim2 thou3 chit8-e5 toa7-khui3, lai5 pang3-he7 i e5 cha2-tng3, khi2-lai5 kiaN5-kau3 teng5-a2-khau2 khi3 beh suh goa7-bin7 e5 khong-khi3.
In-ui7 i cha7-mi5 ia7 u7 bang7-kiN3 chit8-e5 bang7.  Hit-hang7 si7 tu2-tu2 kap A-hoa e5 bang7 siong7-hoan2 e5.
Pek-jim2 bang7-kiN3 i u7 kiaN5-kau3 chit8-keng chin-toa7 e5 bio7-u2 jip8-khi3.  Long2 bo5 khoaN3-tioh8 lang5 ti7 bio7-u2 e5 lai7-goa7.  Lai7-bin7 u7 chin ki5-koai3 e5 an-cheng7, khiok Pek-jim2 tah8-jip8 hit e5 chong3-toa7 e5 mng5 e5 si5, hoat-kian3 ti7 hit e5 mng5-au7 u7 khia7 chit8-e5 lau7-lang5.  Hit-e5 lau7-lang5 chin choat8-bang7 iu-chhiu5 e5 khoan2-sit.  Pek-jim2 na2 jip8-khi3, chiu7 hoat-kak ti7 hiah e5 mng5-au7, piah-kak, am3-sam3 bo5 lang5 khoaN3 e5 sou2-chai7 long2 u7 khia7 lang5 ti7 hia, in e5 iuN7-siuN3 hui-siong5 chiau-chui, lo2-soe, in e5 piau2-cheng5 long2 chin pi-siong, choat8-bang7.  Hiah e5 lang5 e5 khoan2-sit tu2-tu2 si7 kap the3-sin siang7-khoan2.
Hit e5 bio7-u2 na2 jip8-khi3 na2 toa7, chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-e5 kou-lip8 e5 se3-kai3.  Lai7-bin7 chin am3-ut chhiN-chhin3, ia7 u7 sio-hiuN e5 huh-bi7 moa2-moa2.

Tui3 lai7-bin7 e5 sou2-chai7 chhin-chhiuN7 kui-lut8-tek u7 cheng-siaN teh tan5 e5 khoan2.  Hit e5 siaN na2-beng5, khiok kam2-kak hit e5 siaN-im u7 toa3-tioh8 pi-chham2 choat8-bang7 teh hiang2.  Pek-jim2 in-ui7 chhiN-chhin3 lai5 io5 i e5 sin-khu.  Pek-jim2 u7 chit8-keng chit8-keng lai5 jip8-khi3, chiam7-chiam7 u7 thiaN-tioh8 bi5-jiok8 e5 siaN teh lau5 chhut-lai5.
Au7-lai5 beng5-pek8 hit e5 siaN chiu7-si7 choat8-bang7 thou2-khui3 e5 ai-siaN.  Pek-jim2 ti7 hit e5 siaN-im e5 lai7-bin7 kui-sin tang7-koaN7, kha-chhiu2 phi7-phi7-chhoah.  I ka-ki7 pun2-sin ia7 beh hau2 chhut-lai5 lah.  I kin2-kin2 lai5 kiaN5, khoaN3 oe7-thang thoat-chhut hit e5 sou2-chai7 a2-boe7, khiok na2 kiaN5 na2 chhim, hiah e5 pi-chham2 au5-kio3 e5 siaN-im na2 oa2 lai5 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7.  Au7-lai5 Pek-jim2 chiu7 chau2-chong5 hit e5 be5-kiong¡]°g®c¡^.
I na2 kiaN5 na2 bo5-lou7, u7 ou-am3 e5 hun5-bu7 tui3 lai7-bin7 teh chheng3 chhut-lai5.  Au7-lai5 hun5-bu7 chiu7 pau-bat8 Pek-jim2, koh hiah e5 thang-kiaN pi-chham2 e5 siaN-im i2-keng ki-ki-hau2 ti7 i e5 hiN7-khang cheng5.  Pek-jim2 kin2-kin2 eng7 i e5 chhiu2 lai5 that-bat8 i e5 hiN7-khang.  Iau2-ku2 hiah e5 pi-chham2 au5-kio3 e5 siaN tit8-tit8 pek-oa2 lai5.
Pek-jim2 kiaN-kau3 phi-phi-chhoah lai5 khia7 tiam3 hia.  I kau3-boe2 soa3 toa7-jiong2 chhut-lai5, ¡§kiu3 goa2! kiu3 goa2!¡¨, chiu7 hun7-to2 ti7 hit lai7-bin7.
Hit chit8-mi5 Pek-jim2 iu5-goan5 toa3 A-hoa khi3 hu3 chu7-hoe7.  Bok8-su kang2-to7 liau2-au7 u7 chiau3-siong5 kou2-bu2 lang5 chiap-siu7 Ia5-sou soa3 kiaN5-kau3 tai5-cheng5.
Pek-jim2 e5 sim phok-phok-chheng2, bok8-su ke3-siok8 teh kio3 lang5, A-hoa tit8-tit8 khoaN3 bok8-su e5 bin7 kap Pek-jim2 e5 bin7.  Au7-lai5 Pek-jim2 chiu7 khan A-hoa cho3-cheng5 lai5 kiaN5-chhut in e5 ui7.  U7 hu7-chek e5 hiaN-ti7 sui5-si5 hoat-kian3 tioh8 in, chau2-oa2 lai5 beh an3-nai7 in kau3 tai5-cheng5.  Cheng3-lang5 i2-keng khai-si2 teh gim5-si lah, chong3-giam5(±RÄY¡^, heng-hun3 e5 khong-khi3 moa2-moa2 ti7 hoe7-tiuN5-lai7.
Pek-jim2 chiu7 kap Pat8-e5 lang5 saN-kap pai5-liat8 ti7 tai5-cheng5.  Bok8-su u7 chit8-e5 chit8-e5 teh kap in ak-chhiu2, soa3 kong2 kam2-sia7 Chu2.  Koh u7 hu7-chek e5 hiaN-ti7 lai5 toe3 ti7 tak8-lang5 e5 au7-bin7.

¡§HiaN-ti7 ah, li2 si7 toa3 ti7 to2-ui7?¡¨  Hu7-chek Pek-jim2 e5 tam5-to7 hiaN-ti7 u7 an2-ni mng7.  Pek-jim2 chiu7 chiong chu7-chi2 po3 i chai.
¡§Ia5-sou oe7 kiu3 lan2 thoat-li7 choe7-ok long2-chong2 e5 thong3-khou2 kap khu-sok.  I beh eng7 I e5 po2-huih lai5 soe2-tu5 lan2 e5 choe7, hou7 lan2 u7 sin e5 oah8-mia7, si7 beh chiap-siu7 I e5 kok e5 oah8-mia7.  I ia7 beh taN lan2 e5 tang7-taN3, beh i-ti7 lan2 it-chhe3 e5 piN7-cheng3.¡¨  Hu7-chek e5 lang5 kong2 kau3 chia chiah chai-iaN2 Pek-jim2 si7 chhiN-mi5 lang5.  ¡§Lan2 ti7 se3-kan u7 khou2-lan7, chong2-si7 Ia5-sou beh hou7 lan2 u7 peng5-an, in-ui7 lan2 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 khou2-lan7 ti7 I e5 kok long2 beh beng5-pek8, si7 chhut ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 ho2 i3-su3, koh hiah e5 khou2-lan7 beh piN3-chiaN5 kek8-toa7 e5 eng5-kng, kek8-toa7 e5 bian2-liu5.  Sou2-i2 lan2 bo5 liah8 sip8-ji7-ke3 cho3 tang7-taN3, si7 hoan2-tng2 khoaN3 bo5 ka-ki7 lai5 gia5 sip8-ji7-ke3.  In-ui7 hian7-se3 e5 sip8-ji7-ke3 si7 piau2-beng5 lai5-se3 e5 eng5-kng bian2-liu5.  Ti7 hit-jit8 lan2 beh in-ui7 hoaN-hi2 kap khoai3-lok8 lai5 boe7 ki3-tit it-chhe3 siok8-se3 e5 kan-khou2.¡¨
Gim5-si e5 siaN u7 pau-moa2 lai5 tin2-tang7 pai3-tng5-lai7.  Pek-jim2 hut-jian5 siuN7-tioh8 A-hoa cha7-mi5 sou2 bang7-kiN3 e5 bang7.  I ti7 hit e5 si-koa e5 lai7-bin7, ti7 hiah e5 sin3-tou5 e5 bin7-cheng5 kam2-kak chin-toa7 e5 giam5-siok.  U7 chit8-chiong2 boe7-thang piau2-beng5 sin5-seng3 e5 lek8-liong7 tit8-tit8 phah i e5 sim.  Lian5 A-hoa e5 chun5-chai7 ti7 hit-si5 ia7 oan5-choan5 li7-khui i e5 sim.
Koe3-khi3 hiah e5 put-heng7 e5 jit8-chi2 koh chit8-pai2 chio3-iaN2 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.  Siu7-khou2 e5 lau7-bu2 e5 bin7, i2-kip8 ti7 i hoai5-lai7 long2-chong2 bak8-sai2 e5 jit8.  Ti7 A-ku7 e5 ka-teng5 sou2 keng-koe3 hiah e5 leng5-jiok8 siu7 khou2-chhou2 e5 jit8, kau3 ti7 Tai5-lam5, khou2-tan3 phoe-mia7 lou2-lek8 thak8-chheh e5 si5-tai7.  I3-khi3 iong5-iong5 chin3-kau3 Tai5-pak ko-teng2 hak8-hau7 e5 si5, hut-jian5 tu2-tioh8 phoa3-piN7, Tai5-pak toa7 kio5-teng2 e5 kong-keng2.  Hoa5 i-seng, i-seng niu5, Tai5-lam5 tu2-tioh8 pok8-kek, chham2-tam7 khou2-bun7 e5 am3-mi5, lou7-piN kiu5-seng e5 choat8-keng2, kong-hok8 au7 chiaN5-cho3 thian-gai5(¤Ñ²P¡^phiau-liu5 e5 lou7-piN gak8-jin5, koh kau3 Tai5-pak, A-hoa e5 chhut-hian7!!!
Chiah e5 su7 chhin-chhiuN7 chau2-be2-teng lai5 chau2-koe3 i e5 sim-lai7.  I io5-thau5 lai5 io5-chau2 hiah e5 iaN2-siong7.  U7 bak8-sai2 chhut-lai7 ti7 i e5 bak8-chiu.

¡§Siong7-te3 ah, kiu5 Li2 lin5-bin2 goa2!  Kiu5 Li2 in2-chhoa7 goa2 e5 lou7!¡¨  Pek-jim2 ti7 sim-lai7 ki5-to2, bak8-sai2 u7 lau5 chhut-lai5.
Chong2-si7 bo5 loa7-ku2 i chiu7 sui5-si5 kam2-kak u7 chin-toa7 e5 peng5-an kap khoai3-lok8 ti7 sim-lai7.
Gim5-si e5 siaN tiam7-khi3, bok8-su u7 khai-si2 ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 hoaN-hi2 chhut-lai5 chiap-siu7 Ia5-sou e5 hiaN-che2 ki5-to2.  ¡§Siong7-te3 ah, goa5 kam2-sia7 Li2, in-ui7 Li2 kim-mi5 u7 kam2-tong7 chiah e5 lang5 lai5 khia7 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 beh chiap-siu7 Li2 e5 kiu3-un.
Kiu5 Li2 eng7 Li2 e5 Seng3 Sin5 toa3-nia2, po2-siu2 in, hou7 in oe7 ku2-tng5 ti7 Li2 e5 lai7-bin7 tiong2-chin3, tit8-kau3 Li2 koh lai5 e5 jit8, thang chin3-jip8 ti7 Li2 e5 kok, chiu7-si7 tui3 chhong3-cho7 e5 tai7-seng sou2 ke3-ek8 beh siuN2-su3 hou7 Li2 e5 chu2-bin5 e5...¡¨
Bok8-su e5 oe7 chin koaiN5, tak8-ku3 oe7 chin beng5-pek8.  Au7-lai5 hit-ui7 hiaN-ti7 u7 ku3-ku3 tang5-sim lai5 hoat-chhut A-meh e5 siaN.
Pek-jim2 e5 sim u7 chhiong-moa2 peng5-an e5 hoaN-hi2.  I hoat-kian3 tioh8 Ki-tok e5 chin-li2 si7 lang5 eng3-kai tioh8 tui-chhoe7 e5..., chit e5 chin-li2 sit8-chai7 thau3-thiat ti7 i long2-chong2 sim-lai7 e5 bun7-te5, lai5 pau-moa2, lai5 chheng-sng3 hiah e5 khun3-lan5.
I chhin-chhiuN7 chit8-e5 toa7 bun7-te5 tit-tioh8 kai2-koat chit8-iuN7 chin hoaN-hi2.
¡§Li7-li7 chiah e5 lang5 si7 m7-si7 chhin-chhiuN7 li2 cha7-mi5 sou2 bamg7-kiN3 e5 thiN-sai3 e5 khoan2-sit!?¡¨
Pek-jim2 u7 lan2-oa2 A-hoa, soa3 aN3-sin soe3-siaN lai5 mng7 i, chong2-si7 A-hoa ng3 i bi5-chhio3 chit8-e5....  ¡§Pa-pa, thiN-teng2 e5 Chu2 Ia5-sou kap long2-chong2 e5 thiN-sai3 chit-si5 ia7 ti7 thiN-nih8 ui7-tioh8 lan2 teh toa7 hoaN-hi2 gim5-si!¡¨

¡§Phah-sng3 si7 an2-ni, hiah e5 gim5-si e5 siaN chiah oe7 hiah-nih8 ko3-iuN7 e5 ho2-thiaN.¡¨
Seng3-si-pan khai-si2 teh gim5-si lah.  A-hoa e5 sim ia7 chin hoaN-hi2, chin khoai3-lok8, i e5 sin-khu kheh-oa2 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 kha-thui2 lai5 lam2-oa2 i.
10 CHAI3-HOE7 AH, GOA2 E5 THIN-SAI3
Ke3-jit8 chiu7-si7 le2-pai3-jit8, Pek-jim2 kap A-hoa chin-cha2 chiu7 lai5 kau3 ti7 pai3-tng5 teh tan2-hau7 chu7-hoe7.
Hit chit8 cha2-khi2 bok8-su e5 kang2-to7 te5-bak8, chiu7-si7 ¡§U7 chit8-e5 ong5-kok, kio3-choe3 thiaN3.¡¨  Keng-ke3 gim5-si, ki5-to2, thok8-keng liau2-au7, bok8-su u7 khia7 khi2-lai5 kong2 ¡§Chhin-ai3 e5 hiaN-che2, ti7 Iok-han7 it-su si3-chiuN chhit-chat, peh-chat u7 teh kong2: ¡¥Sou2 thiaN3 e5 hiaN-ti7 ah, lan2 tioh8 saN-thiaN3; in-ui7 thiaN3 si7 tui3 Siong7-te3 lai5, kiN3-na7 thiaN3 e5 si7 tui3 Siong7-te3 siN, koh bat Siong7-te3.  Bo5 thiaN3 e5 m7-bat Siong7-te3, in-ui7 Siong7-te3 si7 thiaN3.¡¦  Koh chap8-lak8 chat kong2, ¡¥Siong7-te3 sou2 u7 thiaN3 lan2 e5, lan2 ia7 chai ia7 sin3.  Siong7-te3 chiu7-si7 thiaN3, koh lang5 tiam3 ti7 thiaN3, chiu7-si7 tiam3 ti7 Siong7-te3, Siong7-te3 ia7 tiam3 ti7 i.¡¨
Siong7-te3 si7 thiaN3, I tui3 thiaN3 lai5 chhong3-cho7 se3-kan, tui3 thiaN3 lai5 chhong3-cho7 ban7-mih8, tui3 thiaN3 lai5 cho7 lang5 chiau3 I e5 heng5-siong7.  I tui3 thiaN3 hou7 lang5 tai7-piau2 I, thang koan2-li2 chit e5 se3-kan, hou7 lang5 u7 chu2-koan5 kap chu7-iu5.  Lang5 hoan7-choe7 tui7-loh8 liau2-au7, Siong7-te3 tui3 thiaN koh chiong I tok8-siN KiaN2 siuN2-su3 hou7 lan2, kam-goan7 chhek-chiu7 pi-bi5.  Koh tui3 thiaN3 hou7 I e5 KiaN2 lai5 tai7-thoe3 lan2 lang5 long2-chong2 e5 choe7-giat8, tam-tng lan2 e5 choe7-chek, siu7 pah-poaN e5 leng5-jiok8, khou2-chhou2.  I tui3 thiaN3 hou7 I e5 KiaN2 si2 ti7 sip8-ji7-ke3 teng2, hou7 lan2 tit-tioh8 an-un2 peng5-an.  I tui3 thiaN3 koh ui7 lan2 khui kiu3-siok8 e5 oah8-lou7, hou7 kiN3-na7 sin3 KiaN2 e5 lang5 oe7-thang tit-kiu3 lai5 siam2-bian2 chit se3-kan e5 biat8-bo5.
I tui3 thiaN3 koh ui7 lan2 hoe2-kai2 e5 choe7-jin5 siat-lip8 chit8 e5 ong5-kok, beh hou7 lan2 ti7 hia hiong2-siu7 eng2-oan2 oah8.  I tui3 thiaN3 hou7 lan2 ti7 hit e5 kok thang koh kap I kau-poe5.  In-ui7 Siong7-te3 si7 thiaN3, koh si7 chhiat-chhiat su-iau3 thiaN3 e5.  I e5 
ong5-kok ia7 beh kio3-cho3 thiaN3 e5 ong5-kok.  In-ui7 thiaN3 si7 hit e5 kok e5 chit8-tiau5 e5 hoat-lut8, koh lang5 ti7 hia chi2-u7 beh saN-thiaN3, ia7 beh kong2 thiaN3 e5 su7 i2-goa7 bo5 pat8-mih8.
Ti7 hit e5 thiaN3 e5 kok bo5 u7 iu-siong kan-khou2 e5 su7-cheng5.  Put-heng7 kap pi-chham2 ia7 bo5 koh jip8 hit e5 sou2-chai7.  Ti7 hia lang5 bo5 koh lo5-khou2, bo5 koh chhoe7-kiu5, in-ui7 ti7 thiaN3 e5 lai7-bin7 u7 chin-li2 kap oah8-mia7 moa2-moa2.
Ti7 thiaN3 e5 lai7-bin7 ia7 bo5 oan3-than3, put-an, kou-tok8, in-ui7 thiaN3 e5 kng beh chio3-moa2 lang5 e5 sim.  Ti7 hit e5 thiaN3 e5 lai7-bin7 lang5 chi2-u7 beh hiong2-siu7 thiaN5 ki5-biau7 e5 khoai3-lok8.
Se3-kan lang5 ah, li2 tioh8 giong2-bong7 hit e5 thiaN3 e5 ong5-kok, li2 tioh8 giah8-thau5 ng3-bang7.
Tu5-khi3 chit chan5 su7, lang5 ti7 se3-kan si7 choat8-bang7, put-heng7, pi-chham2.
Se3-kan lang5 ah, li2 tioh8 chhoe7-kiu5 hit e5 thiaN3 e5 ong5-kok.  Ti7 hia u7 oah8-mia7 kap chin-li2 moa2-moa2.
Tu5-khi3 chit chan5 su7, lang5 ti7 se3-kan u7 kan-khou2, kiaN-hiaN5, put-an.
Ti hit e5 kok, I e5 ong5 ia7 si7 kio3-choe7 thiaN3, in-ui7 ong5 e5 thau5-hiah8 u7 I e5 mia5, thiaN3 e5 ji7.
ThiaN3 e5 ong5 beh hoat-chhut thiaN3 e5 kng lai5 chio3-iau7 i e5 siaN5, kok-lai7 e5 kang-ho5 ia7 beh hoan2-sia7 thiaN3 e5 peh8-kng.  Ti7 hia bo5 u7 am3-si5 e5 iaN2.  Peh-siN3 beh ti7 hit e5 thiaN3 e5 ho5-piN, ng3 thiaN3 e5 ong5 lai5 chhiuN3 thiaN3 e5 chan3-koa.  SaN-thiaN3 e5 cheng5-keng2, ti7 hia e5 ke-chhi7, lou7-siong7, chhiu7-kha long2 u7 khoaN3-kiN3.
Chit e5 ui2-tai7, thiaN3 e5 kok si7 heng7-hok, khoai3-lok8 e5 kok.  Lang5 beh ti7 hit lai7-bin7 boe7 ki3-tit it-chhe3 se3-chiuN7 e5 kan-khou2.¡¨

Bok8-su e5 kang2-to7 u7 kek-khi2 chin-toa7 e5 heng-hun3 ti7 hoe7-tiuN5 lai7.  SoaN3-hoe7 liau2-au7 Pek-jim2 tng2 lai5 kau3 ti7 lu2-koan2 e5 pang5-keng e5 si5, i e5 sim iau2-ku2 chhin-chhiuN7 toa3-tioh8 chit8-e5 kek8-ki5 ki5-biau7 e5 bin5-bang7 e5 khoan2, u7 chit8-chiong2 sin5-pi3 e5 hoaN-hi2 lau5-teh.
Tui3 chiah e5 su7 i2-au7 Pek-jim2 chiu7 chhoa7 A-hoa jiat8-sim khi3 hu3 mui2-pai2 e5 chu7-hoe7.  U7 chit8-am3 chu7-hoe7 liau2-au7, Pek-jim2 u7 chhoa7 A-hoa kau3 Ho5-peng5-to2 e5 hai2-chui2-ek8 tiuN5 khi3 thit-tho5.
Hit chit8-mi5 tek8-piat sio-joah8, koh si7 chin-sui2 e5 geh8-am3.  Sui-jian5 si5-kan si7 chhut chap8-tiam2 lah, iau2-ku2 ke-lou7 chiuN7 kiaN5-iu5 e5 lang5 chin-chiaN3 choe7.
Hai2-chui2-ek8 tiuN5 u7 chin7-choe7 siu5-ek8 e5 lang5 teh jiat8 kun2-kun2.  Pek-jim2 u7 khan A-hoa lai5 kiaN5 hit e5 nau7-jiat8 e5 hai2-hoaN7.  In chin khui-sim lai5 khoaN3 hiah e5 hou3-chui2 e5 chheng-lian5, gin2-na2 ti7 chui2-lai7 teh cho3 pah-iuN7 e5 hi3-chui2.  Pek-jim2 khiok long2 bo5 khoaN3-tioh8 sim2-mih8, iau2-ku2 i tauh8-tauh8 mng7 A-hoa u7 sim-sek bo5?  A-hoa kam2-kak chin hoaN-hi2 khoai3-lok8.  Pek-jim2 ia7 si7 chin khoai3-lok8.  In sun5 hit e5 hai2-hoaN7 lai5 na2-kiaN5 na2-khoaN3, kiaN5 kau3 li7-khui siu5-ek8 hng7-hng7 e5 piN-kak khi3.  Ti7 hia tak8-hang7 long2 chin an-cheng7, chi2-u7 hng7-hng7 u7 thiaN-tioh8 siu5-ek8 e5 lang5 teh hoat-jiong2 bi5-jiok8 e5 siaN ti7 cho3-tin7 teh hau2 hai2-eng2 e5 siaN-im e5 lai7-bin7 teh khi2-hiat na7-tiaN7.  Kau3 ti7 chit8-e5 u7 chioh8-thau5 e5 sou2-chai7 A-hoa chiu7 khan Pek-jim2 lai5 poaN5 hiah e5 chioh8-teng2 ke3-siok8 kiaN5.  Toa7-chioh8 sio2-chioh8 khi-khi khu-khu chiam3-moa2 hit-tai3 e5 hai2-piN.  A-hoa tioh8 eng7 lat8 lai5 pang-chan7 Pek-jim2 keng-ke3 hit e5 chioh8-thau5 e5 hai2-hoaN7.  In nng7 lang5 ti7 khun3-lan5 e5 chin3-heng5 tiong kam2-kak chin chhu3-bi7, lai5 na2-chhio3 na2-poaN5.  Kau3 ti7 chit8-te3 chin su-hok e5 toa7-chioh8-poaN5 teng2 e5 si5, Pek-jim2 chiu7 the5-gi7 beh che7 hit teng2-bin7 hioh-khun3.  In chiu7 saN-kap che7 ti7 hia, koh soah thng3 in e5 oe5 khi2-lai5, chiong kha lai5 chhun-loh8 ti7 hai2-chui2 e5 lai7-bin7.  Au7-lai5 A-hoa u7 giah8-thau5 khoaN3 tioh8 au7-bin7 Ki-lun5 chhi7 e5 ia7-keng2.
¡§Pa-pa, chin-sui2 e5 kong-keng2!!  Chhin-chhiuN7 thian-tong5 e5 khoan2-sit!¡¨  A-hoa hut-jian5 jiong2 chhut-lai5.  Ko2-jian5 u7-iaN2, Ki-lun5 chhi7 e5 ia7-keng2 kng-beng5 chhan3-lan7 phu5-chhut ti7 hai2-chui2 e5 hit peng5 hoaN7.

¡§Goa2 long2 bo5 khoaN3-tioh8 sim2-mih8.  Li7-li7 chhiaN2 li2 kong2 hit e5 chhin-chhiuN7 thian-tong5 e5 ia7-keng2 hou7 goa2 thiaN.¡¨  Pek-jim2 eng7 kha lai5 la7 hai2-chui2.

¡§Hit e5 phah-sng3 si7 soaN-teng2 e5 chhu3 e5 kng lah!¡¨  Pek-jim2 an2-ni thoe3 A-hoa soat-beng5.

¡§Hit e5 phah-sng3 si7 hoan2-chio3 ti7 chui2-lai7 e5 kng lah.  An2-ni it-teng7 si7 chin-sui2!  Chong2-si7 khiok goa2 bo5 khoaN3-kiN3.¡¨  Pek-jim2 an2-ni kong2 lai5 to2-tit8 ti7 hit e5 chioh8-poaN5 teng2.  A-hoa ia7 hoan-sin phak-loh8 ti7 i e5 sin-piN lai5 khoaN3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7.

¡§An2-ni tioh8, koh chiam7-si5 e5 jim2-nai7 na7-tiaN7. I chiu7 pho7 A-hoa khi2-lai5.  In loh8 chioh8-poaN5-e7 e5 si5 hai2-chui2 i2-keng kau3 ti7 kha-thui2 lah.  Gong5-ngiah8 kap kiaN-hiaN5 hou7 Pek-jim2 e5 choan5-sin long2 nge7-tit8 khi3. A-hoa kui-sin long2 chim3 ti7 chui2-lai7 lah, A-hoa chhiN2 khi2-lai5.  ¡§Pa-pa, pa-pa!¡¨  A-hoa ia7 toa7 tioh8-kiaN lai5 lam2-oa2 ti7 Pek-jim2!
¡§Li7-li7, m7-bian2 kiaN!  Li2 kin2-kin2 chhoa7 goa2 kiaN5 khah bo5 chui2, koan5 e5 sou2-chai7!¡¨  In nng7-lang5 chiu7 saN lam2-oa2, saN hu5-chhi5 lai5 thoat-li7 hit e5 gui5-hiam2 e5 sou2-chai7.
Tu2-tioh8 chit-e5 su7 keh-jit8, A-hoa chiu7 phoa3-piN7 bo5 hoat-tou7 thang khi2-chhng5 lah.  I tui3 poaN3-mi5 chiu7 hoat-sio, kau3 ti7 keh-cha2-khi2 long2 bo5 the3-liang5.
Pek-jim2 u7 pai3-thok lu2-koan2 e5 A-po5 kin2-kin2 chhiaN2 i-seng lai5.  Chong2-si7 kau3 hit tiong-tau3 jiat8 long2 ke3-siok8 chheng3-koaiN5.  A-hoa in-ui7 jiat8 e5 ian5-kou3 long2 bo5 chhiN2 teh khun3.  Kau3 hit e7-pou A-hoa khai-si2 cho3-pang3.  Hit chit8-mi5 u7 koh chhiaN2 i-seng lai5 khoaN3 e5 si5, kong2 si7 ok-seng3 e5 ui7-tng5 iam7.
Hit chit8-mi5 A-hoa u7 pang3 chin li7-hai7, Pek-jim2 u7 chhiaN2 A-po5 lai5 su-hau7 A-hoa.  Ka-ki7 ia7 long2 bo5 khun3 lai5 che7 ti7 A-hoa e5 chhng5-piN lai5 khan i e5 chhiu2, bong i e5 thau5-khak, thiaN i e5 chhoan2-khui3.  Te7-ji7 jit8 A-hoa chiu7 pang3 ng5-sek e5 mih8.  I e5 cho3-pang3 na2-lai5 na2 li7-hai7.  Ta7-saN jit8 chiu7 pang3 ang5-sek e5 huih lah.  Pek-jim2 e5 put-an kap pe2-pak8 long2 hian2-chhut lai5.  I si3-koe3 khi3 chheng2-kau3 lang5, koh long2 bo5 sioh sou2-hui3 lai5 chong5-tang chong5-sai.

Kau3 ti7 te7-si3 jit8, A-hoa e5 soe-jiok8 i2-keng kau3 ti7 choat8-tiam2 lah, khiok cheng5-heng5 long2 bo5 khah ho2-se3.  Ti7 mi5-si5 tan2-hau7 boe7-kau3 thiN-kng thang koh chhiaN2 i-seng.
¡§Chit e5 gin2-na2 e5 siN3-mia7 i2-keng chin gui5-hiam2!¡¨  Hit cha2-khi2 chhiaN2 lai5 e5 lau7 i-keng chin2-toan3 A-hoa liau2-au7 u7 io5-thau5 lai5 tui3 Pek-jim2 an2-ni kong2, Pek-jim2 thiaN-tioh8 chit-ku3 oe7, bin7 pian3-sek, sin-khu ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah.
¡§Sian-siN ah, u7 sim2-mih8 khah tho3-tong3 e5 pan7-hoat, a2-si7 ioh8 thang chu3 a2-bo5?¡¨
Pek-jim2 chin tioh8-kip8 lai5 mng7 i-seng, khiok i-seng siuN7 chit8-e7..., liau2-au7 thou2 chit8-e5 khui3.
¡§Goa2 siuN7 kin2-kin2 chhiu2-siok8 khi3 jip8 piN7-iN7.¡¨
I-seng tng2-khi3 liau2-au7 Pek-jim2 chiu7 chhiaN2 lang5 khi3 tham3-mng7 koan-he7 jip8-iN7 e5 pan7-hoat.
¡§Tioh8 seng kiau2-lap8 500 khou e5 jip8-iN7-hui3,¡¨ to3-tng2 lai5 e5 chheng-lian5 an2-ni po3-ko3 Pek-jim2.
Chong2-si7 Pek-jim2 e5 chhu3-lai7 chha-put-to long2 bo5 chiN5 lah.  ¡§U7 sim2-mih8 pan7-hoat?!¡¨  Pek-jim2 ti7 seng-lai7 kiaN5-lai5 kiaN5-khi3 siuN7 kau3 chin choat8-bang7 thong3-khou2.  Chong2-si7 au7-lai5 i chhin-chhiuN7 u7 siuN7-tioh8 sim2-mih8 ho2 e5 pan7-hoat lai5 theng5-kha, koh kin2-kin2 kiaN5 kau3 piah-kak e5 toh-kui7 khi3.  Pek-jim2 e5 chhiu2 u7 liah8-tioh8 i e5 chhiu2-the5-khim5, lai5 giah8 khi2-lai5 ti7 i e5 heng5-cheng5, i u7 chiong i e5 chhui3 aN3 ti7 khim5 e5 peN3 lai5 chiam7-si5 khia7 ti7 hia tiu5-tu5, u7 bak8-sai2 e5 iaN2 chhut-hian7 ti7 i e5 bak8-chiu, chong2-si7 i sui5-si5 chiong bak8-sai2 koh thun loh8-khi3, chau2-kau3 A-hoa e5 chhng5-piN, lai5 tham3 i e5 cheng5-heng5, au7-lai5 tan2-hau7 A-po5 jip8 lai7-bin7, i chiah giah8 khim5 chhut-mng5 khi3.
Theng5 tiap8-a2-ku2 i jip8-lai5 e5 si5, i e5 chhiu2-the5-khim5 i2-keng bo5 khoaN3-kiN3 lah.  Khiok i u7 tui3 te5-a2-lai7 jim5 500 khou chhut-lai5, kau-tai3 A-po5 kin2-kin2 khi3 chhiu2-siok8 beh jip8-iN7.

A-po5 chhut-mng5 e5 si5 Pek-jim2 kin2-kin2 koh lai5 che7 ti7 A-hoa e5 chhng5-piN.
I hoat-kak tioh8 A-hoa e5 hou-khip i2-keng u7 ko3-iuN7 lah.  Jiat8 ia7 koh chheng3 chin-koaiN5.
Pek-jim2 u7 khan-an5 A-hoa e5 chhiu2, i e5 sim-cheng5 chin tioh8-kip siong-pi.
A-hoa u7 in-ui7 kan-khou2 teh chhoan2, koh tin2-tang7 i e5 sin-khu.
¡§Li7-li7!  Li7-li7!  Li2 an2-choaN2?!¡¨  Pek-jim2 u7 chit8-chhiu2 gim7-oa2 A-hoa e5 chhiu2, chit8-chhiu2 lai5 so i e5 heng-kham2.
¡§Pa-pa, pa-pa, pho7 goa2, pho7 goa2!¡¨  A-hoa soe-lam2 bo5 lat8 e5 siaN u7 an2-ni ai-kiu5.
Pek-jim2 kin2-kin2 tui3 chhng5-teng2 lai5 pho7 A-hoa khi2-lai5.  Siong-pi, choat8-bang7 e5 ou-hun5 chhin-chhiuN7 kiong5-hong, po7-u2 sau3-loh8 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7.
¡§Siong7-te3 ah, kiu3 goan2!  K-i-u3 g-o-a2-n!!¡¨
Pek-jim2 pho7 A-hoa lai5 kui7-loh8 ti7 pang-keng-lai7, soa3 pang3-siaN toa7-hau2.
¡§Goa2 e5 thiN-sai3!  Goa2 e5 thiN-sai3!¡¨
Bak8-sai2 chhin-chhiuN7 toa7-chui2 piaN3-loh8 ti7 i e5 heng-cheng5.  I e5 bin7 ng3 tui3 thiN-teng2 khi2-khi3, khau3-siaN ti7 i e5 na5-au5 choat8-kau3 ou7-ou7-kio3.
I pi-chham2, ki5-iN7 e5 siaN u7 kiaN-chhiN2 A-hoa.  A-hoa bak8-chiu thi2-khui lai5 khoaN3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7, chiu7 chhun i soe-jiok8 e5 chhiu2 lai5 bong Pek-jim2 piN3-peh8 e5 thau5-mng5.
¡§Pa-pa, li2 m7-thang hau2, lan2 koh chiam7-si5 e5 jim2-nai7 na7-tiaN7.  Na7 ti7 thian-tong5 lan2 bo5 koh lau5 bak8-sai2, bo5 koh kan-khou2.  Lan2 koh chiam7-si5 e5 jim2-nai7 na7-tiaN7!¡¨

A-hoa e5 siaN chhin-chhiuN7 beh hoa-khi3 e5 khoan2, i e5 bak8-chiu ia7 u7 chit8-tiau5 bak8-sai2 sui5-loh8 lai5.  Pek-jim2 khoaN3-kiN3 A-hoa chhiN2 koh tui3 i kong2-oe7, chiu7 kin2-kin2 an-cheng7.
¡§Si7 lah, lan2 koh chiam7-si5 e5 jim2-nai7 na7-tiaN7!  Bin5-na2-jit8 pa-pa oe7 chhoa7 li2 khi3 jip8-iN7, bo5 loa7-ku2 Li7-li7 chiu7 oe7 ho2, hit si5 Li7-li7 oe7-thang koh thit-tho5, oe7-thang chiah8-mih8.  Ah, tioh8!  Pa-pa chiah boe2 phong7-ko2 hou7 li2 chiah8, phong7-ko2 si7 li2 ku2-ku2 sou2 him-bou7 ai3 beh chiah8 e5.¡¨  Pek-jim2 sim-cheng5 chin kip e5 tiong-kan lai5 kong2 an2-ni beh kou2-bu2, an-ui3 A-hoa.
Khiok A-hoa ng3 i bi5-chhio3 chit8-e5..., chiu7 koh khun3-khi3.
¡§Li2 m7-thang an2-ni hau2 lai5 kiau2-jiau8 gin2-na2 e5 sim.  Tioh8 an-cheng7!¡¨  A-po5 u7 khui mng5 jip8 lai5, kiaN5-kau3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7 chiong A-hoa chiap-khi3, he7 ti7 chhng5-nih8.
¡§Gin2-na2 i2-keng chiah-nih8 chiah8-lat8 lah, toa7-lang5 tioh8 leng2-cheng7!¡¨  A-po5 u7 he7 A-hoa hou7 ho2-se3, chiu7 khia7 ti7 A-hoa e5 chhng5-piN lai5 khoaN3 i e5 bin7.
¡§Sit8-chai7 si7 chit8 e5 chin koai, chin kho2-ai3 e5 gin2-na2!  Chin kho2-sioh!  Chin kho2-sioh!¡¨
A-po5 u7 khan i e5 kun5 khi2-lai5 chhit i e5 bak8-sai2, Pek-jim2 ia7 chau2-oa2 lai5 ti7 chhng5-piN, chiu7 kui7 ti7 A-hoa e5 sin-piN, chhiu2 liah8 A-hoa e5 chhiu2, in-ui7 siong-sim lai5 sin-khu tin2-tang7.  ¡§Li7-li7, li2 m7-thang li7-khui goa2 khi3!  Tek-khak m7-thang li7-khui goa2 khi3!¡¨  I e5 bak8-sai2 koh chit8-pai2 moa2-lau5 i e5 bin7.
Chong2-si7 ti7 hit chit8-mi5 e5 poaN3-mi5, A-hoa e5 leng5-hun5 chiu7 kui-thiN, li7-khui se3-kan lah.
¡Ñ¡Ñ¡Ñ
Keng-ke3 liau2 saN, si3-jit8, bai7-chong7 e5 su7 ia7 i2-keng chheng-chho2 liau2 lah.

Lau7 A-po5 ti7 chit8 cha2-khi2 u7 phang5 moe5 jip8-lai Pek-jim2 e5 pang5-keng, khoaN3-kiN3 i tiam7-tiam7 che7 ti7 thang-a2 piN e5 i2-nih8, bin7 ng3 tui3 thang-goa7 chhut-khi3.  Si5 si7 chhit-geh8 chhou, i2-keng chin pek-joah8 lah.  Khiok Pek-jim2 e5 pang5-keng e5 thang long2 koaiN teh.
¡§Li2 cha7-mi5 ia7 bo5 khun3 e5 khoan2 neh?!¡¨  A-po5 khoaN3 Pek-jim2 e5 cheng5-heng5 lai5 an2-ni kong2 soa3 thou2 toa7-khui3.  I u7 chiong chiah8-mih8 pai5 ti7 toh-teng2 hou7 ho2-se3, chiu7 khi3 khui thang-a2-mng5 hou7 khui.
¡§Li2 koaiN ti7 chit lai7-bin7 lai5 kek-sim, iu-siong u7 sim2-mih8 li7-ek!  Lang5 i2-keng si2 lah, kiam2 m7-si7 tioh8 khoaN3-phoa3 lai5 kou3 pun2-sin!  Kui le2-pai3 bo5-chiah8 bo5-khun3, li2 ia7 chin thiam2 lah!¡¨  A-po5 an2-ni kong2 lai5 tham3 Pek-jim2 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 sin5-hun5 e5 lang5 tiam7-tiam7 che7, long2 bo5 tin2-tang7.  I e5 thau5-mng5 long2 bo5 cheng2-li2, sam3-sam3, bin7 ia7 long2 bo5 se2, u7 lah-sap ti7 bak8-chiu.  I e5 khoan2-sit ti7 chit kui2-jit8 oan5-choan5 chiau-chui7, lo2-mou khi3 lah.
¡§Si2 si7 kek8 phou2-siong5 e5 su7, ti7 se3-kan tak8-jit8 long2 u7 lang5 teh si2.  Si2 m7-si7 hiah-nih8 thang siong-pi e5 su7, si2 si7 tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 lang5 teh poaN-chhu3, tui3 lau5-e7 poaN chhu3 kau3 lau5-teng2 chit8-iuN7.¡¨  A-po5 khai-si2 lai5 cheng2-li2 lai7-bin7 e5 mih8-kiaN7.
¡§Lang5 chhut-si3 lai5 ti7 se3-kan hit chit8-tiap tioh8 ai3 siuN7 kau3 si2 e5 su7, na7-u7 an2-ni an3-sng3 chiu7 si2 long2 boe7 tui3 lan2 u7 sim2-mih8 taN2-kek.¡¨  A-po5 kong2 an2-ni chiu7 koh tham3-khoaN3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7.
¡§Sit8-chai7 si2 si7 kek8 peng5-siong5 e5 su7!  Tek8-piat kau3 ti7 goan2 e5 ni5-ki5, si2 si7 sit8-chai7 thang ng3-bang7 e5 su7, in-ui7 lang5 ti7 chit e5 se3-kan si7 chin bo5 chu-bi7.¡¨  A-po5 u7 theng5-tiam7 i e5 kang-chok lai5 koh thou2 chit8-e5 khui3.  I chiu7 koh khai-si2 beh chheng-sau3 pang5-lai7.
¡§Li2 ia7 sng3 si7 iau2 siau3-lian5 lang5, na7 kiat-hun iau2 oe7-thang tit-tioh8 gin2-na2.  Li2 e5 chian5-tou5 iau2 u7 chin-toa7 e5 ng3-bang7.  Tai5-pak thiaN kong2 u7 bong5-jin5 e5 
hiap8-hoe7 beh ai3 chhiaN3 bong5-jin5 ti7 hia cho3-kang.  Chhin-chhiuN7 li2 na7 khi3 jip8, it-teng7 oe7 tit-tioh8 chhai2-eng7.  Ti7 hia li2 oe7 thang cho3 chit8-e5 ki-sut8 jin5-oan5, lai5 tit-tioh8 ho2 e5 thai7-gu7, chit8-geh8 jit8 kaN2 u7 chheng-goa7 khou ouh.  Na7-si7 an2-ni li2 oe7-thang chhoa7 chit8-e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 lai5 pang-chan7 li2, li2 oe7-thang koh u7 chit8-e5 chin bi2-moa2 un-loan2 e5 ka-teng5.¡¨
¡§Ah tioh8, ti7 Tai5-pak ia7 u7 thiaN kong2, u7 chit8-e5 Bi2-kok bok8-su, oe7 ki5-to2 i-piN7, li2 e5 bak8-chiu na7 khi3 hou7 i thoe3 ki5-to2, Siong7-te3 kiam2-chhai2 oe7 hou7 li2 koh khoaN3-kiN3!  Sit8-chai7 li2 e5 chian5-tou5 u7 chin-toa7 e5 ng3-bang7!  U7 chin-toa7 e5 heng7-hok!¡¨  A-po5 kiaN5 lai5 kau3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7-cheng5, chiu7 theng5 i e5 kang-chok lai5 chhiu2 chhah, koh khoaN3 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7.  ¡§Li2 na7 sit8-chai7 u7 hit e5 i3-su3, goa2 oe7 pai3-thok8 bok8-su thoe3 li2 chhut-lat8, li2 siuN7 an2-choaN2?  Li2 siuN7 an2-choaN2?¡¨  A-po5 ai3 beh chai Pek-jim2 e5 i3-su3.  Khiok Pek-jim2 ka-leng2-sun2 chit8-e5, chiu7 khui-chhui3 in3 A-po5.
¡§A-po5, hou7 li2 chin to-sia7!  Goa2 hian7-chai7 long2 bo5 teh siuN7 hiah e5 su7.  Goa2 ia7 bo5 ng3-bang7 goa2 oe7 khoaN3-kiN3, ia7 bo5 ng3-bang7 goa2 oe7-thang tit-tioh8 sim2-mih8 heng7-hok e5 seng-oah8.  Hiah e5 hoan2-tng2 si7 goa2 sou2 kiaN-hiaN5 e5-¡Ð.  Hiah e5 i2-keng kap goa2 oan5-choan5 sou-oan2 lah.¡¨  Pek-jim2 e5 piau2-cheng5 chin chhiN-chhin3, i soe3-siaN ti7 chhui3-lai7 an2-ni liam7.  Bak8-sai2 kap phiN7-chui2 iau2 ta bo5-liau2 lau5-teh.  ¡§Si2 m7-si7 u7 sim2-mih8 thang hou7 lang5 hiah-nih8 kau3 choat8-bang7.  Li2 tioh8 khoaN3-phoa3!  Tioh8 pang3-khi3 koe3-khi3 e5 su7!  Tioh8 kiu5 sin e5 lou7!¡¨  A-po5 u7 eng7 chhiu2 lai5 pi2 ti7 Pek-jim2 e5 bin7-cheng5.  Khiok Pek-jim2 kin2-kin2 that i e5 hi7-khang, sim-cheng5 chin-kip kong2, ¡§A-po5, chhiaN2 li2 m7-thang koh ka7 goa2 kong2 sim2-mih8!  Goa2 m7-ai3 koh thiaN sim2-mih8!  Kiu5 li2 hou7 goa2 ka-ki7 chit8-lang5 tiam3 chia, thang tit-tioh8 an-cheng7!¡¨  A-po5 chai-iaN2 Pek-jim2 e5 i3-su3 chiu7 ka7 i koh khoaN3 chit8-e5, lai5 khui-mng5 li7-khui i e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut-khi3.
Iu-siong, thong3-khou2 chhin-chhiuN7 ou-hun5 koh ta3-oa2 i e5 sim.  I e5 bak8-sai2 koh chhut-hian7.  I choan5-sin ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, chiu7 khia7 khi2-lai5, lai5 soa2 kha-pou7 kau3 ti7 thang-a2 piN khi3.  I u7 chiong i bak8-sai2 e5 bin7 khi3 oa2 ti7 thang-a2 kiN5, i e5 hau2-siaN koh kau3 ti7 na5-au5.
¡§Li7-li7!  Li7-li7!¡¨  Pek-jim2 an2-ni jiong2 chhut-lai5, soa3 khui-siaN hau2.  I u7 koh chau2 kau3 A-hoa e5 chhng5-piN, lai5 kui7 ti7 thou5-kha, soa3 eng7 chhiu2 lai5 bong hit e5 khang-khang e5 chhng5-teng2 e5 phoe7.

¡§Li7-li7, goa2 e5 thiN-sai3!  Li2 pang3 goa2 chit8-lang5 beh an2-choaN2!!¡¨  Pek-jim2 e5 sim chhin-chhiuN7 beh piak-lih8 e5 kan-khou2.  Chong2-si7 i hut-jian5 siuN7-tioh8 i2-cheng5 i ti7 Tai5-pak e5 hak8-hau7 hu3-siok8 piN7-iN7 sou2 keng-koe3 hiah e5 choat8-bang7 e5 jit8.  Pek-jim2 chiu7 tong3-tiam7 i e5 bak8-sai2, lai5 siuN7 hiah e5 siong5-se3 e5 su7.  I siuN7 liau2 koh pi2-kau3 i hian7-si5 sou2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7.  Chong2-si7 kiat-kiok8 i kam2-kak chit-pai2 si7 koh khah oh-tit hou7 i jim2-siu7 e5 su7.  I u7 koh siuN7 tioh8 ti7 Tai5-pak toa7-kio5 teng2 e5 su7.
¡§Chong2-si7 chit tiap goa2 beh eng7 sim2-mih8 hong-hoat lai5 kai2-koat chit e5 koh-khah oh-tit jim2-siu7 e5 su7!!¡¨  I ti7 sim-lai7 an2-ni liam7, i e5 bak8-sai2 kap khau3-siaN chiu7 koh hoe5-hok8 lai5.
Ke3-jit8 cha2-khi2, Pek-jim2 chiu7 oaN7-saN cheng2-li2 thau5-mng5, chhit i e5 bin7 lai5 chhut lu2-koan2 e5 mng5.
A-po5 u7 ti7 sim-lai7 teh siuN7, i tau3-te2 si7 beh khi3 ta2-ui7, chiu7 kio3 gin2-na2 toa3 i e5 au7-bin7.  Theng5 tiap-a2 ku2 gin2-na2 u7 tng2-lai5 kong2, i che7 kong-lou7-kiok8 e5 chhia khi3 Tai5-pak.
Chha-put-to ti7 10 tiam2 e5 si5, Tai5-pak e5 kau-thong tng teh toa7 jiat8-khai e5 si5, ti7 Tai5-pak toa7-kio5 teng2 u7 chit8-e5 chheng7 peh8-saN e5 lang5, tiam7-tiam7 khia7-oa2 ti7 hit e5 kio5-lan5.  Iam7-jiat8 e5 thai3-iong5 u7 chio3 loh8 ti7 i e5 sin-chiuN7, khiok i long2 bo5 kiaN5.  I khia7 ti7 hia iok-liok8 chiaN tiam2 cheng-ku2, au7-lai5 chiu7 khoaN3-kiN3 i koh kiaN5 kau3 Tam5-chui2-khoe piN e5 chui2-mng5-lou7 khi3.  I u7 ti7 lou7-piN e5 chhiu7-a2 kha koh khia7 beh chiaN tiam2-cheng.
I e5 khoan2-sit tu2-tu2 chhin-chhiuN7 bo5 sin5-hun5 e5 lang5 e5 khoan2 chin chhiN-chhin3.
Hit e5 chheng7 peh8-saN e5 lang5, ti7 tiong-tau3 12 tiam2 u7 koh chhut-hian7 ti7 Ki5-lun5 e5 chhia-cham7 cheng5.  I u7 kiaN5-jip8 chit8-keng png7-tiam3.  I u7 tiam7-tiam7 che7 ti7 hit e5 chiah8-png7 e5 i2, khiok long2 bo5 tang7-tioh8 sou2 pai5 ti7 bin7-cheng5 e5 chiah8-mih8.  I che7 ti7 hia iok-liok8 poaN3-tiam2-cheng, chiu7 koh chhut png7-tiam3.  ThiN-khi3 hut-jian5 piN3 chin ou-im.  ThiN-teng2 u7 ou-hun5 bit8-pou3 ta3-oa2 lai5.
Hit e5 chheng7 peh8-saN e5 lang5 u7 kiaN5 kau3 kang2-khau2 e5 chui2-gin5-teng kha-e7 khi3.  Ti7 hia khia7 bo5 loa7-ku2 i chiu7 koh kau3 ti7 chit8-te3 chioh8-liau5 khi3 che7.

Tui3-hoaN7 e5 lau5-teng2 u7 chit8-e5 bo5-liau5 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 teh chu3-sin5 khoaN3 i.  I khoaN3-liau2 chiu7 at i e5 chng2-thau5-a2.  ¡§Chha-put-to chit8 le2-pai3 bo5 khoaN3-tioh8 in lah.  Kau3 kin-a2-jit8 chiah koh khoaN3-tioh8, chong2-si7 i2-keng u7 toa7 ko3-iuN7, chiu7-si7 nng7-lang5 piN3 chit8-lang5, chong2-si7 hit e5 chit8-lang5 si7 ho5-teng2 e5 kou-toaN, sit-sin5.¡¨
Pek-jim2 e5 bin7 piN3 chin chhiN-peh8 nge7-tit8.  I chhin-chhiuN7 ti7 mi5-kan teh cho3-bang7 e5 lang5 e5 khoan2 ka-ki7 hong-bat8 ti7 hoe5-kou3 e5 lai7-bin7.
¡§A-peh ah, hia u7 chit8-chiah chin toa7-chiah e5 toa7-chun5, ia7 u7 chit8-chiah chin soe3-chiah e5 sio2-chun5 saN-kap tui3 hai2-nih8 teh jip8-lai5, hit-chiah toa7-chun5 phah-sng3 si7 pa-pa chun5, soe3-chiah e5 si7 kiaN2-chun5, saN-kap kheh-oa2 teh kiaN5.¡¨  A-hoa e5 oe7 hok8-to3 ti7 i e5 sim-lai7. I u7 chau2-jip8 toa7-hou7 e5 lai7-bin7 lai5 bo5 khoaN3-tioh8.  U7 lui5-kong e5 tian7-kng phah-loh8 lai5, lai5 koh chio3-chhut i e5 si5, i i2-keng chau2-kau3 chin hng7 e5 sa2-chai7 khi3 lah.
Toa7-hou7 koh chit8-pai2 an-bat8 long2-chong2 e5 mih8, khiok tui3 hng7-hng7 u7 thiaN-tioh8 chit8-e5 jiat8-kong5 e5 siaN teh jiong2.
